Chapter 1600: Second Supreme Being!

Chapter 1600: Second Supreme Being!

The two Eternal Ancient Pine Leaves turned into streaks of light and entered Ye Tian’s soul.
At this moment, Ye Tian felt incomparable joy in his soul, and his comprehension, as well as his grasp of the Eternal Law, seemed to have instantly risen to an incredibly unbelievable level.
Afterward, Ye Tian also took some other auxiliary treasures to help himself break through to the Second Supreme Being realm.
Time slowly passed—
Although Ye Tian had about a seventy to eighty percent confidence in his breakthrough, it was not a hundred percent certain, so he remained extremely calm and did not allow his state of mind to fluctuate in the slightest.
Much later, Ye Tian’s body began to change.
Countless source sea origin power poured into Ye Tian’s body. This was a sign of breaking through the shackles and absorbing external energy to promote the body’s transformation.
Simply put, Ye Tian successfully broke through to the Second Supreme Being realm.
After that, Ye Tian spent a little more time stabilizing his realm.
At this point, the time was about right.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian entered the Source God Pavilion.
……
Source God Pavilion, a trading space.
One Supreme Being after another entered here, and soon a total of ninety-one Supreme Beings gathered.
At this time, the Supreme Being who had discovered the Eternal Tribulation Domain, Storm Source God, said, “Since everyone has arrived, let’s set off!”
The many Supreme Beings nodded, then followed Storm Source God and, with the help of Source God Pavilion’s shifting ability, directly moved to a region of the source sea.
The many Supreme Beings followed Storm Source God and continuously traversed the source sea. Before long, they arrived at a place where space and time were distorted.
There were many places in the source sea where space and time were distorted; this was a common type of region in the source sea.
These distorted places of space and time often gave birth to some unique void lands, but the area of distortion here was very small, and if one did not approach it, it was almost impossible to notice.
Moreover, this place should not have existed for a very long time.
“This is it! Follow me in together!”
Storm Source God said softly.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!!!
One Supreme Being after another entered this area, and soon, under Storm Source God’s lead, they spotted a black rift.
This black rift was the entrance to the Eternal Tribulation Domain.
“It really is the entrance to the Eternal Tribulation Domain!”
A Third Supreme Being recognized it at a glance.
Another Third Supreme Being nodded slightly. “It is indeed the Eternal Tribulation Domain. I once went to the entrance of a high-level Eternal Tribulation Domain. Although I didn’t dare go in, the aura was the same. This Eternal Tribulation Domain is indeed only at the initial level.”
“Let’s go in together. Once we enter, this entrance will become even more unstable, and in a short time it won’t be able to let in any more Supreme Beings; otherwise the entrance will disappear, and then it will be somewhat troublesome for us to leave.” Storm Source God said.
The other Supreme Beings nodded, then one by one entered the Eternal Tribulation Domain.
Ye Tian also followed them into this Eternal Tribulation Domain, and at the moment he entered, he immediately unleashed several defensive Supreme Techniques to prevent himself from being attacked.
However, he was not attacked.
Clearly, no one from the Eternal Tribulation Race was guarding this entrance.
This was also very normal; after all, it had never been discovered, so the Eternal Tribulation Race naturally did not pay much attention to it. Besides, if it really were discovered, guarding here would instead be very dangerous.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!!!
After entering the Eternal Tribulation Domain, the Supreme Beings dispersed at once, concealing their auras and figures as they infiltrated various parts of the Eternal Tribulation Domain.
Ye Tian also concealed his aura and slowly traversed toward a certain direction.
The goal of this entry was very simple: find some members of the Eternal Tribulation Race, kill them, and obtain the Eternal Tribulation Crystal Stones on them.
Very soon, Ye Tian spotted a member of the Eternal Tribulation Race.
The other party was traveling through the void like an ancient star, and Ye Tian happened to run into it.
This member of the Eternal Tribulation Race was not weak, roughly comparable to a First-Tier Peak Supreme Being.
Ye Tian discovered it, and it also discovered Ye Tian.
“A cultivator from the outside world!”
The first thing this member of the Eternal Tribulation Race did upon seeing Ye Tian was to flee, not to kill him.
After all, Ye Tian’s cultivation had now reached the Second Supreme Being realm; it did not think itself a match, so it chose to run.
But it could not escape.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian crossed the void with one hand, and with only a single strike, he shattered this member of the Eternal Tribulation Race’s body, extinguishing all vitality. Only some tribulation blood, origin law tribulation crystals, tribulation bones, and a one-person-high Eternal Tribulation Crystal Stone remained.
Ye Tian waved his hand and collected these things, then continued searching for other members of the Eternal Tribulation Race.
At the same time, the members of the Eternal Tribulation Race in this Eternal Tribulation Domain learned that intruders had broken in and immediately assembled to resist the outside Supreme Beings.
The Supreme Beings and the Eternal Tribulation Race began fighting in this Eternal Tribulation Domain. One by one, members of the Eternal Tribulation Race fell, but some Supreme Beings also fell into the Eternal Tribulation Race’s trap, were surrounded on all sides, and were ultimately besieged to death.
And Ye Tian’s strength was very great; when he encountered several members of the Eternal Tribulation Race, he easily killed them all.
On this day.
Ye Tian encountered a member of the Eternal Tribulation Race at the Second Supreme Being level, and with only a single strike he heavily wounded the other party to the point of near death. If he struck a second time, this member of the Eternal Tribulation Race would surely die.
But at this moment, a scroll suddenly manifested in the void, intending to draw Ye Tian in.
This scroll was not an ordinary scroll, but a source weapon.
Ye Tian was seen fully urging the Endless Eternal Body, unleashing multiple power-type Supreme Ancestor Techniques, and then layering on Top of that the use of Shattering Void.
“Break!”
　443　Ye Tian threw a punch, and entire regions shattered; even that scroll collapsed as well.
This strike had already surpassed a Third Supreme Being, coming close to the full-force strike of a Fifth Supreme Being.
And inside the scroll, three members of the Eternal Tribulation Race were directly killed.
“Not good, this Supreme Being is too powerful, all together!”
One member of the Eternal Tribulation Race after another appeared, numbering around several dozen.
Ye Tian knew that member of the Eternal Tribulation Race was bait, but he was not the least bit afraid.
With his strength, he was practically an Invincible existence in this low-level Eternal Tribulation Domain. Even if he encountered a large number of members of the Eternal Tribulation Race, even if he might not necessarily be able to defeat them, no one could stop him if he wanted to leave.
“Kill!”
A great battle erupted.
Ye Tian was too perfect in every aspect; whether speed, strength, or defense, he far surpassed these members of the Eternal Tribulation Race. Although among them there were also geniuses comparable to the Children of the Void, compared with Ye Tian, the gap was too great.
In just a short while, some members of the Eternal Tribulation Race died at Ye Tian’s hands.
And Ye Tian did not want to continue fighting either, after all, he did not know how many members of the Eternal Tribulation Race there were in this Eternal Tribulation Domain. The fall of this copied body was a small matter, but if the Eternal Tribulation Crystal Stones he had obtained were lost, then the loss would be far too great.
Thus, Ye Tian broke out of the encirclement and soon disappeared.

Chapter 1601: The Entry Late-Stage Endless Eternal Body!

Chapter 1601: The Entry Late-Stage Endless Eternal Body!

After Ye Tian broke out of the encirclement, he did not stop there, but continued searching for the Eternal Tribulation Race.
Once he was surrounded, he would immediately break out of the encirclement, absolutely never lingering in battle.
At this moment, he had roughly figured out the strength of this Eternal Tribulation Domain; it was not very powerful.
Moreover, this Eternal Tribulation Domain had already been discovered. If they waited for the entrance to stabilize, the next batch of Supreme Beings would enter here.
Even if the entrance disappeared, those powerful Supreme Beings of the eighth or ninth level could completely tear open an entrance and let the Third Stage Supreme Beings enter here.
By then, the Eternal Tribulation Race in this Eternal Tribulation Domain would simply be unable to hold them back, and this Eternal Tribulation Domain would absolutely be destroyed.
Therefore, he had to seize this opportunity now and gain as many benefits as possible.
As time passed, more and more Supreme Beings poured in here, and the Eternal Tribulation Race completely fell into a disadvantage.
This day.
A large group of Eternal Tribulation Race members set up a great formation and tore open another exit, leaving this Eternal Tribulation Domain.
They knew very well that if they did not leave, they would be slain by the experts outside.
After all, the Eternal Tribulation Race and those living beings grown in other domains and the Eternal Heaven were mortal enemies; only some special lifeforms in the Source Sea would not deliberately target them, but some special lifeforms of the Source Sea also wanted the Eternal Tribulation Crystals on them.
It had to be said that the Eternal Tribulation Race was simply a moving treasure vault; everyone wanted to take a bite out of them.
Rumble!!!
The Eternal Tribulation Race successfully tore open a gap, and a large number of Eternal Tribulation Race members rushed out.
There were over ten thousand Eternal Tribulation Race members here, and they were also all the remaining Eternal Tribulation Race members in this Eternal Tribulation Domain.
……
Source Sea.
The Eternal Tribulation Race rushed out, and very quickly they were discovered.
A large number of Supreme Beings began hunting down the Eternal Tribulation Race, and Ye Tian also came out of the Eternal Tribulation Domain at this time.
Just as he was about to follow the other Supreme Beings to pursue this group of Eternal Tribulation Race members, a change occurred.
“You actually dare to attack my race, courting death!”
A black giant hand that covered a vast stretch of Source Sea territory tore through the Source Sea void and reached in.
The Source Sea was incomparably stable; the fact that it could be torn apart showed just how terrifying the other party’s strength was.
Those Third and Fourth Stage Supreme Beings could not withstand the collision with this black giant claw; their Eternal Tribulation bodies shattered one after another, turning into corpses.
Then countless streaks of black light pierced through the void and blasted toward the Supreme Beings one by one.
Many Supreme Beings simply could not contend with these black lights and were shot dead one after another.
Although Ye Tian was relatively far away, to such a powerhouse, that distance was nothing at all. Thus, a streak of black light also locked onto him and blasted over.
Ye Tian did everything he could, unleashing one defensive Supreme Technique after another, turning them into layers of light shields.
The black light pierced through layer after layer of light shields, and in the end it was blocked by Ye Tian’s Endless Eternal Body, but he was still injured.
The power of this strike was enough to kill a Fifth Stage Supreme Being. If not for the fact that his Endless Eternal Body had fused with the Ancient Star Eternal Body and its life-preserving ability was too powerful, he would not have been able to withstand the black light’s attack either.
“This mysterious powerhouse should also be from the Eternal Tribulation Race; its strength is definitely above an Eighth Stage Supreme Being, and it may even be a Ninth Stage Supreme Being!”
Ye Tian guessed.
Rumble!!!!
A powerful Supreme Being appeared and instantly blocked that Eternal Tribulation Race powerhouse. The two sides began fighting fiercely.
But after only a few exchanges, that Eternal Tribulation Race powerhouse wrapped up the remaining Eternal Tribulation Race members and disappeared without a trace. Clearly, it did not dare delay any longer; otherwise, if it were surrounded by multiple powerhouses, it would not be able to escape either.
The surviving Supreme Beings all sighed in relief, but there were truly too many Supreme Beings who had fallen this time.
“Entering an Eternal Tribulation Domain without an organization really is too dangerous!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
The Eternal Tribulation Race in this Eternal Tribulation Domain was indeed not powerful, but the Eternal Tribulation Race had experts. Once they got in touch with some powerhouse for help, Third Stage Supreme Beings and even Fourth or Fifth Stage Supreme Beings were just ants.
If a Ninth Stage Supreme Being were in charge, only then could a low-level Eternal Tribulation Domain be easily taken down.
“It’s time to leave!”
Ye Tian immediately left, distancing himself from this area before returning to the Void Source Hall.
After returning, Ye Tian took out those Eternal Tribulation Crystals.
“182 Eternal Tribulation Crystals, not a bad harvest!”
Ye Tian said with a smile.
Even a single Eternal Tribulation Crystal was already very valuable, let alone so many of them. However, most of these Eternal Tribulation Crystals came from Eternal Tribulation Race members with the strength of First Stage Supreme Beings, so their grade was not very high, and their value was not as great as the Eternal Tribulation Crystals from stronger Eternal Tribulation Race members.
But for Ye Tian, so many Eternal Tribulation Crystals were enough to advance his Endless Eternal Body somewhat.
Afterward, Ye Tian began secluded cultivation to absorb and refine the Eternal Tribulation Crystals.
The energy contained within the Eternal Tribulation Crystals was extremely vast, so completely absorbing and refining them would take a very long time. However, Ye Tian’s Eternal Ancestor Tribulation could take effect, increasing his absorption and refining speed by well over tens of thousands of times.
Thus, in merely ten thousand years, Ye Tian could completely refine one Eternal Tribulation Crystal.
As the energy of the Eternal Tribulation Crystals poured into his body, the Endless Eternal Body seemed like a seed that had absorbed nourishment and was growing vigorously; this was a situation that had never happened before.
As the Endless Eternal Body improved, Ye Tian’s strength also improved accordingly.
However, the improvement brought by one Eternal Tribulation Crystal was not obvious.
So Ye Tian continued refining Eternal Tribulation Crystals.
Gradually, one Eternal Tribulation Crystal after another was absorbed and refined by Ye Tian, and his Endless Eternal Body was also growing rapidly.
More than ten million years later, Ye Tian had completely refined all the Eternal Tribulation Crystals, and his strength was much greater than before.
“Pity, I still haven’t reached the Minor Endless Eternal Body level!”
Ye Tian sighed.
Perhaps if it were someone else, their Eternal Body would already have reached Minor Stage long ago; if it were an ordinary Eternal Tribulation body, it might even have directly reached Major Stage or even Perfected Stage.
But his Endless Eternal Body was too powerful, so it had only advanced to the Entry late-stage realm, not even reaching Entry Peak.
However, even having improved to this extent, he could still easily dominate others’ Minor Stage mid-tier Eternal Bodies.
---------------
Starry Ancient Domain.
Star Ancestor was now one hundred percent certain that Xu Chen had betrayed him and betrayed the Ancient Star Race; at the same time, he was also preparing to lay everything bare.
“Xu Chen!”
Star Ancestor roared.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian appeared and arrived at the Ancient Star Tower.
“Ancestor, what is it?”
Ye Tian pretended to know nothing and asked.
Star Ancestor was very angry, and forcefully suppressed the rage in his heart as he questioned, “Xu Chen, do you not want to release me?”杂.

Chapter 1602 Spirit Source Contract Stone!

Chapter 1602 Spirit Source Contract Stone!

“Old Ancestor, what do you mean by that?”
Ye Tian pretended to be confused and asked back.
Star Ancestor said coldly, “Xu Chen, Dong He, Gu Chen, and the others have either fallen or been imprisoned by you. What exactly do you want to do?”
Star Ancestor saying this was equivalent to tearing off all pretenses.
Ye Tian could no longer keep pretending to be confused, so he said, “Star Ancestor, since you already know, then I won’t hide it anymore. That’s right, Dong He and those other Supreme Beings have already been killed by me.”
“Why?”
Star Ancestor had no sadness at all, only anger.
“I want to completely take control of the Ancient Star Race. They would obstruct me!” Ye Tian said.
“Ridiculous!” Star Ancestor sneered. “Is your vision really that short-sighted? If you keep staying in the Starry Ancient Domain and don’t have my guidance, you simply can’t become a top powerhouse. You won’t even be able to leave the Starry Ancient Domain. Don’t tell me you want to stay inside the Starry Ancient Domain for your entire life?”
“The Starry Ancient Domain is very good. It isn’t as dangerous as the outside world, so what’s wrong with staying here?”
Ye Tian countered.
“……”
Star Ancestor was furious. He had never seen a Supreme Being so content with the status quo and so lacking in ambition. Moreover, Xu Chen’s talent was so good—443 even after consuming Primal Source Liquid, his future potential was still immense.
Little did he know that Ye Tian was just stringing him along.
If not for squeezing out the last bit of benefit, he would probably have directly annihilated this portion of Star Ancestor’s consciousness.
Suddenly
Star Ancestor said, “Xu Chen, do you think that by living in the Starry Ancient Domain, you will remain eternal and indestructible?”
Ye Tian heard the sarcasm in Star Ancestor’s words and couldn’t help asking, “Why not? Our lifespans are infinite, and the Starry Ancient Domain exists eternally as well. Outer Supreme Beings cannot enter the Starry Ancient Domain. Who would be my match?”
“Hahahaha!!!!” Star Ancestor burst into wild laughter. “You’re too naive. It’s true that your lifespan is eternal, but that doesn’t mean no one can enter the Starry Ancient Domain. The Starry Ancient Domain is the prison that confines me, and that half-step Eternal Realm expert who imprisoned me did not fall. If he comes back and sees you people, he absolutely won’t mind erasing you along the way. As the long years pass, that person may already have stepped into the Eternal Realm. Do you think you can contend with an Eternal Realm expert?”
“Who is that half-step Eternal Realm expert who imprisoned you?”
Ye Tian was somewhat curious.
Thinking of that Eternal Realm expert, Star Ancestor’s expression darkened, and he did not reveal the other party’s identity.
Star Ancestor only reminded him, “Xu Chen, if you help me break the seal, the restrictions of the Starry Ancient Domain will disappear. Only then will you be able to leave the Starry Ancient Domain. At that time, you can simply enter some remote territory and live freely, instead of being casually erased in the future by that half-step Eternal Realm expert.”
Ye Tian pretended to think deeply, but inwardly he was not worried at all.
This was only a clone; he was not afraid of falling.
“What good will it do me if I help you? Although you gave me quite a few good things before, you also cheated me. Primal Source Liquid consumes potential. You think I don’t know that?” Ye Tian exposed it directly.
“You actually know about the flaw in Primal Source Liquid?”
Star Ancestor was somewhat surprised.
The Starry Ancient Domain had little contact with the outside world, and Primal Source Liquid was exceedingly rare. The Supreme Beings inside the Starry Ancient Domain should not have known about it.
However, he did not think too much about it.
Since Ye Tian had already discovered the flaw in Primal Source Liquid, there was no point in hiding it anymore.
“Xu Chen, Primal Source Liquid does indeed have some regrets, but it is still a treasure that countless Supreme Beings dream of. That tiny flaw is not worth mentioning compared to its own value,” Star Ancestor said.
“If there are no other earth-shattering benefits, I won’t help you get out,” Ye Tian said.
“If I give you earth-shattering benefits, what if you don’t help me then?”
Star Ancestor said.
“Believe it or not, that’s up to you!” Ye Tian said indifferently.
Star Ancestor’s expression changed several times before he finally said, “I want to sign a contract with you. Later, I will send out a special contract stone. You will enter into a contract with me. If you violate it, you will suffer consequences beyond imagination.”
“What contract stone?”
Ye Tian was very surprised. What kind of contract could restrain a Supreme Being?
“Spirit Source Contract Stone!”
Star Ancestor said.
Void Source Hall.
Ye Tian asked the artifact spirit about the Spirit Source Contract Stone.
“Artifact spirit, do you know about the Spirit Source Contract Stone?” Ye Tian asked.
“I do!” the artifact spirit said. “Strictly speaking, the Spirit Source Contract Stone is a kind of Eternal Source Object, but at the beginning of the Source Sea, this Eternal Source Object was shattered into pieces. Each fragment is also equivalent to a Spirit Source Contract Stone. This kind of contract stone can restrain Supreme Beings, but it is ineffective against half-step Eternal Realm experts.”
“If my clone signs a contract with the Spirit Source Contract Stone, can the contract affect my true body?” Ye Tian wanted to know this, so he asked.
“It can’t affect it!” Star Ancestor answered. “For Supreme Beings with special clones, the Spirit Source Contract Stone cannot take effect. This is also one of its flaws. The reason the Spirit Source Contract Stone can affect Supreme Beings is that it releases a special energy that surges into the body of the Supreme Being and completely merges with them, leaving them inseparable. Once the contract is broken, the Supreme Being will suffer the consequences of the vow. But the master’s clone and the master are not the same body, so naturally it won’t be affected.”
“So that’s how it is!”
Ye Tian understood, and no longer worried about this so-called Spirit Source Contract Stone.
……
Starry Ancient Domain.
“Fine, I agree!”
Ye Tian said.
“Good, I’ll send the Spirit Source Contract Stone over right now!”
Boom!!!!!
Even the Starry Ancient Domain began to shake. This was Star Ancestor expending power to send the Spirit Source Contract Stone out from the sealed land.
With a ripping sound!
A gap split open in the void, and a blue stone fell out. It was exactly the Spirit Source Contract Stone.
“Xu Chen, let’s sign the contract!”
Star Ancestor demanded.
“No problem!” Ye Tian nodded.
Then, the two signed the contract.
This contract was drafted by Star Ancestor and was extremely strict. It required Ye Tian to rescue Star Ancestor. If, when capable, Ye Tian did not rescue Star Ancestor, then not only would Ye Tian be unable to advance any further in strength, he would also suffer backlash and pain until the day his body collapsed and he died.
It had to be said that such a vow was extremely cruel, but Ye Tian still signed it.
After the contract was signed, Star Ancestor finally let out a sigh of relief and burst into laughter.
Clearly, he believed that he would definitely be able to break through the seal.
“It’s time to give me the benefits, right? I’ve already signed the contract. I can’t possibly violate it, so you must truly cultivate me!!” Ye Tian demanded.
“Alright, I’ll give you a great opportunity right now!”
Star Ancestor promised.

Chapter 1603 A Finger of a Eternal Stage Expert!

Chapter 1603 A Finger of a Eternal Stage Expert!

A true great opportunity?
Ye Tian immediately felt somewhat excited. After all, Star Ancestor had previously given him quite a few good things, such as treasures like the Primordial Source Liquid. But now, since he had spoken the three words “great opportunity,” it was probably even more precious than the Primordial Source Liquid, and perhaps even more valuable than the Ancient Star Stone, an Eternal Source Object.
Very soon, Star Ancestor’s true body sent out something from the place of seal.
Ye Tian looked over and found that it was a finger.
This finger was sealed layer upon layer. It looked plain and ordinary, but since even Star Ancestor called it a great opportunity, that meant this finger was no simple thing.
This finger was about three meters long, which meant that the life form it came from was not small. The finger was purple in color, covered with countless patterns, and it was not the finger of any creature Ye Tian knew.
So after looking at it for a while, Ye Tian still could not identify it.
“Star Ancestor, what is this finger?”
Ye Tian could not help asking.
Star Ancestor’s consciousness touched this finger, somewhat reluctant to part with it, but still handed it to Ye Tian.
“Xu Chen, this finger is the most important opportunity I have ever obtained. In fact, the reason I was able to create the Ancient Star Body has something to do with it. It is a finger of a Eternal Stage life form, containing a sliver of Eternal Stage power. If it were not sealed, just the aura of its power would be enough to shatter the entire Starry Sky Ancient Domain.” Star Ancestor explained.
“Then why don’t you use this finger to break open the Starry Sky Ancient Domain?”
Ye Tian asked curiously.
Star Ancestor said with a dark expression, “If I could do that, would I still need to cultivate you? This finger was sealed by another Eternal Stage expert, so there is no way to lift the seal. Even if the seal were really broken, with Eternal Stage power, it might launch indiscriminate attacks and Annihilate my body. At that point, trying to save myself would turn into suicide instead.”
“What use does it have for me?” Ye Tian asked.
“Ignorant!” Star Ancestor said disdainfully. “A finger of a Eternal Stage expert, though sealed, can still be comprehended. Even obtaining a little insight from it is a heaven-defying opportunity. In the Source Sea, you simply cannot find a single Eternal Stage being. If other Supreme Beings learned that you had a finger of a Eternal Stage expert in your hands, I’m afraid even half-step Eternal Stage experts would come looking for trouble.”
“What do you mean, there isn’t a single Eternal Stage expert in the Source Sea?”
Ye Tian was very curious.
“I don’t know either!” Star Ancestor seemed unwilling to say more, and changed the subject. “Perhaps when you have the chance to rise to half-step Eternal Stage, you may know. Asking me now is useless.”
Ye Tian could not tell whether Star Ancestor did not want to say it, or truly did not know.
But no matter what, this finger of a Eternal Stage expert was indeed a true great opportunity.
Afterwards.
Ye Tian took this finger and left.
After Ye Tian left, Star Ancestor thought inwardly, “Xu Chen, once the contract is signed, you cannot violate it. When you rescue me, I will grant you death. This Eternal Stage finger is indeed real, and it is useful for comprehending Eternal Stage laws. It can even give you many insights and help you raise your cultivation realm faster, but the faster your cultivation realm rises, the sooner you must rescue me!”
If not for the contract, he would never have given this finger of incalculable value to Ye Tian.
In fact, he was also extremely anxious.
His great enemy might descend at any time, so he did not want to keep delaying. Escaping from his predicament as soon as possible was the most urgent matter.
---------------------
After obtaining a finger of Eternal Stage, Ye Tian immediately decided to take it out of the Starry Sky Ancient Domain.
He copied himself from when he was at the First-Tier Supreme Being realm. This copied body entered the Starry Sky Ancient Domain, obtained the finger of Eternal Stage from his clone, and then left the Starry Sky Ancient Domain, silently taking away this treasure.
It could be said that Star Ancestor’s plan had completely come to nothing. If he knew about it, he would probably have wanted to die.
Once inside the Void Source Hall, Ye Tian immediately handed the finger of Eternal Stage to the artifact spirit.
After all, the Void Source Hall artifact spirit was the artifact spirit of Void Source Ancestor, a half-step Eternal Stage expert. It had broad knowledge and might even know more than Star Ancestor in some areas, so perhaps it knew more secrets regarding Eternal Stage.
“Artifact spirit, what do you think this is?”
Ye Tian took out the finger.
The artifact spirit stared closely at it and cried out in shock, “Master, this is the finger of a Eternal Stage expert, isn’t it? Where did you get it?”

Ye Tian briefly explained Star Ancestor’s situation.
After hearing it, the artifact spirit could not help but smile and say, “Master, if this Star Ancestor knew that his Eternal Stage finger had been completely lost, he would probably be heartbroken to death.”
“Artifact spirit, Star Ancestor said this Eternal Stage finger is very valuable. Does it have any other uses?”
Ye Tian asked.
“There is another very important use!” the artifact spirit said. “Eternal Stage experts are unimaginably terrifying beings. Even my former master, Void Source Ancestor, had never seen one. They are too mysterious; in fact, no one even knows how many Eternal Stage experts exist, but they definitely do exist, because there are relics left behind by Eternal Stage experts in the Source Sea. This finger of Eternal Stage can be fused into a finger. Others would not dare to fuse it, because if the fusion fails, they will die without a doubt. But Master can use a copied body to fuse this finger of Eternal Stage, and if you try countless times, there will eventually be a day of success. Once it succeeds, Master will have a killer trump card. For example, you could use this finger of Eternal Stage to unleash a finger technique-type supreme skill, enough to leap levels and blast top-tier Supreme Beings to death. Moreover, once Master fuses this finger, it will also be easier to comprehend more mysteries and benefits.”
.... .... ...
“Yes, this method is indeed suitable for me!”
Ye Tian nodded.
It had to be said, the artifact spirit was really clever; he had not thought of this method at all.
Afterwards, Ye Tian found a secret technique for fusing foreign objects in the inheritance of Void Source Ancestor, which could be used to attempt fusion with this finger of a Eternal Stage expert.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian had his copied body fuse with this finger of a Eternal Stage expert.
The first fusion.
Boom!!!!
The copied body directly shattered, and the fusion failed.
After that, Ye Tian copied another body and began the second fusion.
It was obvious that the second fusion still failed.
Again and again, the fusion failed again and again.
For Ye Tian, these repeated failures were nothing; he only lost a little resources.
Unknowingly, Ye Tian had attempted countless times, and the outside world had already passed through the time of ten great tribulation epochs and.

Chapter 1604 Half-Step Eternal Technique!

Chapter 1604 Half-Step Eternal Technique!

This day.
Ye Tian continued to fuse the cloned body with the finger of an Eternal Realm mighty figure. After such a long period of fusion, he gradually came to understand this finger more and more, gaining more and more insights.
The Eternal rule contained in this finger of an Eternal Realm mighty figure was Destruction. What he was comprehending was the endless Eternal rule, which contained all kinds of Eternal rules, so the Destruction rule was also of great use to him.
Moreover, the rules influenced each other. The Destruction rule could also give rise to the rule of life, and the rule of life nurtured all things and could in turn give birth to other rules.
Therefore, even just comprehending the Eternal rule could greatly enhance Ye Tian’s endless Eternal rule.
Let alone the fact that this was a finger from the Eternal Realm, which could help him better understand the life structure of the Eternal Realm and was of tremendous help to his cultivation of the Eternal Body.
In fact, the Eternal Body was a body that was gradually refined and improved step by step into the Eternal Realm. If the Eternal Body reached Perfected, then one could possess the body of the Eternal Realm. Although it could not exert much power, the strength it displayed was still far beyond that of Supreme Beings of the same stage.
This fusion went relatively smoothly because he had already mastered the knack of fusion, and coupled with his profound comprehension of the Destruction Eternal rule, no rejection problem appeared from the very beginning.
One could see Ye Tian’s power seeming to turn into billions of filaments, merging into this finger and slowly assimilating it.
No one knew how much time had passed before the fusion finally succeeded.
This was also the first time Ye Tian had succeeded in fusion!
“It’s done. Next, I only need to try a few more times, and then I can ensure a 100% fusion success rate!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
However, before the next fusion, Ye Tian intended to test what kind of attack he could unleash with this finger of the Eternal Realm.
So, Ye Tian came to the Source Sea.
His gaze pointed toward a distant region, and he activated his right index finger, executing a peerless ancestral technique of finger arts.
“Break!”
A terrifying force erupted, and that patch of the Source Sea shattered like glass.
After unleashing this strike, Ye Tian felt as if his body was about to split apart. Even with the recovery and life-saving power of his endless Eternal Body, he was almost completely Annihilated.
But in the end, Ye Tian still survived, though he was severely injured.
“The price is too great. If other twofold Supreme Beings or even threefold Supreme Beings and fourfold Supreme Beings were to luckily fuse this finger of the Eternal Realm, then if they dared to borrow it to launch an attack, they would certainly die without a doubt!” Ye Tian murmured.
He estimated the power of this attack, and it was very likely at the level of an ordinary eightfold Supreme Being, second only to the realm of a ninefold Supreme Being.
This was still because his own strength was too weak, so he could not display too much power.
If he advanced to the realm of a threefold Supreme Being, then with the power of this strike, he would probably be able to unleash combat strength comparable to that of a ninefold Supreme Being.
Of course, this move could only be used as a trump card.
Moreover, Ye Tian decided not to let his true body fuse this finger. It would be enough for the cloned body to fuse it. Otherwise, if his true body were severely injured, it would affect his attacks, whereas there would be no need to worry if it were a clone.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian disassembled the cloned body, condensed it anew, and started the fusion process again.
Just like that, the success rate of fusion grew higher and higher. After a great kalpa era of research, Ye Tian had already secured a 100% success rate, and only then did he stop the fusion experiments.
Afterward, he began using this finger to comprehend the Eternal rules, comprehend the life structure of the Eternal Realm, and even attempt to create a Eternal technique.
Of course, the true Eternal techniques were too terrifying in power, and he found it very difficult to create one. But with the help of this finger from the Eternal Realm, he could create a peerless technique containing a trace of Eternal technique power, which could also be called a Half-Step Eternal Technique.
According to what the artifact spirit said, Half-Step Eternal Realm experts basically possessed many Half-Step Eternal techniques, and the most outstanding among them had even mastered multiple Eternal techniques.
Therefore, he still had a great chance of creating a Half-Step Eternal Technique.
This closed-door cultivation lasted quite a long time. Ye Tian comprehended for a full kalpa epoch.
During this period, the Dark Forbidden Domain fell into a great destruction, but the human race had other foreign lands, so all humans were transferred to other foreign lands.
In this great destruction, a tribulation beast was born again in the Dark Forbidden Domain, but it was slain by a human Invincible.
.........
After the great destruction, the Dark Forbidden Domain entered the next kalpa epoch.
One kalpa epoch was almost a very short time to other Supreme Beings, but Ye Tian’s cultivation speed had always been too fast, so he felt that this period of seclusion was very long.
A full kalpa epoch of seclusion instead allowed Ye Tian to make progress in the Eternal Body.
The Eternal Body was very difficult to improve unless one had treasures like the Eternal Tribulation Crystal, which could raise the Eternal Body.
But there was another way to improve the realm of the Eternal Body, and that was to actively enhance the Eternal Body.
Basically, other Supreme Beings could not do this, but Ye Tian did it.
He had comprehended this finger of the Eternal Realm, and his comprehension of the Eternal Body was too profound. Thus, he broke through the shackles and forcibly raised the Eternal Body from the late Entry Stage to the Peak Entry Stage, but this was already the Limit. To raise it to the Minor Stage was almost impossible without relying on treasures like the Eternal Tribulation Crystal.
But such an improvement was already enough.
At the same time, Ye Tian also successfully created a Half-Step Eternal Technique. This was a Destruction Half-Step Eternal Technique, completely modeled after this finger of the Eternal Realm.
Ye Tian named this Half-Step Eternal Technique Destruction Severing Finger. Once he borrowed this finger of the Eternal Realm, the power unleashed would definitely be no less than that of a true Eternal technique.
Right now, with the realm of a twofold Supreme Being, Ye Tian could activate this finger and unleash an attack comparable to that of a ninefold Supreme Being, but it would only be a single strike.
After that, Ye Tian began trying to control this finger so that it would not erupt with its full power—for example, by unleashing power comparable to that of a sixfold Supreme Being or a sevenfold Supreme Being. In that case, would the consumption and cost be smaller, allowing him to unleash multiple attacks?
However, this finger of the Eternal Realm was too advanced, and controlling it was rather difficult.
Ye Tian tried for a long time, but could only manage to unleash attacks at the level of a sevenfold Supreme Being, and he could do it ten times. He could not control it any further down.
Moreover, after a kalpa epoch of bitter cultivation, Ye Tian’s cultivation had finally reached the Limit of a twofold Supreme Being, and he was preparing to make preparations for charging into the realm of a threefold Supreme Being.

Chapter 1605: The Battle of Fenggu River!

Chapter 1605: The Battle of Fenggu River!

It was more difficult for a Second Supreme Being to advance to a Third Supreme Being than for a First Supreme Being to advance to a Second Supreme Being, but the difficulty was only somewhat greater.
However, last time, in order to break through to the Second Supreme Being, Ye Tian had used up all of the Eternal Ancient Pine Leaves and the other auxiliary materials. Thus, if he were to continue striving for the Third Supreme Being realm now, the success rate would not be very high.
So Ye Tian entered the Source God Pavilion again.
However, there were too few resources that could help a Second Supreme Being break through to a Third Supreme Being. Even within the Source God Pavilion, it would be very difficult to trade for such resources unless one happened to possess resources desired by other Supreme Beings, in which case one could trade for the resources one needed.
“Eh, there’s actually a mission posted by one of the twelve ancestors of the Source God Pavilion!”
Ye Tian said in surprise.
This mission concerned the Battle of Fenggu River. Fenggu River was one of the properties of Fenggu Source Ancestor, one of the twelve ancestors of the Source God Pavilion. Fenggu River could also be said to be a treasured land, continuously giving birth to Fengyuan Crystal Sand.
Fengyuan Crystal Sand was one of the materials used to refine source weapons, and it held great value in the Sea of Sources. One could imagine how much Fengyuan Crystal Sand the entire Fenggu River could produce.
However, not long ago, the Eternal Tribulation Race had set its sights on Fenggu River and used special means to drag Fenggu River into the depths of the void, preparing to transform Fenggu River into an Eternal Tribulation Domain, and an advanced Eternal Tribulation Domain at that.
This time, the Eternal Tribulation Race had mobilized a large number of its clansmen, even six Half-Step Eternal Realm experts, joining forces to lay out the scheme.
Because it was a sudden move and the defenders of Fenggu River were wiped out instantly, the news never spread. By the time Fenggu Source Ancestor learned of it, Fenggu River had already been half transformed.
At present, Fenggu River had not yet been fully transformed and was only equivalent to a mid-level Eternal Tribulation Domain, allowing at most Sixth Supreme Beings to enter.
Fenggu Source Ancestor was now preparing to take Fenggu River back.
To that end, Fenggu Source Ancestor had dispatched a large number of Supreme Beings into Fenggu River to slaughter the Eternal Tribulation Race. If they could kill a large number of Eternal Tribulation Race members, or even wipe out the Eternal Tribulation Race within Fenggu River, then the Eternal Tribulation Race would be unable to transform Fenggu River, and there would be hope for Fenggu Source Ancestor to reclaim it.
Ye Tian was aware that many Eternal Tribulation Domains were transformed from treasured lands. He just had not expected the Eternal Tribulation Ancestor to be so bold as to actually strike against Fenggu Source Ancestor, one of the twelve ancestors of the Source God Pavilion. Was it really worth offending such a powerful being?
If Fenggu Source Ancestor were to spare no cost, he would definitely bring enormous losses to the Eternal Tribulation Race.
Ye Tian did not dwell on the reason. For him, this was also a good thing.
At the very least, in order to gather more Supreme Beings, Fenggu Source Ancestor had posted this mission within the Source God Pavilion, and the rewards were extremely generous.
Among these lists were many resources that could help Supreme Beings break through their realm. Some of them had no side effects at all, and there were even top-tier resources that could help Sixth Supreme Beings break through to Seventh Supreme Beings.
Of course, if one wanted better treasures, one had to kill more members of the Eternal Tribulation Race.
If Ye Tian were to kill an Eternal Tribulation Race member at the level of a Sixth Supreme Being, it would already be enough to exchange for resources sufficient for him to break through to the Third Supreme Being realm.
Unfortunately, it was very difficult to obtain too many resources from Star Ancestor. After all, Star Ancestor was sealed and was also consuming resources himself. On top of that, he had been sealed too early, so the resources accumulated on him were not very many. Otherwise, if Ye Tian squeezed him a few more times, he would also be able to gather enough resources, and there would be no need to obtain resources from Fenggu Source Ancestor here.
“I’ll take this mission!”
Ye Tian decided.
Although his cultivation was only at the Second Supreme Being realm, even without relying on the finger of an Eternal Realm mighty figure, he was already capable of displaying combat strength comparable to an ordinary Fifth Supreme Being. If he used the power of the Eternal Realm finger, one strike would be enough to heavily injure or even kill a relatively weak Eighth Supreme Being.
But compared with Ninth Supreme Beings, he was still far from enough. After all, at most he could unleash one strike, and he still could not harm a Ninth Supreme Being.
Yet Fenggu River only allowed Sixth Supreme Beings to enter. What did he have to fear?
After taking the mission, Ye Tian dispatched his clone body, carrying a section of an Eternal Realm finger, to Fenggu River.
……
Fenggu River.
Ye Tian arrived here, and after reporting his identity, he entered Fenggu River.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian passed through a spatial rift and arrived above a boundless stretch of river.
This was Fenggu River.
Fenggu River was composed of islands and river water, and Fengyuan Crystal Sand existed at the bottom of Fenggu River.
However, without enough manpower and time, not much Fengyuan Crystal Sand could be collected, so Ye Tian had little interest in collecting it.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian moved through Fenggu River without the slightest concealment of his aura. If he could attract the Eternal Tribulation Race to attack him, that would be even better.
If the other side underestimated him and only thought he was an ordinary Second Supreme Being, then that would be sending him heads on a platter.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian’s clone talent sensed a talent’s existence, and an Eternal Tribulation Race member appeared in his perception.
The other side had concealed its form and aura and was approaching him.
Boom!
The other side suddenly launched a sneak attack. It was an Eternal Tribulation Race member comparable to the Fifth Supreme Being realm.
The other side was very excited, believing that it would certainly be able to kill Ye Tian with one strike.
However, after Ye Tian added many Supreme techniques for defense to himself, he immediately executed the Destruction Severing Finger.
Of course, Ye Tian did not fully activate the Destruction Severing Finger, but only unleashed part of its power, displaying a strike comparable to the Seventh Supreme Being level.
That Eternal Tribulation Race member at the Fifth Supreme Being realm had completely not expected Ye Tian’s strength to be so terrifying. Only at the Second Supreme Being realm, yet he actually unleashed a strike at the Seventh Supreme Being realm—this was unreasonable!
However, he had no time to think further.
With a puff!
His body was pierced with a huge hole, and all vitality was annihilated, turning into a corpse.
Ye Tian forcefully suppressed the discomfort in his body, immediately put away the corpse of that Eternal Tribulation Race member, and then quickly left the area.
Much later.
Ye Tian found an island, hid within a grain of sand, and did his utmost to conceal his aura before finally breathing a sigh of relief.
Then, he began to heal the injuries brought about by activating the Eternal Realm finger.
Much later, the injuries finally recovered.
“Continue the operation!”
Ye Tian muttered.
Whoosh!
He left this place and continued to use this method to lure members of the Eternal Tribulation Race into attacking him, then counterkill them.
Of course, Ye Tian was also extremely cautious. Once he sensed two or more members of the Eternal Tribulation Race, he would immediately leave.
Just like that, tens of thousands of years passed.
In total, Ye Tian had killed thirteen members of the Eternal Tribulation Race: six at the Fourth Supreme Being realm, five at the Fifth Supreme Being realm, and two at the Sixth Supreme Being realm.
In order to kill those Sixth Supreme Beings, Ye Tian even activated the Eternal Realm finger twice, and the injuries were not light.

Chapter 1606: Wind Source Gold Crystal Vein, Strike!

Chapter 1606: Wind Source Gold Crystal Vein, Strike!

Having slain so many Eternal Tribulation Race members, it was enough for Ye Tian to exchange for sufficient resources to help him break through to the third Supreme Being realm, or even the fourth Supreme Being realm. Thus, he prepared to leave and no longer continue taking risks.
After all, this body was still carrying a finger of an Eternal realm expert, and that could not be lost; otherwise, the loss would be too great.
After that.
Ye Tian prepared to leave Wind Ancient River, but at that moment, he sensed a huge fluctuation of battle; the fighting there was probably extremely intense.
“A large-scale battle?”
Ye Tian guessed.
He was wondering whether to go take part, or simply ignore that large-scale battle and choose to leave directly?
“Go take a look. What if there’s a great opportunity? Besides, with my strength, as long as I’m not surrounded by multiple six Supreme Beings, I won’t fear danger, and I can even leave easily!” Ye Tian thought to himself.
Thus, he moved in covertly.
Very quickly, he arrived at this battlefield.
A large number of Eternal Tribulation Race members and Supreme Beings were slaughtering each other here. There were even quite a few six Supreme Beings, and the battle was unimaginably tragic; even five Supreme Beings could only count as slightly stronger cannon fodder, and would fall here if they were not careful.
And at this moment, many Eternal Tribulation Race members were guarding an island. Dense arrays protected that place, and although quite a few arrays had been damaged, the Supreme Beings were unable to force their way in for the time being.
Clearly, the Supreme Beings’ target was this island.
Suddenly, a six Supreme Being holding a top-tier source weapon joined the battlefield, and suddenly burst forth with battle power comparable to a top-tier seven Supreme Being. He was clearly an extraordinary genius, probably no weaker than the Void Divine Son.
In an instant, three Eternal Tribulation Race members at the six Supreme Being level were heavily injured.
Then, this six Supreme Being took out a defensive source weapon and, under the protection of many Supreme Beings, charged toward that island.
He took out a formation-breaking source weapon, and with a single strike, directly pierced through all the dense formations.
With a tearing sound!
The island was shattered, and a massive mine vein connected beneath the island to the bottom of Wind Ancient River was exposed.
This was not a Wind Source Crystal Sand mine vein, but rather...
“My heavens, it’s actually a Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein!”
Even Ye Tian was tempted.
Although Wind Source Gold Crystal belonged to the same vein as Wind Source Crystal Sand, their values were worlds apart. Wind Source Gold Crystal could not only be used to refine source weapons, but could even have Wind Source Gold Liquid extracted from it, and this material was of enormous help to an Eternal Body, its value far exceeding even that of Eternal Tribulation Crystal by a great deal.
Just how many Wind Source Gold Crystals could be born from such a Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein? It was simply unimaginable.
One could imagine how immense the value of this Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein was; even half-step Eternal realm experts would be tempted!
However, mining the Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein was also rather troublesome.
The Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein was too sturdy. Naturally, the difficulty of separating out Wind Source Gold Crystal was very high, and the mine vein was connected to Wind Ancient River. It was impossible to uproot the vein in one go, even for a half-step Eternal realm expert, unless a true Eternal realm expert made a move.
The Eternal Tribulation Race had long discovered this mine vein and had been secretly mining it all along, but the efficiency was not high.
Even so, the Eternal Tribulation Race had still mined a great deal of Wind Source Gold Crystal and made a huge profit!
At this moment, many Supreme Beings had already rushed into the Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein, and they were not thinking of obtaining too much Wind Source Gold Crystal. Even if they could get a large piece of Wind Source Gold Crystal, that would already be a tremendous harvest.
Rumble, rumble, rumble!!!!
One Supreme Being after another bombarded the mine vein, not caring at all whether some Wind Source Gold Crystal would be damaged.
Occasionally, a piece of Wind Source Gold Crystal would be blasted out, and if a Supreme Being snatched it, they would immediately choose to flee, not thinking about a second piece of Wind Source Gold Crystal at all.
Ye Tian did not make a move immediately. Aside from that finger of an Eternal realm expert, his true strength was not very formidable. His normal combat power was insufficient, so he could not sustain prolonged fighting. He could not possibly only seize a few pieces of Wind Source Gold Crystal, could he?
Therefore, he was waiting for an opportunity.
At this time, not only were the Supreme Beings fighting over Wind Source Gold Crystal, but once the Eternal Tribulation Race saw that they could no longer stop it, they also began fighting the Supreme Beings for Wind Source Gold Crystal.
It had to be said that the Eternal Tribulation Race still had quite a large number of members, so they did snatch quite a bit of Wind Source Gold Crystal, but many Wind Source Gold Crystals were also destroyed. After all, the Supreme Beings’ mining methods were too brutal, directly bombarding with supreme techniques, and nearly seventy to eighty percent of the Wind Source Gold Crystal was wasted.
But if they did not use this method, then mining even one piece of Wind Source Gold Crystal would take a very long time. Right now, where would they find that much time to spare?
Time slowly passed, and this Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein was already torn apart and utterly miserable.
However, many Wind Source Gold Crystals had still been mined away.
Still, many Supreme Beings fled after snatching Wind Source Gold Crystal, and at this moment, the Eternal Tribulation Race held the advantage.
Helplessly, the other Supreme Beings did not dare remain here any longer and chose to flee.
The Eternal Tribulation Race was also worried that their own Wind Source Gold Crystal would be snatched by the Supreme Beings, so they had to send these Wind Source Gold Crystals out of Wind Ancient River at the first possible moment.
Thus.
Those Eternal Tribulation Race members who had snatched Wind Source Gold Crystal immediately took out their Wind Source Gold Crystal and handed it to a six Supreme Being. This six Supreme Being was very powerful, the leader here, and an existence comparable to the Void Divine Son.
Just as this Eternal Tribulation Race member had collected the Wind Source Gold Crystal and was about to leave this place and return to the Eternal Tribulation Race headquarters, Ye Tian made his move.
“．‖Good opportunity!”
Ye Tian immediately activated that finger of an Eternal realm expert and unleashed the Destruction Severing Finger.
This time, although he did not fully activate that finger of an Eternal realm expert, he still activated nearly more than half of its power, unleashing a strike comparable to the battle power of a top-tier eight Supreme Being.
“No!”
That Eternal Tribulation Race member and the Eternal Tribulation Race members around him were all dumbfounded.
This was a strike comparable to the eight Supreme Being level. Had a eight Supreme Being entered Wind Ancient River?
But how could that be possible?
Wind Ancient River currently only allowed six Supreme Beings to enter!
They could not block it!!!!
The other Eternal Tribulation Race members, because they were gathered together, had no time to escape. One after another, they turned to ash, while that Eternal Tribulation Race member comparable to the Void Divine Son tried his best to resist this strike, but he was still slightly lacking.
With a loud boom!
This Eternal Tribulation Race member’s body collapsed, his life force was annihilated, and he turned into a corpse.
Swish, swish, swish!
Ye Tian collected their corpses and treasures, forcibly enduring the injuries in his body as he left this place at extremely high speed.
Very quickly, Ye Tian arrived at one of Wind Ancient River’s exits and returned to the outside world.

Chapter 1607: The Limitless Eternal Body has reached Minor Stage!

Chapter 1607: The Limitless Eternal Body has reached Minor Stage!

Ye Tian came out of Fenggu River and immediately chose to enter the Source God Pavilion. Although his injuries were severe, they were not enough to cause him to fall. Right now, he wanted to exchange for resources as quickly as possible, otherwise, if the resources suitable for Fenggu Domain Ancestor to break through were all exchanged away, he would have no choice but to exchange for other resources.
So, he began to submit the mission, taking out one Eternal Tribulation Race corpse after another to hand in as proof.
Source God Pavilion naturally had a way to verify the time of death of these Eternal Tribulation Race members, and could also infer whether they had fallen within Fenggu River. This mission could not be faked.
Very soon, the appraisal was completed, and Ye Tian finished the mission.
After that, Ye Tian began exchanging for some scarce resources.
For example, the Water Marsh Cold Leaves and the Other Shore Three Flower Fruit, both of which are very suitable for a Second-Tier Supreme Being breaking through to the Third-Tier Supreme Being realm. Their value is quite high, even somewhat better than Eternal Ancient Pine Leaves, but these two treasures are only found in certain special blessed lands, so they are also relatively rare.
Ye Tian immediately exchanged for these two treasures, and finally exchanged for another rare treasure that could help a Third-Tier Supreme Being冲击 the Fourth-Tier Supreme Being—Undying Source Heart Liquid. This treasure is obtained from the heart-blood essence of the Undying Source Bird, condensed into a single drop of Undying Source Heart Liquid. Its value is extremely high because the Undying Source Bird is very powerful, a special lifeform of the Source Sea. Upon adulthood, it can become a Supreme Being, and among them, the outstanding ones can even become Seventh-Tier Supreme Beings.
To obtain one drop of Undying Source Heart Liquid, one has to kill an Undying Source Bird, which is why its value is so high.
Undying Source Heart Liquid can help a Third-Tier Supreme Being break through to Fourth-Tier Supreme Being, and it has no side effects, but once used, it will have no further effect in the future.
It could be said that this kind of resource can only be used once.
After exchanging for these resources, the contribution points Ye Tian had obtained from completing the mission were also almost exhausted, so he left Source God Pavilion and soon returned to Void Source Hall.
……
Void Source Hall.
Ye Tian let the copied body automatically collapse, because recreating a copied body did not consume much, but healing the injuries of a copied body would consume even more, and take a very long time.
Rather than that, it was better to simply let the copied body collapse.
With the copied body collapsed, Ye Tian retrieved that section of Eternal realm finger, then began organizing his gains.
This time, after killing those Eternal Tribulation Race members, the other resources obtained could be set aside; the Wind Source Gold Crystal was the real great harvest.
Whoosh!
A large amount of Wind Source Gold Crystal was placed on the floor of Void Source Hall, piling up into a huge mountain.
“This time my luck was not bad; I obtained so much Wind Source Gold Crystal!” Ye Tian was in a very good mood.
If others knew he had obtained so much Wind Source Gold Crystal, they would probably be jealous to death.
--------------------
Eternal Tribulation Race, the only Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain.
A Ninth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race member in charge of the battle at Fenggu River heard that a Sixth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race member comparable to a Void Divine Son had been killed, and that a large amount of Wind Source Gold Crystal had been seized, and was instantly extremely furious.
Unfortunately, he could not enter; otherwise he would definitely have intercepted and killed Ye Tian.
Afterward, he relayed the news to an existence of the Eternal Tribulation Race at half a step from the Eternal realm—Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor!
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor was also an incomparably powerful existence among those at half a step from the Eternal realm, ranking among the top three in the Eternal Tribulation Race. It was he who had advocated annexing Fenggu River and carried out this plan.
When he learned that Ye Tian had displayed strength comparable to a strike from the Eighth Heaven, he immediately frowned.
“That Supreme Being’s own cultivation is not high; he should have relied on outside power to erupt with the strength of an Eighth-Tier Supreme Being. He definitely paid a heavy price, but it’s very possible that it was only a clone. If it were his true body, he wouldn’t have paid such a great price!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor thought to himself.
Losing some Wind Source Gold Crystal was nothing. Fenggu River was not limited to just that one source of Wind Source Gold Crystal.
Besides, the Eternal Tribulation Race’s real goal was not to seize these Wind Source Gold Crystals.
A bit of Wind Source Gold Crystal was not enough to make him risk offending Fenggu Domain Ancestor. He had a much larger purpose, and even Fenggu Domain Ancestor might not know this secret.
“If that Supreme Being can continue to strike, then he could easily threaten my plan. I must send a few Sixth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race members with powerful trump cards—at the very least, they must have a way to withstand a strike from an Eighth-Tier Supreme Being. From the situation at the time, the other side likely only had the power of one strike. As long as they withstand that strike, the other side will have no power to resist.”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor decided.
Very quickly, he summoned two Sixth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race members.
Not long after, the two Sixth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race members arrived before Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor and respectfully said, “We greet Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor directly ordered, “I am sending you to Fenggu River. There is an important mission for you.”
“Yes!”
The two Sixth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race members immediately responded.
Whoosh whoosh!!
Two treasures fell into their hands.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor introduced them: “These two treasures are the Indeterminate Armor and the Void Water. The Indeterminate Armor defends against everything; even a strike from an Eighth-Tier Supreme Being would find it hard to kill you. However, once you use it, it will consume your own potential. As for the Void Water, it can turn your body into a void state. Even an attack from an Eighth Stage Supreme Being can be weakened by more than ninety-nine percent, but it will also initially affect the Eternal Body. Therefore, unless you are in a desperate situation, you must not use these two treasures. But once you are in a desperate situation, you must use them!”
“Yes, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor!”
The two Sixth Stage Eternal Tribulation Race members nodded repeatedly in agreement.
Afterward, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor transmitted the details of this mission to the two Eternal Tribulation Race members, telling them to keep it absolutely secret, and that even if they fell, they could not speak of it.
Then, the two Eternal Tribulation Race members headed for Fenggu River.
On the other side.
Ye Tian began refining the special substance Wind Source Gold Liquid from within the Wind Source Gold Crystal. Essentially, only a small drop of Wind Source Gold Liquid could be refined from a large piece of Wind Source Gold Crystal.
Although there seemed to be a great deal of Wind Source Gold Crystal, after all of it was refined, it would probably amount to about 100 milliliters of Wind Source Gold Liquid.
Years passed one after another, and the refining process went very smoothly.
One day, Ye Tian finally refined all of the Wind Source Gold Crystal into Wind Source Gold Liquid.
After that, he began absorbing the Wind Source Gold Liquid to enhance his Limitless Eternal Body.
The first drop of Wind Source Gold Liquid entered his mouth and turned into a vast surge of energy that swept through his entire body.
Boom!!!!
The Limitless Eternal Body seemed to have turned into a monstrous maw, devouring that drop of Wind Source Gold Liquid.
The Limitless Eternal Body, which had originally been at the peak of Entry Stage, actually broke through the shackles of the Limitless Eternal Body with the help of this drop of Wind Source Gold Liquid.
Crack!!!!
The bottleneck shackles were broken, and Ye Tian’s Limitless Eternal Body just like that entered Minor Stage.

Chapter 1608 Breakthrough, Triple Supreme Being!

Chapter 1608 Breakthrough, Triple Supreme Being!

“The effect of the Wind Source Golden Liquid is too good, no wonder those Supreme Beings are all so疯狂抢夺 Wind Source Gold Crystals!”
Ye Tian said in shock.
Of course, he was actually only one step away from a breakthrough to begin with; the Wind Source Golden Liquid merely acted as a catalyst. That was why it could help him break through the bottleneck all at once and raise the Endless Eternal Body to the Minor Stage.
However, it was somewhat difficult to raise the Endless Eternal Body to the Major Stage. I’m afraid that even refining all of this Wind Source Golden Liquid might not necessarily succeed.
Afterward.
Ye Tian continued refining the Wind Source Golden Liquid. Drop after drop of Wind Source Golden Liquid was refined by him, further advancing the growth of the Endless Eternal Body.
Gradually, Ye Tian’s Endless Eternal Body became stronger and stronger.
Minor Stage initial phase!
Minor Stage middle phase!
Minor Stage late phase!
Minor Stage Peak!
Just as the Wind Source Golden Liquid was completely exhausted, Ye Tian’s Endless Eternal Body finally broke through the bottleneck from the Minor Stage to the Major Stage and advanced to the Major Stage.
Boom!!!!
The Endless Eternal Body at the Major Stage was far, far stronger than the Endless Eternal Body at the Entry Stage Peak.
At this moment, Ye Tian felt the formidable power of the Endless Eternal Body at the Major Stage.
If his copy body were to drive that severed finger of the Eternal Realm expert again and unleash a full-power strike comparable to an eighth-level Supreme Being, he would not suffer too severe injuries. Even if he fully activated that severed finger of the Eternal Realm expert and unleashed a strike with the power of a ninth-level Supreme Being, the injuries would not be too serious.
If he went all out, the copy body might even be able to unleash the attack power of a ninth-level Supreme Being twice.
Moreover, his regular combat strength had probably also risen to the top combat power of a fifth-level Supreme Being, and he was not very far from a sixth-level Supreme Being.
Once he broke through to the Triple Supreme Being realm, he would probably truly possess top combat power of a sixth-level Supreme Being.
After the Endless Eternal Body was raised to the Major Stage, the difficulty of continuing to improve it would probably become extremely great.
After all, his Endless Eternal Body had surpassed the Upper Eternal Body and reached the level of the Legendary Eternal Body. Such an Eternal Body was incomparably powerful, but it was also incomparably difficult to improve.
However, even just the Major Stage Endless Eternal Body was comparable to the Perfected stage of an ordinary Upper Eternal Body.
“It’s time to charge into the Triple Supreme Being realm!”
Ye Tian murmured.
He took out Water Marsh Cold Leaf, the Other Shore Three Flower Fruit, and several other auxiliary resources, then swallowed them and began refining them.
“Break!”
With a low shout from Ye Tian, the bottleneck between the Second Supreme Being realm and the Triple Supreme Being realm was forcefully broken through by Ye Tian, and an even more powerful aura spread out from his body.
At this moment, he broke through the bottleneck and advanced to the Triple Supreme Being realm.
“The breakthrough was very easy!”
Ye Tian felt it.
However, this was also very normal. After all, his comprehension of the Eternal Rule was too profound, and he also had Water Marsh Cold Leaf and the Other Shore Three Flower Fruit as breakthrough aids. If he still could not break through easily, that would have been strange indeed!
Ye Tian spent more time stabilizing the Triple Supreme Being realm, then began inquiring about the situation in Wind Ancient River.
If there were not too many changes in Wind Ancient River, he planned to enter Wind Ancient River again.
If he killed more Eternal Tribulation Race members, he would be able to obtain more resources from Wind Ancient Ancestor. If he was lucky, he might even encounter Wind Source Gold Crystal, and that would be a huge gain.
Now, the Eternal Tribulation Crystal of the Eternal Tribulation Race was no longer very effective for him. He had refined some before, but unfortunately gained little improvement from it. However, Wind Source Gold Crystal still remained effective.
If he had enough Wind Source Golden Liquid, he estimated that he could raise the Endless Eternal Body to the Perfected stage.
Therefore, he still wanted to obtain more Wind Source Gold Crystal.
……
Source God Pavilion.
Ye Tian entered this place. Since this time the battle in Wind Ancient River was organized by Wind Ancient Ancestor, he could only learn the latest information within Source God Pavilion.
After exchanging and communicating with many Supreme Beings, Ye Tian roughly understood the situation.
After learning that Wind Ancient River possessed Wind Source Gold Crystal, numerous Supreme Beings poured into Wind Ancient River.
The Eternal Tribulation Race suffered heavy losses, but the Supreme Beings also suffered greatly. Many powerful and famous Supreme Beings had fallen in Wind Ancient River.
Moreover, even a disciple at the half-step Eternal realm had died in Wind Ancient River.
Ye Tian found it very strange that the Eternal Tribulation Race was so determined to seize Wind Ancient River.
Although the Eternal Tribulation Race was very powerful, it should not be able to endure fighting like this forever!
The Eternal Tribulation Race only had one Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain, and it was being targeted by many forces. This time, in order to occupy Wind Ancient River, the Eternal Tribulation Race had continuously drawn members from the Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain and had already lost many of its people.
·········request for flowers··· ·····
If they kept losing people, even if the Eternal Tribulation Race truly occupied Wind Ancient River, would they even be able to recoup their losses?
Even if Wind Source Gold Crystal had high value, it still could not make up for the cost of losing so many clansmen, right?
So Ye Tian could not understand it at all.
“Perhaps the Eternal Tribulation Race has a greater plan!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
This time, he planned not to bring that severed finger of the Eternal Realm expert first.
Although with his strength he could not contend against those sixth-level Eternal Tribulation Race members comparable to Void Sky Sons, his life-preserving ability was strong!
Star Ancestor could rely on the Ancient Star Eternal Body to save his life in front of top half-step Eternal realm experts, while his Endless Eternal Body was even slightly more formidable than the Ancient Star Eternal Body in terms of life-preserving ability. Sixth-level Eternal Tribulation Race members simply could not kill him, and even some seventh-level Eternal Tribulation Race members could not kill him.
.... .... ...
Therefore, even without carrying the Eternal Realm expert’s finger, he was still enough to protect his life.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian quickly rushed to Wind Ancient River again, then entered Wind Ancient River, preparing to investigate the situation.
-------------------
Deep within Source God Pavilion.
The Twelve Ancestors were holding a meeting.
“Wind Ancient Source Ancestor, you are a special lifeform of the Source Sea. Wind Ancient River was once your place of birth. What exactly is there that is worth the Eternal Tribulation Race going to such great lengths? As far as I know, the Eternal Tribulation Race has lost hundreds of thousands of clansmen this time, and the resources mobilized to transform Wind Ancient River into an Eternal Tribulation Domain are countless. If it’s only for those wind source gold crystal veins of unknown quantity, then I don’t believe it.”
One of the Twelve Ancestors, True River Sword Ancestor, said.
Wind Ancient Source Ancestor shook his head and said, “I really do not know. Although I was born in Wind Ancient River, I have not returned there for endless ages. In my original view, Wind Ancient River did not have many resources. Only Wind Source Crystal Sand could be considered a good thing. I didn’t even know when Wind Source Gold Crystal was born in Wind Ancient River. As far as I know, Wind Source Gold Crystal should have only been born not long ago, otherwise I could not possibly have failed to receive the news. As for why Eternal Tribulation Ancestor is seizing Wind Ancient River, I do have a guess in my heart.”
“What guess?”
True River Sword Ancestor and the others all asked curiously.
