Chapter 1609: Innate Eternal Life!

Chapter 1609: Innate Eternal Life!

“What if an Innate Eternal Life was born in Fugu River?”
Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor speculated.
“What? You mean Innate Eternal Life?”
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor said in disbelief.
The other twelve ancestors were also shocked by this guess. Innate Eternal Life is an extremely rare form of life. Once born, it possesses an Eternal body, and if it reaches adulthood, it is enough to match a half-step Eternal Realm expert.
Moreover, the chance for Innate Eternal Life to break through to the Eternal Realm is much greater than that of a half-step Eternal Realm expert.
According to rumors, among the mighty experts in the Eternal Realm, half are Innate Eternal Life.
This shows just how formidable Innate Eternal Life is.
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor quickly asked again, “Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor, Innate Eternal Life is so rare. Why would you make such a guess?”
Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor said, “I’m not guessing randomly. First of all, if Innate Eternal Life truly comes into the world, the commotion will be enormous and attract many powerful experts. The last time Innate Eternal Life appeared, it drew in many half-step Eternal Realm experts, and they even fought over it, causing three half-step Eternal Realm experts to fall. In the end, a mighty Eternal Realm expert appeared and took that Innate Eternal Life away. If the Eternal Tribulation Race discovered that Innate Eternal Life was about to be born, they would occupy Fugu River and then transform it into an Eternal Tribulation Domain. Then they would pay a huge price to seal off the Eternal Tribulation Domain. In that case, outsiders would not be able to get in, and they would also be unable to discover the phenomenon and commotion of Innate Eternal Life being born.”
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor shook his head and said, “That’s only speculation, not evidence.”
Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor smiled and said, “Indeed, it’s not evidence, and it’s not even really related. But before Fugu River was occupied by the Eternal Tribulation Race, a subordinate stationed there sent me a message saying that a strange place had been discovered somewhere in Fugu River, as if some lifeform was gestating there. I didn’t pay much attention at the time, because it was just a small matter, so I ignored it. Looking back now, could it have been Innate Eternal Life in gestation, and my subordinate, lacking knowledge, didn’t know about Innate Eternal Life at all, so he only reported to me that it was a special lifeform?”
“If we add this piece of information, then it really could be Innate Eternal Life.”
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor nodded.
At this moment, another one of the twelve ancestors, Bei Yang Yuan Ancestor, asked, “Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor, do you know the exact location of that special lifeform?”
“I don’t know!” Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor shook his head. “Because I didn’t pay attention, I never asked for the location. If I had known the location, I would have immediately sent Supreme Beings to investigate the information, and I wouldn’t be here speculating.”
“If Innate Eternal Life really exists, then the Eternal Tribulation Race will definitely spare no effort to occupy Fugu River. As for the Supreme Beings under us, there aren’t many of them. Even if we issue a bounty mission, many Supreme Beings are very protective of their lives and may not be willing to risk their lives for that little bit of resources. In the end, the Eternal Tribulation Race will suffer heavy losses, but if they obtain that Innate Eternal Life, all those losses will be made up for.” Zhenhe Sword Ancestor said.
“Then what should we do?” Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor asked.
After thinking for a while, one of the twelve ancestors, Saint Ya Yuan Ancestor, suggested, “Just spread the news that there is a high possibility of Innate Eternal Life in Fugu River, and even publicize the message your subordinate sent you. I believe some people will believe it and even take risks to enter Fugu River. Many forces will probably also send people to investigate whether it is true or false. In that case, the Eternal Tribulation Race can forget about successfully taking Fugu River.”
“This method works. I agree!” Feng Gu Yuan Ancestor immediately agreed.
Thus.
Next, the twelve ancestors spread this news, and it quickly spread throughout the major forces of the Source Sea.
--------------------
Void Source Hall.
Ye Tian also received a message from the Source God Pavilion and was immediately shocked.
“Innate Eternal Life?”
Was this guess reliable?
He was not too sure, but if it were true, then it could explain why the Eternal Tribulation Race was acting this way.
When Ye Tian shared the matter of Innate Eternal Life with the hall spirit of Void Source Hall, the hall spirit revealed some information.
“Master, in fact, the previous master also fell because of Innate Eternal Life!”
the spirit said.
“Wasn’t it said that he was pursued by a great enemy and eventually fell?”
Ye Tian asked in confusion. .........
The spirit explained, “In fact, back then the master and that great enemy were fighting over Innate Eternal Life. If not for the master, that half-step Eternal Realm expert really might have successfully taken away Innate Eternal Life, but the master stopped him in time. In the end, the master was severely injured and gave up the struggle. Later, it was said that a mysterious Eternal Realm expert appeared and, in an instant, took that Innate Eternal Life away. That great enemy lost Innate Eternal Life and blamed all of it on the master, so he came to hunt down the master while he was severely injured and healing. The master knew he wouldn’t survive, so he threw Void Source Hall into a forbidden land and fled, but in the end he was still killed by the other side. However, the master also severely injured the other side at the cost of his life.”
“So that’s how it was!”
Ye Tian understood.
Soon after, he became even more curious and asked, “Why does everyone want to seize Innate Eternal Life?”
The spirit said, “When Innate Eternal Life reaches adulthood, it can grow to the half-step Eternal Realm. If one uses special methods to possess an Innate Eternal Life, then once successful, one can grow into a half-step Eternal Realm expert in the future, and even has a certain chance of breaking through to the Eternal Realm! Of course, the success rate of possessing Innate Eternal Life is too low, so most people who want to seize Innate Eternal Life do not do it for this reason. In fact, the body of Innate Eternal Life contains extremely high innate Eternal rules. If one possesses an Innate Eternal Life, one can continuously comprehend the innate Eternal rules, which is of some help for future breakthroughs in realm and for charging toward the Eternal Realm. Many forces want to seize Innate Eternal Life with the goal of confining it and letting the Supreme Beings comprehend and cultivate from it. Moreover, the innate Eternal crystal core of Innate Eternal Life also has the effect of assisting Ninth-Level Supreme Beings in breaking through to the half-step Eternal Realm.”
Hearing these benefits from the spirit, Ye Tian finally understood why everyone wanted Innate Eternal Life.
At this moment, he felt somewhat excited.
If the Source God Pavilion’s speculation was true, and he found Innate Eternal Life, did that mean he could also replicate Innate Eternal Life?
Thinking of this, he immediately sent his clone to search and investigate for Innate Eternal Life in Fugu River.

Chapter 1610 Found It!

Chapter 1610 Found It!

Fenggu River.
Ye Tian kept activating his copying talent at all times to probe the surrounding situation. Although the innate Eternal Life did not yet fully come into being, so its talent would not be apparent, and he might not necessarily be able to detect it, there would certainly be many Eternal Tribulation Race members stationed near the innate Eternal Life.
Therefore, this method of probing was still useful.
However, Fenggu River was too large, and this way of searching would probably take a very long time.
During this period, Ye Tian was also discovered by the Eternal Tribulation Race. Although he did not have that section of a finger from an Eternal Realm powerful being with him, he still displayed not weak combat power as well as terrifying recovery and survival abilities. Even when surrounded by several Eternal Tribulation Race members of the sixth level, he could easily escape.
And as news of the innate Eternal Life spread, a large number of Supreme Beings poured into Fenggu River, bringing great pressure to the Eternal Tribulation Race in an instant.
A large number of Eternal Tribulation Race members were slain and became the gains of the Supreme Beings.
At the same time, the Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor of the Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain grew anxious.
If things continued to develop like this, Fenggu River was likely to be lost.
If that happened, the price paid by the Eternal Tribulation Race would all go to waste.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!!!
One after another half-step Eternal Realm Eternal Tribulation Race members appeared before Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor, among them the Eternal Tribulation Race’s number one half-step Eternal Realm being—Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor.
“Greetings, Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor said respectfully.
As soon as Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor arrived, he asked, “Tianxu, does Fenggu River possess innate Eternal Life? The battle for Fenggu River was entirely a plan initiated by you, and we did not interfere. But this time, the Eternal Tribulation Race has suffered heavy losses, and rumors outside say that innate Eternal Life has been born in Fenggu River, so I had no choice but to come and ask you.”
The other half-step Eternal Realm beings were also waiting for Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor’s answer.
After a moment of silence, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor replied, “Yes!”
He did not dare to lie; otherwise, Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor would certainly be able to find out. After all, Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor had greater authority than he did. With a single order, the situation in Fenggu River would certainly be placed before him.
Therefore, he could only answer truthfully.
“The matter of innate Eternal Life is very important, but you should have discussed it with me!” Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor said coldly.
“Yes!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor lowered his head, not daring to retort.
“Forget it, you did not do anything wrong in this matter. Anyone else would have done the same. Right now, we must completely capture Fenggu River, and absolutely cannot allow the innate Eternal Life to be exposed. At present, the outside world only suspects it, but has no definite evidence.” Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor said.
Afterward, Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor issued orders, dispatching more Eternal Tribulation Race members into Fenggu River and granting down all kinds of powerful treasures, deciding to protect the innate Eternal Life at all costs.
As a large number of Eternal Tribulation Race members reinforced Fenggu River, an even greater war began.
The entire Fenggu River turned into a huge battlefield, which made it harder for Su He to search for the innate Eternal Life.
At this time, even if he transformed into the body of an Eternal Tribulation Race member, he still had no way to find the innate Eternal Life.
Because the Eternal Tribulation Race members who knew about the innate Eternal Life were certainly very few; perhaps only a small number of Eternal Tribulation Race members throughout Fenggu River knew.
“Search slowly and depend on luck!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Time passed, and the slaughter in Fenggu River grew increasingly fierce. Ye Tian’s gains were not small either, and another Wind Source Gold Crystal mine vein appeared. Ye Tian also once again snatched a bit of Wind Source Gold Crystal.
In the blink of an eye, a Dark Age of time had passed.
Finally, on this day, Ye Tian’s copied body detected some Eternal Tribulation Ancestors.
These Eternal Tribulation Race members were located at the bottom of Fenggu River and were extremely concentrated.
Even when he came here, these Eternal Tribulation Race members did not attack him.
Moreover, these Eternal Tribulation Race members were hidden very secretly. If he did not use his copying talent to probe, he would have had no idea that there were still Eternal Tribulation Race members here.
“Could this be it?”
Ye Tian speculated.
He prepared to go down and take a look; even if this copied body were to fall, it would not matter much.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian moved to the bottom of Fenggu River and sensed a large formation.
This formation covered a region at the bottom of Fenggu River, which was why no one could discern what was going on here.
Ye Tian did not say another word and immediately attacked the formation.
Rumble rumble rumble!!!!!
With just a single strike, the formation shattered.
After all, such a concealment formation could not possibly have much defensive power; if its defense were too strong, it would be easily discovered.
When the formation shattered, two furious gazes from Eternal Tribulation Race members shot over.
The next moment, they attacked Ye Tian.
As soon as the fight began, Ye Tian was completely suppressed.
These two Eternal Tribulation Race members were very strong, no weaker than the top Void Son, and their distance from the Void Lord who had passed through the third level of the Void Tower was definitely not far. They were absolutely the most top-tier geniuses of the Eternal Tribulation Race in this era.
During the exchange, Ye Tian spied on the situation here.
He sensed a vast life aura, incomparably dense, and it emanated an exalted and supreme Eternal aura.
“It really is innate Eternal Life. Although it has not yet been fully nurtured, the day it is born is not far off!”
Ye Tian said in surprise.
At this moment.
Those two Eternal Tribulation Race members were also tense, while the other Eternal Tribulation Race members were not strong enough to be of help.
They could indeed defeat Ye Tian, but Ye Tian’s survival ability was too terrifying.
“He is hard to kill. Don’t kill him, seal him instead!”
The two Eternal Tribulation Race members decided.
443 Ye Tian was very clear that he probably would not be able to escape, after all, these two Eternal Tribulation Race members were truly very strong, so he did not make much resistance. Soon, the two Eternal Tribulation Race members sealed him up.
Of course, Ye Tian could at any time annihilate this copied body himself.
But he did not do so.
“The innate Eternal Life has not yet fully come into being. Even if I let the copied body bring that section of the Eternal Realm powerful being’s finger and destroy these two, I still would not be able to completely take over this place. By then, the Eternal Tribulation Race would certainly dispatch a large number of their clansmen to encircle and attack me. It would be better to wait until the final moment and then send the copied body over!”
Ye Tian thought to himself like this.
The Eternal Tribulation Race sealed Ye Tian, thinking the problem was solved, and immediately began to reestablish the formation to conceal this place.
Time passed slowly like this—
The Eternal Tribulation Race was also very anxious, because the day the innate Eternal Life would be born was drawing closer and closer. If they still could not completely occupy Fenggu River, then when the innate Eternal Life was born, it would draw the attention of a large number of Supreme Beings.
By then, the Eternal Tribulation Race would likely have to pay a very heavy price to have any hope of taking away the innate Eternal Life, and they might not even succeed.
On this day.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor and Natural Disaster Tribulation Ancestor held a meeting.
They had a new plan!.

Chapter 1611: Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor Who Severed His Own Cultivation!

Chapter 1611: Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor Who Severed His Own Cultivation!

At the meeting.
The Calamity Tribulation Ancestor ordered, “Tianxu, according to the current progress, it’s probably impossible to completely transform Wind Ancient River into an Eternal Tribulation Domain, so I order you to immediately enter Wind Ancient River and take away the Innate Eternal Lifeform when it is about to be born. In that case, no one will be able to stop you. Once you bring the Innate Eternal Lifeform here, even an Eternal Realm expert will find it very difficult to snatch the Innate Eternal Lifeform from us.”
“Calamity Tribulation Ancestor, I am at Half-Step Eternal Realm and can’t enter Wind Ancient River!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor said in a deep voice.
“No, you can enter. You know that!” Calamity Tribulation Ancestor said.
Suddenly.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor realized what Calamity Tribulation Ancestor meant by those words.
“Calamity Tribulation Ancestor, you want me to sever my cultivation?”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor was furious.
“That’s right!” Calamity Tribulation Ancestor said. “Your cultivation is already very difficult to advance any further. Severing your cultivation is not necessarily a bad thing, and after severing it, you can still continue cultivating. It won’t take long before you can ascend back to Half-Step Eternal Realm.”
“But if I sever my cultivation, my own potential and foundation will also be severed, and I will never be able to advance any further in the future!” Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor said angrily.
“This is for the sake of the clan!”
Calamity Tribulation Ancestor said.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor was unwilling to accept it. Although his hope of further progress was very slim, he was at least the third Tribulation Ancestor of the Eternal Tribulation Race!
But he did not dare oppose Calamity Tribulation Ancestor, because Calamity Tribulation Ancestor was truly powerful. If not for Calamity Tribulation Ancestor, the Eternal Tribulation Race would have been destroyed long ago.
“Calamity Tribulation Ancestor, I will sever my cultivation and enter Wind Ancient River!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor reluctantly agreed.
That’s right, everything was for the sake of the clan.
An Innate Eternal Lifeform, if used properly, would be enough to bring enormous benefits to the Eternal Tribulation Race, and could even allow the Eternal Tribulation Race to completely soar and rise, no longer having to cower within the Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain.
In the future, the Eternal Tribulation Race would even dare to appear openly in the Source Sea.
Time passed——
On this day, Ye Tian clearly sensed changes in the outside world.
Although he was sealed, he could still initially sense the situation outside.
At this moment, the phenomenon of the Innate Eternal Lifeform’s birth had already begun to appear.
“It’s time to prepare!”
Ye Tian immediately Annihilated this clone body of his.
He did not want to waste any more time. If he missed the opportunity and let the Eternal Tribulation Race instantly take away the Innate Eternal Lifeform, then he would have no time to encounter the Innate Eternal Lifeform.
After all, he was sealed now and could not copy the Innate Eternal Lifeform, so he could only come in again.
Void Source Hall.
Ye Tian accelerated time and soon condensed a clone body, then had the clone body carry that severed finger of an Eternal Realm mighty figure. After all, once he got close to the Innate Eternal Lifeform, he would probably have to fight the Eternal Tribulation Race.
No one knew what force the Eternal Tribulation Race would dispatch at the final moment, so he had to go there in his strongest state.
Very quickly, Ye Tian arrived at Wind Ancient River, entered it, and then traversed at top speed to the vicinity of the place where the Innate Eternal Lifeform was about to be born.
At this moment, the phenomenon here had already begun to expand. It probably wouldn’t be long before the entire Wind Ancient River was covered by it.
Boom!!!!!
A phantom of a one-horned creature, unimaginably vast, crouched and roared in the void, its voice rippling and shaking the sky.
This was the phantom of the phenomenon.
Very soon.
Several nearby Supremes sensed it and immediately reported it.
Thus, countless Supremes learned that an Innate Eternal Lifeform had been born here and rushed over.
At the same time, the Eternal Tribulation Race’s densely packed armies also entered this place.
Since it could no longer be hidden, there was no need to hide it anymore.
Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain.
Under the order of Calamity Tribulation Ancestor, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor began severing his cultivation.
In the void, blades formed from eternal laws cut into his body from the nothingness.
Waves of screams came from Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor’s mouth, and his aura kept dropping.
Ninefold Realm!
Eightfold Realm!
Sevenfold Realm!
It kept dropping until the peak of the Sixfold Realm, and only then did Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor stop.
Only the peak of the Sixfold Realm could enter Wind Ancient River, so reducing his cultivation to this level was enough.
At this time, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor quickly recovered from the injuries caused by severing his cultivation by consuming a precious healing treasure.
“Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor, although your cultivation has dropped to the peak of the Sixfold Realm, you have after all mastered an Eternal Technique, and your grasp of eternal laws far exceeds that of other Sixfold Realm experts. Moreover, your Eternal Body has reached the Perfected level, and your body is incomparably strong. You are enough to display strength comparable to the peak of the Eightfold Realm. With the aid of the clan’s treasures, you can even raise your strength to the Ninefold Realm. In Wind Ancient River, you will be an Invincible existence. I hope you won’t let the Eternal Tribulation Race down.” Calamity Tribulation Ancestor said.
“Don’t worry, I will definitely bring the Innate Eternal Lifeform back!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor guaranteed, though he was in a very bad mood. He casually dealt with the reply, then prepared to head to Wind Ancient River, not wanting to talk much more with Calamity Tribulation Ancestor here.
Very soon, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor descended upon Wind Ancient River.
-----------------------
The place where the Innate Eternal Lifeform was born.
Countless Supremes poured into this place and saw the phenomenon, their hearts filled with excitement.
This was an Innate Eternal Lifeform; its value was beyond imagination.
Moreover, outside, one Half-Step Eternal Realm expert after another had already offered sky-high prices. If they obtained the Innate Eternal Lifeform, even if they could not keep it themselves, handing it over to a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert would still earn them enough resources to cultivate to the Ninefold Realm.
“Kill the Eternal Tribulation Race!”
The army of Supremes and the army of the Eternal Tribulation Race began slaughtering each other.
Suddenly.
A gray palm emerged from the void and, with one strike, smashed countless Supremes into pieces.
The power of this strike was terrifying beyond compare!
“No!!!”
One Supreme after another was filled with terror, their bodies crushed into pieces under a terrifying force.
At this moment, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor appeared.
Some Supremes recognized Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor and immediately revealed expressions of disbelief.
“It’s the Eternal Tribulation Race’s third ancestor—Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor. How can he appear here? Only Eternal Tribulation Race members at the Sixfold Realm are allowed in here, and he is at Half-Step Eternal Realm!”
“No, he severed his cultivation. He is now at the Sixfold Realm!”
“Run! Even Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor at the Sixfold Realm is far from something we can deal with!”
A large number of Supremes fled, but Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor did not pursue them, because protecting the Innate Eternal Lifeform was the most important thing!
At this very moment, the Innate Eternal Lifeform was formally born.
And Ye Tian also approached here at the first possible moment, while activating his Copying talent.

Chapter 1612: The Eternal Realm Has Made Its Move!

Chapter 1612: The Eternal Realm Has Made Its Move!

The copying talent instantly enveloped the place where that innate eternal lifeform was located, detected the other party’s talent, and the copying talent memorized the other party’s body.
In the future, Ye Tian could completely copy the body of this innate eternal lifeform.
In addition.
The talent of this innate eternal lifeform was indeed extremely formidable; its entire body was made of eternal ancestral talents, showing just how powerful its talent was. No wonder it was an innate eternal lifeform.
Power Eternal Ancestral Talent!
Speed Eternal Ancestral Talent!
Defense Eternal Ancestral Talent!
……
Ye Tian already possessed these eternal ancestral talents, so he did not pay them much mind. But there was one eternal ancestral talent Ye Tian did not have, and that was the Undying Eternal Ancestral Talent.
This meant that this innate eternal lifeform possessed undying ability; once it grew up, it would be very hard to kill.
Of course, it had only just been born now. Although it was comparable to an Invincible, its strength was very weak and it could still be easily killed.
Suddenly.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor locked onto Ye Tian.
“You still dare to come closer? Seeking death!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor made his move.
He held a long spear and thrust it at Ye Tian, but he did not go all out.
In his view, Ye Tian was only a Third-Tier Invincible, not worthy of him using his full strength.
Therefore, the power of this strike was only at the Seventh-Tier.
However, this strike was blocked by Ye Tian with a single finger, not harming Ye Tian in the slightest.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor’s expression changed. Without another word, he immediately attacked with full power; he did not want Ye Tian to ruin this operation.
Boom!!!
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor attacked with all his strength, endless spacetime shattered, and that terrifying strike seemed as if it was about to Annihilation this boundless expanse.
To Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor, distance was no longer anything. Unless Ye Tian escaped beyond the range of his perception, he could not avoid this strike.
This was an attack power of the Ninth-Tier.
Ye Tian also did not hold back, directly activating the power of that Eternal Realm expert’s finger and unleashing the battle strength of a Ninth-Tier Invincible.
In an instant, a huge finger appeared in the void, as if it stood above all rules, descending directly before Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor and pressing down with a single finger.
With a loud boom!!!!
Ye Tian’s attack collided with Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor’s, causing a spacetime tide; even Fenggu River began to shake violently, and countless regions collapsed.
Crack, crack, crack!!!!
Numerous cracks appeared on Ye Tian’s body. This was the injury caused by forcibly activating the power of an Eternal Realm expert’s finger. However, he only looked a little ferocious; in truth, his injuries were not very serious.
After all, his Endless Eternal Body had now reached the Major realm, and his cultivation had also reached the Third-Tier Invincible realm, so the price he paid for activating the Eternal Realm expert’s finger was somewhat lighter.
But he knew very clearly that even so, he was still no match for Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor.
Even though Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor had cut away his cultivation, with the addition of various treasures, the battle strength he could actually unleash still reached the Ninth-Tier.
Moreover, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor could not only unleash Ninth-Tier battle strength once; he could do so every time.
“Go!”
Ye Tian did not want to continue fighting. He had already achieved his goal, so there was no need to keep taking risks.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian fled rapidly, and Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor struck again, but this was blocked by Ye Tian’s second Ninth-Tier Invincible attack, and he quickly left this place.
If Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor wanted to pursue and kill Ye Tian, Ye Tian probably would not be able to escape.
However, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor did not dare take the risk.
His current goal was to take the innate eternal lifeform back to the Eternal Tribulation Domain, not to kill Ye Tian.
He could tell that Ye Tian possessed a finger from an Eternal Realm expert, and that for some unknown method he had fused with that finger, allowing him to unleash its power and thus erupt with Ninth-Tier battle strength.
However, compared with the innate eternal lifeform, an Eternal Realm expert’s finger was worth far less.
Therefore, he would not take the risk for the sake of the Eternal Realm finger.
Immediately.
He seized the newly born innate eternal lifeform and was about to leave Fenggu River.
However, at this moment, a sudden change occurred.
A fair hand crossed spacetime and came forth; even Fenggu River’s rules found it difficult to restrict the arrival of this hand.
One could see the rules that restricted those above the Sixth-Tier Invincible realm in Fenggu River shattering inch by inch, the entire rule chains of Fenggu River collapsing, the rules of the entire void thrown into chaos, all of them unable to stop this hand’s arrival.
And when this hand arrived, the Eternal Tribulation Race and the Invincibles of Fenggu River were all frozen in place, practically unable to move.
Even Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor found it very hard to move; before this hand, he seemed like nothing more than an ant.
“Eternal Realm!!!!”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor was unwilling.
Just one step short!
If not for Ye Tian stopping him at that moment, perhaps he would already have left with the innate eternal lifeform.
Of course, perhaps that Eternal Realm expert had been hiding in the dark all along.
If that was the case, then no matter what, he could not take this innate eternal lifeform away.
“Why? Why are you coming to snatch the innate eternal lifeform?”
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor questioned.
“Noisy!”
Along with a crisp female voice, a finger descended, and with just one finger it heavily injured Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor and left him critically wounded and dying.
The next instant, the innate eternal lifeform disappeared.
It must be said that the Eternal Tribulation Race suffered too grievous a loss.
Not only had they lost a large number of clansmen, but Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor had even cut away his own cultivation for the sake of the innate eternal lifeform, only for it to still be snatched away at the critical moment by a mysterious Eternal Realm expert.
It could be said that the Eternal Tribulation Race lost miserably.
But the real winner, aside from that Eternal Realm expert, was Ye Tian.
At this time.
Ye Tian left Fenggu River and returned to the Void Source Hall.
Then, he activated layer upon layer of array restrictions in the Void Source Hall, and only then did he解除 the copied body, before copying the body of that innate eternal lifeform.
He did not want to painstakingly copy an innate eternal lifeform only for it to be snatched away by an Eternal Realm expert—that would be far too awkward.
Inside the Void Source Hall, a huge one-horned creature appeared; this was precisely the copied body of the innate eternal lifeform that Ye Tian had condensed.
Ye Tian existed in the body of the innate eternal lifeform and immediately sensed how extraordinary this body was.
Putting aside those eternal ancestral talents, just the countless innate eternal rules contained within its body were enough to allow Ye Tian to comprehend the innate eternal rules at every moment; his progress in the eternal rules was improving at an unbelievable speed.
Moreover, the body structure of the innate eternal lifeform was entirely worth studying by Ye Tian. This was simply an innate eternal body!
“In the years to come, I’ll carefully study and comprehend this innate eternal lifeform!”
Ye Tian murmured.


Chapter 1613: Ye Jingpeng Enters Supreme!

Chapter 1613: Ye Jingpeng Enters Supreme!

Ye Tian was in seclusion, comprehending the body of the Innate Eternal Life, and Fenggu River also underwent new changes.
The Eternal Tribulation Race had failed to seize the Innate Eternal Life. If they continued to stay in Fenggu River, they would probably suffer even greater losses.
Moreover, Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor had been severely injured and could not remain here; otherwise, there would be a risk of death.
Thus, the members of the Eternal Tribulation Race in Fenggu River withdrew one after another, and Fenggu Source Ancestor once again took control of Fenggu River, turning it back into a treasured land. The formations laid out by the Eternal Tribulation Race were destroyed one by one.
In this way, Fenggu River could no longer be transformed into an Eternal Tribulation Domain.
Supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain.
Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor returned and came before Tianzai Tribulation Ancestor, saying shamefully, “Tianzai Tribulation Ancestor, I failed!”
Tianzai Tribulation Ancestor also knew what had happened. Although he was furious, he also knew this could not be blamed on Tianxu Tribulation Ancestor.

Therefore, Tianzai Tribulation Ancestor said, “This cannot be blamed on you. Go back and heal properly. Let this matter rest!”
Let it rest!
Beyond that, what else could they do?
Could they still oppose an Eternal Realm being?
The Eternal Tribulation Race did not have an Eternal Realm, which was also why they had never dared to go out. If they had an Eternal Realm expert, they would not need to fear anything.
Gradually, the matter of the Innate Eternal Life passed.
……
Three Tribulation Yuan years passed.
At this time, the human race was developing rapidly, and a large number of Invincible beings had already been born, while Ye Jingpeng had already cultivated to the level of a First-Tier Invincible being.
Moreover, under the supply of resources from Ye Tian, his wife, children, and younger sister had also all cultivated to the level of First-Tier Invincible beings.
Now, Ye Jingpeng was condensing an Eternal Tribulation Body. Once he succeeded, Ye Tian would prepare to hand the Eternal Source Object—the Eternal Soul Wood—to him, helping him charge into the Supreme Being realm.
Compared with their progress, Ye Tian’s progress was the truly remarkable one.
He had comprehended the Innate Eternal Life for a full three Tribulation Yuan years; during this period, his grasp of the eternal rules had already surpassed many half-step Eternal Realm experts, and he had also created one half-step Eternal skill after another.
Not only that, but his insight into the Eternal Body had also reached an inconceivable level. Without any auxiliary resources, he had forcibly raised the Endless Eternal Body from the early Major stage to the peak of the mid Major stage.
It could be said that his current strength was far greater than before.
“It’s time to charge into the fourfold Supreme Being realm!”
Ye Tian murmured.
He took out the Immortal Source Heart Liquid, and after drinking it in one gulp, he very quickly charged into the fourfold Supreme Being realm, without feeling the slightest bottleneck along the way.
In fact, even without consuming the Immortal Source Heart Liquid, he probably could have broken through very easily, but for the sake of greater safety, he still used the Immortal Source Heart Liquid.
Fourfold Supreme Being was much stronger than threefold Supreme Being, and the gap between fourfold Supreme Being and threefold Supreme Being was even greater than the gap between threefold Supreme Being and twofold Supreme Being.
Especially for Ye Tian, this breakthrough caused his strength to soar by many times in an instant.
Now, even without borrowing the finger of an Eternal Realm expert, his conventional combat strength could reach the level of a sevenfold Supreme Being.
If he used that severed finger of an Eternal Realm expert, his combat strength would likely soar to the top-tier ninefold realm, and he could use it more than ten times.
Several dozen Great Calamity Epochs later, news came from Ye Jingpeng’s side.
Now, Ye Jingpeng had successfully condensed an Eternal Tribulation Body and could charge toward the Supreme Being realm with an incomparably profound foundation.

The bit of origin you absorbed before belonged to the origin of the Eternal Soul Wood. You can perfectly absorb its origin and charge into the Supreme Being realm. Take it!”
“Thank you, Ancestor!” Ye Jingpeng said excitedly.
Supreme Being!
This was the realm he had longed for day and night. Once he broke through to this realm, he would be among the top tier in the Tianlin Realm, fully capable of being compared with Tianfeng Source God.
Ye Jingpeng took the Eternal Soul Wood and went into seclusion in the Void Source Hall to charge toward the Supreme Being realm.
For him, this place was safer than the Tianlin Realm.
Time slowly passed.
Ye Tian did not pay much attention to Ye Jingpeng’s breakthrough, because this was a breakthrough that was one hundred percent guaranteed to succeed. If Ye Jingpeng could still fail to break through like this, then he would truly be useless, enough to break records.
Finally, on this day, Ye Jingpeng succeeded in his breakthrough and stepped into the Supreme Being realm.
After Ye Jingpeng broke through, the origin of the Dark Forbidden Domain once again surged upward by a small margin.
“He’s broken through. If we cultivate one more Supreme Being, then the Dark Forbidden Domain should be able to become an Eternal Heaven and Earth!”
Ye Tian murmured.
The next one most likely to break through was Ye Xingchen. Ye Tian planned to let Ye Xingchen fuse the power of the Ancient Star Stone and let him condense an Ancient Star Body, even if it was a defective Ancient Star Body.
For this, he needed to prepare countless precious resources to help Ye Xingchen grow; otherwise, Ye Xingchen simply would not be able to comprehend the Ancient Star Body, and even cultivating for billions of Tribulation Yuan years would be useless.
In order to let Ye Xingchen successfully condense the Ancient Star Body, Ye Tian also re-fused and produced an Ancient Star Body Eternal Ancestral Gift, and bestowed it upon Ye Xingchen.
.... ...... 0
Coupled with the massive supply of resources, Ye Xingchen now could be considered to have initially created an Ancient Star Body suitable for himself, but its defects were quite serious. Still, it was enough to compare with a lower Eternal Body.
This was already the utmost that Ye Tian could do.
However, according to Ye Tian’s expectations, for Ye Xingchen to break through to the Supreme Being realm would require at least one hundred Tribulation Yuan years, and that was only if countless resources were supplied; otherwise, it would take at least tens of thousands of Tribulation Yuan years or even more.
As for Ye Xingchen’s cultivation plan, Ye Tian had already arranged it.
As for the rest of the time, Ye Tian no longer needed to worry about it.
Before he knew it, another ten Tribulation Yuan years passed, and Ye Tian had also raised his cultivation to the peak of the fourfold Supreme Being realm. The next step was to charge into the fivefold Supreme Being realm.
The Void Source Hall happened to have a treasure suitable for breaking through to the fivefold Supreme Being realm. Ye Tian had never been willing to use it before, after all, using it at a low level would have been too wasteful.
This treasure was the Azure Lihuo Flame Crystal.
After that, Ye Tian used the Azure Lihuo Flame Crystal to break through, and similarly, he very easily broke through to the fivefold Supreme Being realm.
After breaking through to the fivefold Supreme Being realm, Ye Tian’s strength surged once again.
With his current strength, even his conventional combat power was enough to rival a relatively weak eightfold Supreme Being.
And he could also fully use the finger of an Eternal Realm expert; as long as the duration was not long, the burden on his body would not be great.
At this time, Ye Tian was fully equivalent to a true ninefold Supreme Being and.


Chapter 1614 First Eternal Skill!

Chapter 1614 First Eternal Skill!

“It’s time to completely settle the matters in the Starry Ancient Domain. It’s no longer of much value to me there, and it’s not worth having a clone permanently stationed there!”
Ye Tian muttered.
After all, his regular combat strength could already reach the Ninth Supreme Being, and Star Ancestor’s strength was at about that level too. Although he was a bit stronger than Ye Tian, he definitely wasn’t much stronger.
Therefore, Star Ancestor was not of much value to him either.
Besides, Star Ancestor wouldn’t have many treasures on him, and there was no need for him to keep squeezing him for more benefits.
On this day, Ye Tian’s Ancient Star Ancestor clone arrived at the Ancient Star Tower.
“Xu Chen, you’re here!”
Seeing Ye Tian arrive, Star Ancestor showed himself.
“Star Ancestor, I’m here to bid you farewell!”
Ye Tian said.
When Star Ancestor heard Ye Tian’s tone, his expression immediately changed.
“Xu Chen, what do you mean by this?” Star Ancestor said coldly. “There is a contract between us.”
“That’s right!” Ye Tian nodded. “There is indeed a contract between us, but what if this is a special clone?”
“A special clone!”
Star Ancestor’s expression changed drastically.
If the one who had signed the contract with him was Ye Tian’s special clone, then if Ye Tian destroyed this body himself, the contract would no longer count, and it would be impossible to restrain Ye Tian anymore.
“Who exactly are you?”
Star Ancestor roared.
He finally understood why Ye Tian had killed the ten Supreme Beings, and why everything he had done was fundamentally not beneficial to the development of the Ancient Star Race.
The reason for all of it was that Ye Tian was a lifeform from the outside world. He had created this Ancient Star Race clone and sent the clone into the Starry Ancient Domain, allowing it to grow to this day.
He hated it!
“Damn it, why did I not see that this was a clone?”
Star Ancestor said in regret.
If it had been an ordinary clone, he would definitely have seen through it.
But Ye Tian’s clone was actually no different from the main body, so Star Ancestor could not tell.
“Star Ancestor, I’ve told you the reason, so you no longer have any doubts. I’ll seal this place, and your consciousness will no longer be able to break the seal. Moreover, I’ll take away most of the Ancient Star Race’s resources.”
Ye Tian said.
“Xu Chen, if I can get out, I’ll definitely kill you!”
Star Ancestor roared.
“Star Ancestor, do you think that when you come out, you’ll still be my opponent?” Ye Tian sneered.
Then Ye Tian began sealing this space.
He exerted almost all of his comprehension of the Eternal Rule, setting up an incomparably complex restriction. Even if the outside Ancient Star Race wanted to communicate with Star Ancestor, they would not be able to do so.
After setting up the restriction, Ye Tian, under his own identity, took away all the treasure vaults accumulated by the Ancient Star Race over countless ages. He also entered one Ancient Star Race force after another and forcibly took the treasures from their treasure vaults.
In almost no time at all, the Ancient Star Race was completely looted by Ye Tian, and the entire Ancient Star Race fell into chaos.
After that, Ye Tian copied a body of a First-Tier Invincible Being and entered the Starry Ancient Domain, bringing back all the resources plundered by the Ancient Star Race clone.
Then Ye Tian directly Annihilated this clone.
The identity of Xu Chen would completely disappear from this world.
Inside the Ancient Star Tower.
Star Ancestor looked at the restriction sealing this place and deeply felt how difficult the situation was.
Apart from the fact that the sealing power was not very strong, the profundity of the seal itself was so troublesome that even he found it extremely hard to deal with.
“Xu Chen’s mastery of the Eternal Rule has actually risen to this level, absolutely comparable to half-step Eternal Realm. Could he be the clone of some half-step Eternal Realm expert?”
Star Ancestor was utterly despairing.
The Ancient Star Race could not save him. He was probably never going to get out for all eternity.
---------------------
“The Ancient Star Race’s resources are pretty good, but unfortunately they’re not very useful to me. Let’s give them to human race development!”
Ye Tian then had these resources sent to the Human Race Sacred Hall, where they would serve as resources for the future development of the human race.
And his main task now was to help his son Ye Xingchen break through to the Supreme Being realm. Once Ye Xingchen made the breakthrough, then the Dark Forbidden Domain could evolve into Eternal Heaven and Earth, and it would become the true base of the human race.
By then, he could also return to the human race’s base and truly guard the human race.
Moreover, with his own Eternal Heaven and Earth, the human race would truly be able to rise.
In addition, Ye Tian had another goal, and that was to create an Eternal Skill.
A truly top-notch half-step Eternal Skill not only mastered multiple half-step Eternal Skills, but also at least one Eternal Skill. Previously, Ye Tian had been unable to master an Eternal Skill, not only because his cultivation was too low, but more importantly because his understanding of the Eternal Rule was not profound enough, and he did not understand Eternal Skills sufficiently.
But now, he was constantly comprehending the innate Eternal Rule within the innate Eternal lifeform, and his mastery of the Eternal Rule had reached an unimaginable level. Therefore, he had hope of creating an Eternal Skill........
This time, Ye Tian planned to begin with the Destroying Finger, and create an Eternal Finger Skill.
In order to create this finger skill, Ye Tian did not care about time, and endless ages passed.
One hundred great tribulation eras!
One thousand great tribulation eras!
One tribulation era!
Ten tribulation eras!
……
It had to be said that creating an Eternal Skill was indeed incomparably difficult. Many half-step Eternal Realm experts did not know how many tens of thousands of tribulation eras they had spent before they luckily created an Eternal Skill. Naturally, Ye Tian could not create one easily either.
Finally, in the fifty-sixth tribulation era, Ye Tian created a finger skill at the level of an Eternal Skill.
He named this finger skill the Ruinous Finger, meaning to ruin everything.
After the Eternal Skill, Ruinous Finger, was created, Ye Tian underwent a transformation. Not long after that, his cultivation rose to the peak of the Fifth Supreme Being, only one step away from the Sixth Supreme Being.
After some more years passed, news came from Ye Xingchen’s side.
He was about to begin his charge toward the Supreme Being realm.
Under Ye Tian’s vigorous cultivation and pressure, Ye Xingchen had also lived up to expectations and not disappointed him. He finally broke through to the peak of First-Tier Invincible and created an Invincible Skill that suited the Ancient Star Physique.
Now, Ye Xingchen was preparing to condense the Eternal Tribulation Body. Once he succeeded, he would be able to absorb the origin of the Ancient Star Stone and charge toward the Supreme Being realm.
After receiving the massive amount of Eternal resources Ye Tian had bestowed upon him, Ye Xingchen successfully condensed the Eternal Tribulation Body.
Then he began absorbing the origin of the Ancient Star Stone to break through to Supreme Being.
“I must succeed!”
Ye Xingchen calmed himself down and said.
He knew his own potential very well. If not for his father’s support, he would probably never be able to step into the Supreme Being realm, let alone advance to Supreme Being with such a solid foundation now.
This was his fortune!
So, he could not let his father down.
Time passed. After a long while, a Supreme Being aura spread from the space where Ye Xingchen was in seclusion.
Ye Xingchen had successfully broken through to the Supreme Being realm.
And the Dark Forbidden Domain had also given birth to three Supreme Beings, and was about to undergo a transformation.


Chapter 1615 Dark Forbidden Domain Finally Becomes an Eternal Heaven..

Chapter 1615 Dark Forbidden Domain finally becomes an Eternal Heaven!

Dark Forbidden Domain.
Endless source sea origin energy surged back into the Dark Forbidden Domain. At this time, the Dark Forbidden Domain was like a balloon rapidly expanding, yet it would not explode, as if it could expand without limit.
And the living beings within the Dark Forbidden Domain were blessed as well; they also obtained tremendous benefits, and their cultivation bases surged one after another.
Almost all the living beings in the Dark Forbidden Domain were human race, and long before Ye Xingchen was assaulting the Supreme Being realm, the Human Race Sacred Hall had already sent out a message that all human race members in other foreign heavens and worlds must enter the Dark Forbidden Domain to enjoy this opportunity.
Thus, the Dark Forbidden Domain was densely packed with humans.
As the Dark Forbidden Domain continued to expand, endless Eternal Continent lands were born, and boundless resources were being nurtured.
The process of the Dark Forbidden Domain advancing into an Eternal Heaven would take a very long time, roughly a great tribulation cycle.
Of course, before the Dark Forbidden Domain was completely stabilized, Supreme Beings could not enter it either.
Moreover, even after it stabilized, the Eternal Heaven would have a protection period, during which only the native Supreme Beings of the Eternal Heaven would be allowed to enter, and outsiders would not be permitted.
This protection period lasted one hundred thousand tribulation eras, meant to prevent other Supreme Beings from entering the newly born Eternal Heaven to plunder resources.
Because newly born Eternal Heavens would give birth to large amounts of Eternal resources, and even many resources that could rapidly enhance the cultivation of Supreme Beings. This was also why the three Supreme Beings of the Tianlin Realm were so much stronger than the other Supreme Beings.
Because they had occupied the precious resources produced at the birth of the Tianlin Realm, their strength naturally improved very quickly, and they thus stood above the other Supreme Beings.
The Dark Forbidden Domain advancing into an Eternal Heaven could no longer be concealed.
Ye Tian had previously hidden the Dark Forbidden Domain, but now the formation was broken apart as the Dark Forbidden Domain advanced, and it could no longer be hidden.
Some nearby foreign heavens and worlds immediately had Invincible Beings sense the matter of the Dark Forbidden Domain's advancement, and thus the news quickly spread to the Tianlin Realm, which was not far from the Dark Forbidden Domain.
At the first moment, one Supreme Being after another from the Tianlin Realm rushed toward the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Even the three Supreme Beings of the Tianlin Realm had come.
Tianlin Source Ancestor, Qiuyè Source Ancestor, Jianheng Source Ancestor.
These three Supreme Beings were the undisputed three great Supreme Beings of the Tianlin Realm. Among them, Tianlin Source Ancestor was a sixth-level Supreme Being, while Qiuyè Source Ancestor and Jianheng Source Ancestor were both fifth-level Supreme Beings. Their strength completely crushed the other Supreme Beings, and they could slaughter an ordinary Supreme Being with a single hand.
……
“Which foreign heaven and world is this?”
Tianlin Source Ancestor asked in confusion.
He only secluded himself for a bit longer, so how did an Eternal Heaven suddenly appear nearby?
“Lord Tianlin Source Ancestor, this should be the Dark Forbidden Domain, under the Endless Ancestor!”
Tianfeng Source God spoke up.
Endless Ancestor was also Ye Tian’s current title. After becoming a Supreme Being, he planned to use the title Endless Ancestor.
Endless Ancestor?
Tianlin Source Ancestor had never heard of this title, but he very much wanted to see him.
“Tianfeng Source God, can you contact Endless Ancestor?” Qiuyè Source God asked.
“Yes!”
Tianfeng Source God immediately contacted Ye Tian.
In truth, Ye Tian had been paying close attention to the situation in the Dark Forbidden Domain from the shadows. After receiving Tianfeng Source God’s transmission, he immediately came out.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian walked out from the void and looked at the many Supreme Beings of the Tianlin Realm.
In the past, he could be considered to belong to the Tianlin Realm, but now he belonged to the Dark Forbidden Domain, this Eternal Heaven.
“Fifth-level Supreme Being!!!!”
Tianfeng Source God widened his eyes, somewhat unable to believe it.
It had only been how long since he last saw Ye Tian, and Ye Tian had already advanced to this realm?
How difficult was it for a Supreme Being to raise their realm? Which one of them did not spend countless tribulation eras, and some even remained forever stuck in one realm without being able to break through.
Yet Ye Tian, without a sound, had advanced to the peak of fifth-level Supreme Being. It seemed that before long, he would have the hope of advancing to sixth-level Supreme Being.
Tianlin Source Ancestor looked at Ye Tian and felt a fatal threat.
In his perception, Ye Tian was very strong, stronger than him.
“Impossible, he is only a fifth-level Supreme Being. How could he be stronger than me? It should be an illusion!”
Tianlin Source Ancestor thought inwardly.
However, he would not underestimate Ye Tian. He greeted him very politely: “Greetings, Endless Ancestor!”
“And you are...”

“Greetings, Tianlin Source Ancestor!”
Ye Tian said politely.

Ye Tian nodded slightly.
Then the two chatted for a while.

He did not want to become enemies with Ye Tian either; there was no benefit in that.
It was fortunate that he did not have such an idea, or he would have been in great despair.
Unknowingly, a great tribulation cycle passed.
At this time, the Dark Forbidden Domain had completely become a side of Eternal Heaven.
And Ye Tian’s family members all returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain. Although Ye Tian’s true body had not returned, his clone body had come back.
Ye Xingchen and Ye Jinpeng, these two Supreme Beings, naturally also returned, and some Invincible Beings of the human race in the Tianlin Realm also returned to the Eternal Heaven. Even some Invincible Beings who had joined Tianfeng Sea were not retained by Tianfeng Sea; Tianfeng Source God did not dare retain them either!
Since the Dark Forbidden Domain had only recently advanced into an Eternal Heaven, the entire human race was still somewhat chaotic.
Thus, the upper echelons of the human race were dividing regions and managing the human race separately. Many, many human race members obtained large tracts of fiefdoms.
Moreover, the human race encouraged the establishment of various forces, using those forces to manage the many regions. Otherwise, relying solely on the Human Race Sacred Hall to manage everything simply would not be enough.
It took as many as several dozen great tribulation cycles before the Dark Forbidden Domain was finally completely stabilized.
After that, Ye Tian personally established countless teleportation formations for the human race, otherwise ordinary teleportation formations simply could not be used to teleport within an Eternal Heaven. In addition, an Eternal Heaven was simply too vast; unless one had reached the level of Ancestor, there was no way to fly very far at all.
With the Dark Forbidden Domain stabilized, Ye Tian no longer needed to worry about it.
After that, he began collecting all kinds of rare resources in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
His countless clones were scattered throughout the Dark Forbidden Domain, and whenever important resources were born, he would take them away.
Most of the resources were of no use to him at all, but they could be stored in the Sacred Hall. A small portion was given to Ye Jinpeng and Ye Xingchen and the others to use; they had only just advanced to first-level Supreme Being realm.
They were in urgent need of these resources, and Ye Jinpeng and Ye Xingchen no longer cultivated either; they were all searching for resources suitable for Supreme Beings to use.
It could be said that this era was their best era, and also their opportunity.
In this way, the Dark Forbidden Domain ushered in an era of rapid human race development, and countless Invincible Beings were born.


Chapter 1616 Regular Combat Power: Top-Tier Eight-Stage Supreme Being..

Chapter 1616 Regular Combat Power: Top-Tier Eight-Stage Supreme Being!

In the blink of an eye, the Black Dark Forbidden Domain had passed through over a thousand kalpa-era periods.
By now, the human race had produced many powerhouses at the Invincible level; there were even many third-tier Invincible ones, but second-tier Invincible ones were still relatively rare.
And after experiencing over a thousand kalpa-era periods, Ye Tian’s cultivation had not only reached the extreme of the five-stage Peak Supreme Being, he had also created another Eternal technique, called the Shattering Void Sword. It fused various Eternal laws and was an incomparably powerful Eternal technique, much stronger than the Annihilation Finger.
Strictly speaking, the Annihilation Finger was meant to activate a sliver of a finger from a powerhouse of the Eternal realm; in reality, it was not very powerful. The Shattering Void Sword, on the other hand, was the Eternal technique Ye Tian created for regular combat power.
He had originally also wanted to create an Eternal technique for defense or speed, but felt that he currently did not really need one.
Having the Endless Eternal Body, his ability to preserve his life far surpassed other Supreme Beings, so he did not need a defensive Eternal technique to save his life. As for a speed-type Eternal technique, it was not very necessary either; at least it was not as important as an offensive Eternal technique.
“It’s time to break through to the six-stage Supreme Being. I’ve stayed at the five-stage Supreme Being for too long!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Regarding the attempt to reach the six-stage Supreme Being, he was now very confident, and thus he did not go collect resources to assist the breakthrough.
Afterward, he directly chose to break through.
After a long period of time, Ye Tian successfully shattered the bottleneck and advanced to the six-stage Supreme Being realm, with his strength surging once again by a large margin.
From the six-stage Supreme Being onward, it would truly be very difficult to break through a single realm in the future. It was often not something talent alone could determine; unless one was a congenital Eternal Life, it would be very hard to break through the shackles. One needed a very long span of time and many resources to break through the bottleneck.
For example, Tianlin Source Ancestor had spent who knew how many tens of thousands of kalpa-era periods, and still had not broken through to the seven-stage Supreme Being realm to this day.
Among the countless Eternal heavens in the Source Sea, the number of Supreme Beings below the six-stage Supreme Being was large, but the number of Supreme Beings at the seven-stage Supreme Being and above was extremely small.
Any seven-stage Supreme Being held an incomparably high status, and was almost considered a top existence in the Source Sea.
After Ye Tian became a six-stage Supreme Being, he also knew that in the short term he had no way to charge into the seven-stage Supreme Being realm; the difficulty would be extremely, extremely great.
However, he still needed to make preparations for breaking through to the seven-stage Supreme Being in the future.
This day.
He, as usual, came to the Source God Pavilion. The Source God Pavilion’s transactions had brought him many benefits; whenever he lacked some treasure, he could come here to trade for it, without having to spend long years searching for something.
Suddenly.
The Twelve Ancestors of the Source God Pavilion announced a piece of news: the Source God Pavilion was going to invite one inner-circle member.
Aside from the Twelve Ancestors, below them were 108 inner-circle members, and outside the inner-circle members were a large number of outer-circle members.
Outer-circle members had no real constraints and could trade freely, but they could not obtain many of the benefits.
Inner-circle members, however, could not only receive guidance from the Twelve Ancestors, but also enjoy some special treatment and benefits, which was why everyone wanted to become an inner-circle member.
However, inner-circle members were almost fixed; the number of 108 inner-circle members would not change unless another inner-circle member fell, and only then would one be invited from among the outer-circle members.
Of course, to become an inner-circle member, one still had to undergo an assessment. Only after passing the assessment would one truly become an inner-circle member.
……
“Master, I suggest you become an inner-circle member of the Source God Pavilion. The Twelve Ancestors know many secrets, and there are some resources that only the Twelve Ancestors know about. Back then, the previous master was invited to become one of the inner-circle members. And within the Source God Pavilion, aside from the Twelve Ancestors, there are also some Half-Step Eternal realm experts among the inner-circle members, though they are extremely low-key々〃.”
The artifact spirit suggested.
“Then let’s give it a try!”
Ye Tian nodded.
Afterwards, Ye Tian applied for the inner-circle member assessment.
He felt that with his current strength, he should be enough to serve as an inner-circle member of the Source God Pavilion, right?
Source God Pavilion.
After Ye Tian’s application passed, he immediately entered an assessment area.
Whoosh!
A eight-stage Supreme Being appeared before Ye Tian; this person was a member of the Source God Pavilion’s inner circle.
“Six-stage Supreme Being?”
Seeing Ye Tian’s cultivation realm, the other party was somewhat surprised. A mere six-stage Supreme Being dared to apply to become an inner-circle member of the Source God Pavilion?
Among the Source God Pavilion’s inner-circle members, the topmost were Half-Step Eternal realm experts, the majority were nine-stage Supreme Beings, a minority were eight-stage Supreme Beings, and only a very few were seven-stage Supreme Beings.
As for six-stage Supreme Beings, there had practically never been a precedent for becoming inner-circle members.
“Primordial Ancestor, your assessment is to withstand my attacks for one minute. If you succeed, you will enter the waiting selection pool. The Twelve Ancestors will choose based on the combat situations of all of you applicants; whether you can ultimately be selected will depend on luck.” After speaking, the other party added, “By the way, my name is Wuyuan Source Ancestor!”
“．‖ Wuyuan Source Ancestor, make your move!”
Ye Tian said indifferently.
Boom!!!!
The two exchanged blows.
Wuyuan Source Ancestor specialized in fist techniques, and each punch unleashed terrifying attacks, shaking the Source God Pavilion’s void continuously.
In Ye Tian’s eyes, Wuyuan Source Ancestor was a very powerful eight-stage Supreme Being, but not among the most top-tier eight-stage Supreme Beings, simply because Wuyuan Source Ancestor did not even know a single Half-Step Eternal technique. He was merely extremely skilled in many Supreme techniques, having reached the level of using them as he pleased.
“Shattering Void Sword!”
Ye Tian held a top-grade source weapon longsword and, with one sword strike, tore through endless laws as it landed on Wuyuan Source Ancestor.
With a thunderous boom!
The two were actually evenly matched.
No, it should be said that Ye Tian held the upper hand.
At this moment, a sword wound appeared on Wuyuan Source Ancestor’s body and would not disperse at all.
“How is this possible? You actually created an Eternal technique! And you are merely a six-stage Supreme Being, yet your combat power can actually match a top-tier eight-stage Supreme Being!”
Wuyuan Source Ancestor was shocked.
Ye Tian, however, was not surprised at all. When he was at the five-stage Supreme Being, his regular combat power was already enough to match weaker eight-stage Supreme Beings.
Now that his cultivation had risen to the six-stage Supreme Being realm, his combat power was naturally terrifying, almost comparable to Tianxu Calamity Ancestor after self-severing his cultivation.
It was just that Tianxu Calamity Ancestor possessed all kinds of powerful secret treasures and weapons, whereas he did not, so his regular combat power still could not match a nine-stage Supreme Being.
However, once he used the finger of an Eternal realm powerhouse, he would probably be able to unleash a strike comparable to a weaker Half-Step Eternal realm expert.
“Wuyuan Source Ancestor, do we still need to continue fighting?”
Ye Tian asked.
“Of course. I need to test your strength, and that is also the rule set by the Twelve Ancestors!”
Wuyuan Source Ancestor said.
Boom boom boom!!!齐!
The two continued exchanging blows. Ye Tian’s strength was indeed much greater than Wuyuan Source Ancestor’s, and he kept suppressing Wuyuan Source Ancestor.


Chapter 1617 Primordial Sea!

Chapter 1617 Primordial Sea!

A minute passed.
Ye Tian and Wuyuan Source Ancestor both stopped fighting. The result was very obvious: Ye Tian passed the assessment.
Of course, whether he could be selected still depended on the Twelve Ancestors’ choice.
“Endless Ancestor, your strength is truly powerful, far beyond my imagination. I believe the Twelve Ancestors will definitely choose you as an inner-circle member!”
Wuyuan Source Ancestor said in a certain tone.
“I hope so!”
Ye Tian smiled faintly and did not worry at all. Even if he could not enter the Source God Pavilion inner circle this time, it was no big deal. After all, he would only be missing one opportunity, and it would not affect him much.
Not long after, all the applicants’ assessments came to an end.
And the battles of every applicant who passed were all reviewed once by the Twelve Ancestors. When they saw the battle scene between Ye Tian and Wuyuan Source Ancestor, each and every one of them was shocked.
They all understood Wuyuan Source Ancestor’s strength, yet a Sixteenth Supreme Being could suppress Wuyuan Source Ancestor. How was that possible?
Unless it was a half-step Eternal Realm powerhouse who had cut down their cultivation after reaching that level, only then could they possess such battle strength.
But it was obvious that Ye Tian was not such a half-step Eternal Realm powerhouse, otherwise Wuyuan Source Ancestor should have been able to tell.
Whoosh!
Wuyuan Source Ancestor was summoned before the Twelve Ancestors.
Fenggu Source Ancestor asked, “Wuyuan Source Ancestor, how did Endless Ancestor feel to you?”
Wuyuan Source Ancestor thought for a moment before saying, “That Endless Ancestor is monstrously gifted. Not only did he create an Eternal technique, but what he condensed should also be an Eternal Body, and at the very least, an upper-level Eternal Body. Moreover, his foundation is incomparably solid, and his comprehension of Eternal laws also surpasses that of ordinary half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses.”
Wuyuan Source Ancestor’s account was about the same as the Twelve Ancestors’ guesses.
After Wuyuan Source Ancestor left, the Twelve Ancestors had made their decision.
“This Sixteenth Supreme Being called Endless Ancestor has potential that may surpass us. I suggest taking him into the Source God Pavilion inner-circle member ranks.”
“Naturally, he should be taken in. We must be fair; he is indeed extremely outstanding and qualified to become one of the inner-circle members.”
“Then let’s choose him!”
The Twelve Ancestors unanimously passed it and chose Ye Tian to become a Source God Pavilion inner-circle member.
