Source God Pavilion.
In the misty void, black thrones appeared one after another. Each throne had a person seated on it; these black thrones were occupied by Source God Pavilion inner-circle members.
Among them, there were twelve golden thrones, and the ones seated on them were the Twelve Ancestors.
At this moment, one throne was empty, but very soon a figure appeared and sat down on it.
The one who arrived was Ye Tian.
“Welcome, new member!”
“Welcome, new member!”
“Welcome, new member!”
Starting with the Twelve Ancestors, one inner-circle member after another offered their welcome.
“Greetings, everyone!”
Ye Tian also greeted them.
At this time, Fenggu Source Ancestor tossed over a mass of information: “Endless Ancestor, these are some records regarding the inner-circle members. After you absorb them, you’ll understand.”
Ye Tian nodded, took hold of the mass of information, and quickly learned about some matters concerning the inner-circle members.
For example, the inner-circle members of the Source God Pavilion controlled the birthplaces of certain special resources, and now Ye Tian also knew about them.
Most importantly, the Source God Pavilion inner-circle members could go to the Primordial Sea.
The Primordial Sea was a special blessed land, the place where the source of the Source Sea was born. Every drop of seawater there was condensed from boundless Source Sea origin energy.
However, the Primordial Sea was located deep within a special Source Sea spacetime. Without a special guide, it was impossible to find the Primordial Sea at all.
Because of this, ordinary Supreme Beings simply did not know of the Primordial Sea’s existence, and had not even heard of it.
Only some powerful factions knew about the Primordial Sea, and the Source God Pavilion had the means to enter it. Every inner-circle member could enter the Primordial Sea.
For example, this time, just after Ye Tian became a Source God Pavilion inner-circle member, the Source God Pavilion was preparing to enter the Primordial Sea.
At the meeting.
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor said, “The origin tide of the Primordial Sea is about to begin this time, and it is the best opportunity to enter the Primordial Sea. However, after entering the Primordial Sea, I will not be able to protect you, and the likelihood of perishing is rather high. If you do not want to go, you may stay behind. Once we come out of the Primordial Sea, we will hold a private exchange meeting, and everyone can trade the treasures and resources they need.”
“Zhenhe Sword Ancestor, I won’t be going this time!”
One Eight Supreme Being said.
Those few Seven Supreme Beings also immediately declared that they would not enter the Primordial Sea, clearly lacking confidence in themselves.
“Endless Ancestor, are you going?” Zhenhe Sword Ancestor looked at Ye Tian. “Your potential is very high, so I suggest you don’t go this time. You can go next time.”
“Zhenhe Sword Ancestor, I’m going!” Ye Tian said. “I have a special avatar. This time, I’ll enter the Primordial Sea with my avatar, so even if it perishes, the loss won’t be great.”
Special avatar!
Many Supreme Beings were immediately full of envy upon hearing this.
The stronger the path of cultivation one walked, the harder it was to possess a special avatar. Moreover, many avatars had limited potential and simply could not become Supreme Beings. Thus, having such a powerful avatar was truly exceedingly difficult.
Generally speaking, the stronger one’s cultivation, the fewer powerhouses there were who possessed avatars.
“A special avatar!”
Upon hearing this, Zhenhe Sword Ancestor no longer tried to persuade Ye Tian.
With a special avatar, Ye Tian was not afraid of perishing at all, so he naturally should go to the Primordial Sea and try his luck.
This time, a total of nine Supreme Beings were unwilling to go to the Primordial Sea, while all the other Supreme Beings would go.
This time, not only was Ye Tian entering the Primordial Sea for the first time, but many Supreme Beings had also joined the Source God Pavilion inner-circle member ranks long ago, yet had never been to the Primordial Sea before. Thus, Zhenhe Sword Ancestor and the others began explaining the specific situation of the Primordial Sea.
For example, after entering the Primordial Sea, one must leave before the origin tide ends; otherwise, one would be trapped in the Primordial Sea and would certainly perish.
To this day, no one trapped in the Primordial Sea has ever been able to survive.
Because a half-step Eternal Realm powerhouse had once tested this with a special avatar and failed to survive. Once the origin tide ended, the Primordial Sea would release a terrifying black mist that would devour even half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses.
Therefore, one had to leave before the origin tide ended.
Second, the Primordial Sea would give birth to many treasures. Eternal source objects were only ordinary among them; Eternal resources were everywhere, and there were also many resources helpful for breakthroughs from Sixteenth Heavens to Seventeenth Heavens and even Eighteenth Heavens.
Moreover, there were also many resources there that could enhance Eternal Bodies.
Not only that, the Primordial Sea also had some treasures that would drive even half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses crazy.
The Twelve Ancestors listed a treasure catalog and gave one to each member, lest anyone fail to recognize a treasure and miss it. That would truly be a pity!.


Chapter 1618 Entering the Primal Sea, Astonishing Harvest!

Chapter 1618 Entering the Primal Sea, Astonishing Harvest!

Ye Tian also received the treasure list sent over by the Twelve Ancestors. Many of the treasures were things he had never even heard of; there was even one treasure that could forcibly raise a Ninth-Tier Supreme Being to the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
This treasure was called Void True Liquid.
But Ye Tian was very clear that a treasure like this would definitely be incomparably rare. Even in the Primal Sea, it might not exist; there was only a very small chance of it appearing.
Moreover, once it really came into being, a group of top Half-Step Eternal Realm experts would probably fight over it, and it would never轮到 a Ninth-Tier Supreme Being to fight for it.
If a Ninth-Tier Supreme Being could obtain it so easily, then Star Ancestor would not have been trapped at the Ninth-Tier Supreme Being realm for countless years back then, only to be suppressed in the end.
Not long after.
The Twelve Ancestors led many inner-circle members of the Source God Pavilion to the Primal Sea. Everyone kept traveling through space until they finally arrived at an area of the source sea.
There seemed to be nothing here, as if it were no different from any other place and nothing special at all.
But very soon, one Supreme Being after another gathered here; the lowest cultivation level among them was basically Seventh-Tier Supreme Being, and most were Ninth-Tier Supreme Beings as well as Half-Step Eternal Realm experts.
Ye Tian looked very inconspicuous here, but his strength was definitely not weak, placing him at an intermediate level.
Time slowly passed, and the many Supreme Beings and Half-Step Eternal Realm experts waited here slowly, without the slightest impatience.
Suddenly.
This area began to ripple.
Ye Tian had a deep understanding of the Eternal laws, and thus sensed the upheaval of space-time here, as if a special origin power were being transmitted from the depths of an unknown space-time into the source sea.
However, he could not reach that special space-time; there was no trace to follow.
“Sure enough, without a special method, there’s no way to find the Primal Sea. Even after arriving here, I still have no way to enter.” Ye Tian murmured.
“The origin tide has begun!”
One Half-Step Eternal Realm expert after another spoke.
On the Source God Pavilion’s side, the Twelve Ancestors made their move.
They took out pieces of leaves, and each leaf was filled with special power.
“Get on!”
the Twelve Ancestors reminded them.
Whish whish whish!!!!
One Supreme Being after another came onto the leaves, and Ye Tian also stood on a leaf beneath Fenggu Source Ancestor’s feet.
Then, these leaves ignored the source sea’s void and followed the origin tide into the depths of this special space-time.
Space-time around them continuously twisted, and the leaves carried Ye Tian onward without pause.
At this moment, Fenggu Source Ancestor introduced, “These leaves are not ordinary leaves. They are a source sea wonder called Primal Leaves. They have no other function; their only use is to carry Supreme Beings into the Primal Sea. Their number is extremely limited, and they are only controlled by a few top large factions. Without Primal Leaves, even the strongest Half-Step Eternal Realm experts have no way to enter the Primal Sea.”
“Primal Leaves!”
Ye Tian finally understood what was going on.
Very quickly, they arrived at the Primal Sea.
The position where each Primal Leaf entered the Primal Sea was different; after all, Fenggu Source Ancestor and the others could not control the direction, and being able to enter the Primal Sea at all was already good enough.
Primal Sea.
Fenggu Source Ancestor and Ye Tian and the others arrived here, on a small island, while all around them was a golden ocean, entirely made of origin that had been condensed to the extreme.
Moreover, the suppression here was very strong; ordinary Supreme Beings simply could not withstand the suppressive force here.
“Let’s split up. Entering the Primal Sea requires Primal Leaves, but leaving does not. Follow the origin tide, and you can fly out.”
Fenggu Source Ancestor reminded them.
Ye Tian indicated that he understood. Above them was the origin tide, continuously letting origin flow out of space-time. Flying out along that path was enough to leave.
Supreme Beings or Half-Step Eternal Realm experts who entered here all needed to constantly pay attention to the state of the origin tide. Once there were signs that the origin tide was dispersing, they had to rush out immediately, otherwise they would easily become trapped.
Whish whish whish!!!!
One Supreme Being after another dispersed and headed off into the distance, and Fenggu Source Ancestor also left without taking any Supreme Beings with him.
He had already done well enough by bringing Ye Tian and the others into the Primal Sea; naturally, he would not continue to look after them.
Ye Tian casually chose a direction and began slowly searching for resources.
The Primal Sea had no living beings, but that did not mean it had no danger. On the contrary, it was very dangerous; if one lacked sufficient strength, one could easily fall.
One danger came from other Supreme Beings and even Half-Step Eternal Realm experts. If a Eighth-Tier Supreme Being found many treasures and a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert saw it, that expert might casually kill the Eighth-Tier Supreme Being; then there would be no need to search, and they could directly obtain a large amount of resources.
How wonderful that would be!
· ·········求鮮花··· ·····
Another danger was that in some places of the Primal Sea, black fog remained. Once one touched those places, black fog erosion would be triggered.
This black fog would not spread during the origin tide, but once someone actively touched it, even a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert would be seriously injured, and an Eighth-Tier Supreme Being would have almost no chance of surviving.
Precisely because of this, the Primal Sea’s danger was so terrifying that many Supreme Beings were too scared to come in at all.
It had to be said that the Primal Sea had far too many resources.
Very quickly, Ye Tian found quite a few good things.
“An Eternal Source Item!”
Ye Tian saw a stone lying on a mountain of an island, and the aura it emitted was precisely that of an Eternal Source Item.
It looked just like an ordinary stone; if not for its extremely obvious aura, Ye Tian would not have believed it.
.... ...... 0
Whish!
Ye Tian collected the stone, feeling very good.
After all, being able to pick up an Eternal Source Item casually really meant his luck was quite good.
However, after that, Ye Tian did not find a second Eternal Source Item, but he did find quite a few Eternal resources as well as resources that could improve Supreme Being cultivation.
At this rate of harvest, even if Ye Tian did not find any astonishing treasures, this trip would not have been in vain.
“No wonder everyone wants to become inner-circle members of the Source God Pavilion. Just this opportunity alone is enough to drive some daring Supreme Beings crazy!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Time slowly passed, and Ye Tian’s harvest grew greater and greater.
And on this day, he finally encountered another Supreme Being, not from the Source God Pavilion, but from another force.
This Supreme Being was at the Eighth Stage. After seeing Ye Tian, his eyes revealed excited light.
He directly attacked Ye Tian, clearly wanting to kill Ye Tian and seize the treasures on Ye Tian’s body.
For such a Supreme Being, Ye Tian was not polite either.
“Destroying Death Finger!”
Ye Tian executed this Eternal technique, directly mobilizing that severed finger of an Eternal Realm expert. Although he did not unleash his strongest attack with full force, he still produced offensive power comparable to the strongest Ninth-Tier Supreme Being.
Boom!!!!
A single finger strike, enough to annihilate everything, instantly shattered the opponent’s layers of defense, pressed onto the opponent’s body, and directly crushed the opponent’s body into pieces and .


Chapter 1619: This Is Not Black Mist, It Is Black Mist Insects!

Chapter 1619: This Is Not Black Mist, It Is Black Mist Insects!

Although the body of that Eighth-Tier Supreme Being was crushed by Ye Tian with a single finger, he was not killed instantly.
After all, this Eighth-Tier Supreme Being was very powerful. Even a top Ninth-Tier Supreme Being could not kill a Peak Eighth-Tier Supreme Being with one strike, but this Eighth-Tier Supreme Being was still severely injured.
“Shattering Void Sword!”
Ye Tian immediately unleashed another Eternal technique. Although he did not activate the power of the Eternal Stage finger, his ordinary combat strength had also reached the level of a top Eighth-Tier Supreme Being.
Coupled with the fact that this Eighth-Tier Supreme Being had not much combat strength left, he was simply no match for Ye Tian.
Very soon, this Eighth-Tier Supreme Being was killed by Ye Tian.
“This guy found quite a lot of good things!”
After Ye Tian inspected the other party’s void sphere, he could not help but say excitedly.
Killing an Eighth-Tier Supreme Being was far more satisfying than slowly searching for resources.
Of course, he would not deliberately go around looking for other Supreme Beings to kill. As long as they did not provoke him, he would not make a move either. If he developed the habit of hunting others, one day he would also be hunted by other half-step Eternal Stage experts, and by then all his gains would end up belonging to someone else.
Just like this Eighth-Tier Supreme Being—he had thought he could hunt others, but in the end he died at Ye Tian’s hands.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian became even more cautious.
After all, this time he had only encountered an Eighth-Tier Supreme Being. If he encountered a half-step Eternal Stage expert, he would not be that person’s opponent.
Thus, Ye Tian kept his copying talent activated at all times.
In a place like the Primordial Sea, the copying talent was more useful than perception. Once he detected a half-step Eternal Stage expert approaching, he would flee at the first possible moment.
Only this way could he ensure his own safety.
During the following period, whenever Ye Tian detected a half-step Eternal Stage expert, he would leave at the fastest speed possible to avoid meeting them, and thus encountered no danger.
Some Supreme Beings, after obtaining certain benefits, resisted the temptation and immediately chose to leave the Primordial Sea, fearing that if they fell here, they would be left with nothing.
However, most Supreme Beings could not control this temptation. They all wanted to obtain more treasures and were unwilling to leave even if it was very dangerous.
As time passed, one Supreme Being after another fell in the Primordial Sea. Most of the fallen Supreme Beings died at the hands of other powerful experts, and only a small number accidentally touched the black mist, thereby perishing within it.
And on this day, Ye Tian finally had the bad luck to encounter the black mist as well.
……
“This is Yuanqing Eternal Stone. It’s actually such a huge piece!”
Ye Tian passed by a small island and saw Yuanqing Eternal Stone, and was immediately startled.
Yuanqing Eternal Stone was an extremely valuable resource. It could be refined into Yuanqing Eternal Liquid, which could help Eternal Bodies grow, and was one of the top auxiliary cultivation resources for Eternal Bodies.
Ye Tian flew down, preparing to take the Yuanqing Eternal Stone away.
But he discovered that the Yuanqing Eternal Stone was connected to the island and had to be severed before it could be removed.
So he struck at the base of the Yuanqing Eternal Stone, directly separating it from the ground.
Boom!!!!!!
The Yuanqing Eternal Stone was severed and detached from the island.
But the next second, he was stunned.
From the place where the Yuanqing Eternal Stone connected to the ground, there was actually a small space, and at this moment countless black mist were surging out from within that small space.
The speed of this black mist was too fast, even slightly faster than Ye Tian.
“Retreat!”
Ye Tian wanted to escape, but one of his arms was corroded by the black mist.
Just as his body was about to be corroded by the black mist, the Eternal Stage finger fused into his finger suddenly sensed danger, because the black mist also wanted to corrode the finger of the Eternal Stage mighty figure. It had touched the seal on the finger, directly triggering the power of the Eternal Stage.
Boom!!!!!!
The black mist was blasted apart, and although Ye Tian was also injured by the backlash from the Eternal Stage finger’s power, he at least saved his life and promptly withdrew from this area.
The black mist could not spread infinitely; it could only spread across this island, so Ye Tian no longer needed to worry.
He stood outside the island, looking at that mass of black mist, feeling extremely shocked in his heart.
“Good thing it was me. If it had been any other Supreme Being, they’d probably be dead for sure. This corrosion speed is too fast!”
Ye Tian muttered.
Suddenly.
His expression changed as his gaze toward the black mist became suspicious.
“This…”
Ye Tian discovered that this was not true black mist at all, but black mist formed from countless Black Mist Insects.
The so-called corrosion was simply the body being invaded by Black Mist Insects and devoured by them.
Each Black Mist Insect was very tiny and could even shield perception and divine sense probing. When a Supreme Being’s divine sense entered this black mist, it would be devoured, and thus even a half-step Eternal Stage expert might not necessarily know what the black mist was, only feeling that it was incomparably terrifying........
But Ye Tian’s copying talent had detected the talents of these black mist. Endless talents covered his data panel, all of them were the talents of Black Mist Insects.
Type: Black Mist Insect
Strength: Eternal Ancestor Talent
Speed: Eternal Ancestor Talent
Defense: Eternal Ancestor Talent!
Devouring: Eternal Ancestor Talent
Undying: Eternal Ancestor Talent!
……
The talents of these Black Mist Insects were all very luxurious, but the key was that their numbers were too terrifying.
Suddenly, Ye Tian burst out laughing.
“So many Eternal Ancestor Talents. If I copy them one by one, even if it takes a long time, once countless Eternal Ancestor Talents are fused together, could they surpass Eternal Ancestor Talent?”
Thinking of this, Ye Tian became excited.
Looking for resources?
No, he no longer cared about that.
For him, the talents of these Black Mist Insects were the greatest opportunity.
Copy!
Copy!
Copy!
Copy!
……
In order to speed up the copying, each time he copied an Eternal Ancestor Talent, he used time acceleration to pass through the time required for copying.
Just like that, Ye Tian did not spend too long before copying all the talents contained in these Black Mist Insects.
However.
Fusing them would take far too long.
Therefore, Ye Tian did not fuse these talents; he would wait until after leaving to fuse them slowly.
He now had an idea: if he self-annihilated the clone outside, then he could once again expend a body to serve as a clone.
Thus, he prepared to copy the body of a Black Mist Insect.
In this way, even after the source tide passed, he could let the Black Mist Insect clone remain in the Primordial Sea.
Outside.
Ye Tian’s clone self-annihilated.
After that, the copied body located in the Primordial Sea could use the copying ability to begin copying a Black Mist Insect.
Whoosh!
Copy successful.
A Black Mist Insect appeared in Ye Tian’s hand, its body so tiny that it was tens of thousands of times smaller than an ant.
Immediately after, Ye Tian’s Black Mist Insect clone flew toward the island and mixed in with the other Black Mist Insects.


Chapter 1620: The Immortal Ancestor Talent!

Chapter 1620: The Immortal Ancestor Talent!

“It’s done!”
Ye Tian was extremely excited.
The black mist worm clone had been staying in the Primordial Sea all this time. Who could enjoy such treatment?
Suddenly.
Ye Tian thought of a problem: if the black mist worm clone was too weak, then it would be of no use even in the Primordial Sea.
Moreover, once the origin tide of the Primordial Sea ended, he would be unable to enter this place, and the black mist worm would also be unable to leave. In reality, it would not gain too many benefits either.
The only gain was that he had copied a large number of Eternal Ancestor Talents.
Now, he faced two choices.
The first was to continue staying here and not wait until after leaving to fuse the Eternal Ancestor Talents, but instead begin fusing them directly here.
The second choice was to wait until after leaving before fusing these Eternal Ancestor Talents, and use the time to search for resource treasures himself.
After thinking for a while, Ye Tian decided to choose the first.
He planned to fuse them right here, use the fastest speed to fuse out the talents above the Eternal Ancestor Talents, and then bestow them upon the black mist worm clone, letting the black mist worm clone rise completely and become the king of the black mist worms.
In that case, the black mist worm clone would be able to hold a hegemonic position in the Primordial Sea and naturally collect more good things. At worst, the next time he came in, he would be able to gain countless resources.
Moreover, he was also very curious: what exactly was the talent above the Eternal Ancestor Talents?
“Begin fusing!”
Ye Tian set up a time acceleration great array around him and first began by devouring the Eternal Ancestor Talents.
One by one, the devouring Eternal Ancestor Talents fused together, but the fusion speed was rather slow, and even somewhat laborious. After all, the level of the copied talent was not much higher than the Eternal Ancestor Talents, so fusing the Eternal Ancestor Talents was naturally very strenuous.
But in the end, the devouring Eternal Ancestor Talents still fused together one by one.
During this time.
Some Supreme Beings passed by here, but Ye Tian concealed his figure. As soon as these Supreme Beings sensed the black mist on the island, they were so frightened that they fled immediately, not daring to investigate carefully at all.
Thus, Ye Tian had not been discovered to this day.
Time slowly passed—
Ye Tian did not know how much time had passed, but he had stayed within the time acceleration great array for a very long period, and he had also fused many Eternal Ancestor Talents.
Gradually, after the devouring Eternal Ancestor Talent fused, its power became stronger and stronger, as if a qualitative change could occur at any moment.
Finally, on this day, the devouring Eternal Ancestor Talent transformed completely.
【Devouring: Immortal Ancestor Talent】
This was a talent level above the Eternal Ancestor Talents, and it was also the first Immortal Ancestor Talent Ye Tian possessed.
The Immortal Ancestor Talent was almost completely on the same level as the copy talent, and Ye Tian also clearly sensed that the Immortal Ancestor Talent could no longer continue to upgrade. At the very least, the current copy talent was unable to fuse the Immortal Ancestor Talent any further.
Immediately.
Ye Tian stripped the Immortal Ancestor Talent and bestowed it upon the black mist worm clone, and thus the black mist worm clone also possessed the Immortal Ancestor Talent.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian fused the other Eternal Ancestor Talents one by one.
In this way, the Immortal Ancestor Talents of strength, defense, speed, and indestructibility were born one after another, and all of them were bestowed by Ye Tian upon the black mist worm clone.
Gathering these Immortal Ancestor Talents, the black mist worm clone finally underwent a qualitative change.
Rumble!!!!!
The black mist worm clone welcomed its transformation. Not only did its body size begin to surge, but its strength also skyrocketed rapidly, as if it had broken through some kind of boundary.
After all, in the Primordial Sea, the black mist worm was subject to some kind of restriction. If it were outside, there could not possibly be such a tiny creature capable of threatening a Ninth-Tier Supreme Being, but it existed in the Primordial Sea, so it was definitely the Primordial Sea’s rules that had restricted the black mist worm.
And now, Ye Tian was effectively breaking this restriction.
In no time at all, the black mist worm’s body size became comparable to that of a black-armored worm, making it stand out too much among the countless black mist worms.
Moreover, Ye Tian clearly felt that the black mist worm clone could command the other black mist worms, like a king.
In terms of cultivation realm, the black mist worm clone was roughly equivalent to a Sixth-Tier Supreme Being, but it could lead countless black mist worms, and its threat level was comparable to that of a powerful half-step Eternal realm expert.
Moreover, the black mist worm clone could leave the island and was no longer restricted.
Not long after.
Ye Tian discovered that the origin tide was about to end.
“It’s time to leave, otherwise this copied body won’t be able to return, and those talents won’t be taken away either.”
Ye Tian murmured.
Whoosh!
He flew into the void and left the Primordial Sea along with the origin tide.
Not long after.
Ye Tian returned to the Source Sea, and when he carefully tried to sense the location of the Primordial Sea again, he could sense it, but could not enter it.
This time, Ye Tian’s gains were not very great. He definitely could not compare with those half-step Eternal realm experts, but he had obtained some Immortal Ancestor Talents, and that was his biggest gain.
Ye Tian took a look, and the Twelve Ancestors and the other Supreme Beings of Source God Pavilion had also come out.
Very soon, the Supreme Beings of Source God Pavilion returned to Source God Pavilion.
Internal meeting of Source God Pavilion.
One Supreme Being after another sat in their seats, and Ye Tian was also here.
But soon, he discovered that quite a few Supreme Beings had not returned.
Time slowly passed until the origin tide completely disappeared.
At the same time, Ye Tian’s black mist worm clone discovered that the restrictions of the Primordial Sea had completely disappeared, and countless black mist worms flew out, spreading across the entire Primordial Sea.

“The remaining Supreme Beings didn’t come back. Even if they’re still alive, they must have been swallowed by the black mist by now.”

True River Sword Ancestor announced.
Thirty-seven inner-circle members, and among those fallen Supreme Beings, at the very least all of them were at the Eighth-Tier Heavenly realm.
Eighth-Tier Supreme Beings—what a powerful realm, yet so many had fallen all at once.

Fenggu Source Ancestor spoke.
The other Supreme Beings immediately took out the resources they did not need, hoping to exchange them with other Supreme Beings for resources.
Ye Tian also took out some resources, mainly to exchange for resources that could help the Eternal Body grow and develop.
He wanted to raise his Endless Eternal Body to the Perfected realm, and thus needed a large amount of related resources.
Many of the Supreme Beings here had their Eternal Tribulation bodies, Eternal divine bodies, or Eternal bodies reach the Perfected realm, so even if they obtained treasures like the Yuanqing Eternal Stone, they did not need them much, and were therefore willing to exchange them for other resources.
Very quickly, Ye Tian traded for quite a few resources similar to the Yuanqing Eternal Stone.
Not long after, the trading ended, and one Supreme Being after another left this place to go back into seclusion.
Ye Tian also hurriedly returned to the Void Source Hall and disappeared from Source God Pavilion.


Chapter 1621: Huge Harvest!

Chapter 1621: Huge Harvest!

Void Source Hall.
After Ye Tian returned, he immediately began to fuse those Eternal Ancestor Talents.
As time slowly passed, one Eternal Ancestor Talent after another was fused.

When Ye Tian’s true body obtained these Undying Ancestor Talents, its potential became even greater.
And if he were to create Eternal Skills in the future, it would become even easier.
In particular, the Immortal Undying Ancestor Talent—this Undying Ancestor Talent was somewhat related to the Endless Eternal Body, because the Endless Eternal Body had fused the Ancient Star Eternal Body, and the Ancient Star Eternal Body actually possessed the power of immortality, which was why it could have such powerful life-preserving ability.
And now, Ye Tian had obtained the Immortal Undying Ancestor Talent, which would help him cultivate the Endless Eternal Body.
The fusion of talents had already been completed, and Ye Tian began cultivating the Endless Eternal Body.

Ye Tian swallowed a mouthful of Yuanqing Eternal Liquid, and the Endless Eternal Body began absorbing the energy of the Yuanqing Eternal Liquid.
At this moment, the Immortal Undying Ancestor Talent played a certain role, greatly increasing Ye Tian’s utilization rate of the Yuanqing Eternal Liquid, which surprised Ye Tian a little.

Gradually, the Endless Eternal Body advanced to the peak of the late Major realm.
By this point, Ye Tian had already consumed a great deal of substances, and he was only one step away from the Perfected realm of the Endless Eternal Body, but this one step was very difficult to complete and required an enormous amount of resources. Fortunately, Ye Tian was lucky; before those substances were completely exhausted, his Endless Eternal Body finally reached Perfected.
Once the Endless Eternal Body reached Perfected, Ye Tian’s strength surged dramatically.

Primordial Sea.
At this point, the place was already covered with Black Mist Worms, and no matter where Ye Tian went, he could command the other Black Mist Worms; he was the king among the Black Mist Worms.
All kinds of precious resources were collected by Ye Tian and stored in a void he had opened up within his body.
On this day.
Ye Tian discovered an incomparably precious treasure—Void True Liquid.
Void True Liquid appeared in a void-like liquid state, with obscure fluctuations of Eternal Rule, but its main characteristic was that when it came into contact with Eternal Rule, it would turn into a truly void state.
In other words, attacks from Eternal Rule could not touch it. Once external Eternal Rule touched it, it would completely vanish, as if it did not exist in heaven and earth, or within Eternal Rule; even a half-step Eternal realm expert could not detect its existence.
And once the Eternal Rule attack moved away from where it was, it would appear again.
Thus, identifying Void True Liquid was still quite easy.
“To think I actually found Void True Liquid. If those Ninth Supreme Being experts knew about it, they would probably go mad!”
Ye Tian muttered.

Void True Liquid could help any Ninth Supreme Being expert冲击 the half-step Eternal realm, and for some Ninth Supreme Being experts who had used treasures similar to Primordial Source Liquid, it was their last hope.
Ye Tian did not need Void True Liquid all that much, but the human race certainly had people who did—for example, his relatives needed it.
He did not think his relatives could cultivate to the half-step Eternal realm on their own; in the end, they would probably still have to rely on Void True Liquid.
Therefore, even one portion of Void True Liquid was still not enough for him.
After obtaining Void True Liquid, Ye Tian’s luck afterwards seemed to become better and better.

Primordial Leaves are treasures produced by the Primordial Tree; one Primordial Leaf can carry an Supreme Being into the Primordial Sea, but the Primordial Tree had ten leaves, and the Primordial Tree itself likely had special uses as well.
Unfortunately, Ye Tian did not know the uses of the Primordial Tree.

As for the Primordial Tree, he did not take it away, but left it here. It would not be too late to come back after figuring out the Primordial Tree’s use.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian obtained many, many resources, including quite a few that were useful even to half-step Eternal realm experts.
In the entire Primordial Sea, there was no Supreme Being competing with Ye Tian; this place was his home ground.

Then, he would not have to worry at all about the resources needed to cultivate to the half-step Eternal realm, and he could even help the human race nurture multiple half-step Eternal realm experts.
Long years passed.
Ye Tian had almost visited most of the Primordial Sea, and in fact many resources had already been collected by the Supreme Beings who had entered before him. After all, there had been many Supreme Beings entering this place, and they collected things very quickly.

Among them were two drops of Void True Liquid, one Primordial Tree, one Eternal Undying Sacred Flower, three Eternal Comprehension Flowers, and 109 Immortal Primordial Stones.

The Eternal Comprehension Flower could make even half-step Eternal realm experts enter a state of sudden enlightenment, and its value was great.
The Eternal Undying Sacred Flower could heal all injuries; even fatal injuries to a half-step Eternal realm expert could be healed by the Eternal Undying Flower.
Immortal Primordial Stone was an incomparably hard material that could be used to forge Eternal Source Weapons, and after half-step Eternal realm, few people possessed Eternal Source Weapons.
And with so many Immortal Primordial Stones, it was enough to forge many Eternal Source Weapons.
As for the other resources, they were simply innumerable.
More importantly, these were treasures missed by Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal realm experts.
As long years passed, the Primordial Sea would continue to give birth to more treasures, and then Ye Tian could harvest another wave of resources.
Suddenly.
On this day, some changes occurred in the Primordial Sea. Many, many Black Mist Worms were drawn by some kind of attraction and flew toward a certain location in the Primordial Sea together.
Ye Tian could resist this pull, but he still followed over.
He very much wanted to know what exactly this so-called pull came from?.


Chapter 1622 A Black Mist River Formed from a Section of Arm!

Chapter 1622 A Black Mist River Formed from a Section of Arm!

Very soon, Ye Tian followed the other black mist worms to a certain place in the Primordial Sea.
In this place, endless black mist worms gathered here, and the density was very high.
Moreover, more black mist worms were arriving.
“This is……”
Ye Tian saw a pitch-black river, almost separated from the Primordial Sea and located in another void.
Above this river, densely packed life forms were hatching, as if the entire river were a place of incubation.
“The hatching place of the black mist worms!”
Ye Tian had always been curious about where the black mist worms were born, because black mist worms had no need to mate, had no distinction between sexes, and had very low intelligence.
Under such circumstances, why were there so many black mist worms, and why was each black mist worm so powerful.
This was not normal!
Yet after spending a long time in the Primordial Sea, he still had not found the place where black mist worms were born.
Now, he could be considered to have found it.
No, it should be said that this place of birth had appeared on its own.
One after another, black mist worms hatched out and began devouring the shells that had hatched them—if those could be called shells, then they were shells. Almost every shell could hatch countless black mist worms.
At this time, the black mist worms from outside also flew in and devoured these shells.
Even Ye Tian himself felt a primal urge to devour them, as if these shells had great attraction and would be of enormous use in increasing his strength.
“Get lost!”
Ye Tian used the aura of the king of black mist worms to force the other black mist worms to scatter; those shells had to be devoured by him alone.
Crash, crash, crash!!!!
One shell after another was devoured and refined by Ye Tian, and the other black mist worms did not dare resist at all.
As these shells were absorbed and refined by him, Ye Tian’s aura grew stronger and stronger.
For black mist worms, these shells were the true treasure resources, while the other resources of the Primordial Sea held no appeal to black mist worms.
Boom!!!!
Ye Tian’s cultivation actually broke through.
This black mist worm clone had actually advanced to the Seventh Stage.
Thus, Ye Tian continued to devour, as if this body had no bottleneck at all.
Other black mist worms could not do this, however; their potential was insufficient and they were restricted. Even if devouring the shells could increase their strength, the increase was not significant.
Perhaps, by instinct they also wanted to break through the shackles and limitations, but without an immortal-level ancestral aptitude, they simply could not do it.
Very soon, the cultivation of the black mist worm clone improved again.
Early Seventh Stage!
Mid Seventh Stage!
Late Seventh Stage!
Peak Seventh Stage!
Logically speaking, it should be very difficult to break through from Seventh Stage to Eighth Stage. Even for Ye Tian’s true body, if he wanted to charge from a Seventh Stage Supreme Being to an Eighth Stage Supreme Being, it would probably be rather difficult.
However, the black mist worm clone easily broke through the shackles and advanced to Eighth Stage, comparable to an Eighth Stage Supreme Being.
But black mist worms were not Supreme Beings after all, and they had no Eternal Body; those Eternal Techniques were also not suitable for them.
Therefore, the black mist worm clone was not very strong in combat.
Of course, black mist worms mainly won by numbers; individual strength did not matter much.
After a long while, the cultivation of the black mist worm clone finally could no longer improve, but it had already reached the Peak of the Ninth Stage.
Unfortunately, such a breakthrough brought no benefit to the true body, and the true body could not draw any reference from it.
After breaking through to the Nine Heavens Stage, Ye Tian’s black mist worm clone also became about the size of a puppy.
After the breakthrough in strength, Ye Tian clearly felt that something was wrong with this river.
The sensory range of an ordinary black mist worm was not very large, but Ye Tian’s perception now covered this entire river.
Under his perception, this was a river resembling an arm, and it was an amputated arm, as if it had crossed over from the depths of endless spacetime, only to be severed here by someone.
At this moment, he had already imagined a scene from long, long ago.
In an age of boundless antiquity, an incomparably terrifying existence had been cut off from one arm by another strong expert, and this section of the arm had remained in this spacetime of the Primordial Sea. Later, through special evolution, black mist worms hatched from this arm.
But this arm was an eternal existence. Even after nurturing endless black mist worms, it still had not completely disappeared; instead, it had taken on the form of a river and continued to exist.
The so-called river form was merely a decayed state.
“Is it really like this?”
Ye Tian guessed inwardly.
But if it was true, then how terrifying must that expert’s strength have been?
Even after the Eternal Realm, that would still be an incomparably terrifying level, right?
Ye Tian thought for a while, then made a decision: he would go deeper into this river.
This river might conceal itself at any moment; by then, it would not be easy to find.
However, once he entered the depths of the river, problems could easily arise.
Therefore, Ye Tian found a nearby island and first stored away the treasures he had collected.
In this way, even if this black mist worm clone perished, the next time he entered the Primordial Sea, he could still take away those resources and would not lose them.
After dealing with the resource treasures, Ye Tian returned once more to this river, which he temporarily called the Black Mist River.
Entering the Black Mist River, Ye Tian plunged in and kept moving deeper and deeper into it.
Boom!!!!
Endless pressure came crashing down, as if trying to stop him from entering the depths of the Black Mist River.
If it were other black mist worms, they would not be able to go deep at all.
But Ye Tian’s black mist worm clone had already reached the Ninth Stage Supreme Being level, and thus could force its way in.
As time passed, Ye Tian went deeper and deeper.
No one knew how much time had passed before Ye Tian finally discovered something different.
A rod-like weapon emitting brilliant golden light appeared within his perception, and in the distance there were even more, larger objects like this, with varying shapes.
Ye Tian came before this brilliant golden rod and examined it carefully.
“This is bone!”
Ye Tian said with certainty.
Strictly speaking, this was a fragment of bone, and a tiny, insignificant fragment at that.
At this point, Ye Tian could confirm that his guess was correct.
The Black Mist River was indeed a section of an arm. Not only had it been severed, but the bones of the arm had been smashed into countless fragments, almost completely shattered into innumerable bone pieces.
And the one before him was one of those bone fragments.
Ye Tian tried attacking it, using the body of his Peak Ninth Stage black mist worm to ram into it.
Under a full-force strike, this bone fragment actually cracked a little.
“It’s probably because it has existed for too long, and black mist worms have hatched here, continuously absorbing the power of the arm. Even the bones of such an existence can be cracked by me!”
Ye Tian sighed.
Of course.
Even so, a fragment of bone like this was priceless.


Chapter 1623: The Captured Black Mist Worms!

Chapter 1623: The Captured Black Mist Worms!

Primordial Sea.

Chapter 1624 The Primordial Tree Heart That Can Be Refined Into a Clone!

Chapter 1624 The Primordial Tree Heart That Can Be Refined Into a Clone!

True River Sword Ancestor said.>

As for how the Primordial Leaf was brought out of the Primordial Sea in the first place, let’s temporarily assume it was brought out by the Eternal Realm and not dwell on that for now. However, some Primordial Trees have also been discovered, and after many fights and snatchings, our Source God Pavilion once obtained a Primordial Tree. In other words, if one obtains a Primordial Tree heart, it can be refined into a half-step Eternal Realm clone. Moreover, if the Primordial Tree heart exists within the body, then even if the clone perishes, it can be condensed again at the cost of some price. For Supreme Beings or half-step Eternal Realm experts without the ability to create clones, the Primordial Tree heart is extremely valuable. “So I still drew their attention!”
Ye Tian muttered.>
There was nothing to be done about it; asking that question was already strange, so drawing their attention was perfectly normal.>
After all, Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm experts were not fools; with just a little thought, they could guess some things.>
However, he was not afraid, otherwise he would not have asked.>
With his current strength, even a powerful half-step Eternal Realm expert would not make him afraid of anything.>
The Dark Forbidden Domain was still under protection now, and by the time the protection period ended, his cultivation would surely have risen to the realm of an Eighth Supreme Being or even a Ninth Supreme Being.>
By then, he would not fear those top-tier half-step Eternal Realm experts at all.>
Anyone who made him an enemy would face disaster, not him.>
At the same time.>
In some corner of the Source Sea, several Supreme Beings were discussing how to deal with Ye Tian, and they were drawing up a plan.>
--------------------
In a dark hall, six Ninth Supreme Beings were entirely shrouded in darkness.>
“According to my intelligence, the Seventh Supreme Being Nirvana Origin Ancestor should have obtained the Primordial Tree in the Primordial Sea. The Primordial Tree not only has the Primordial Leaf, but its heart can also help us condense clones.”
“Even if it can only allow one of us to condense a clone, that would be enough. The excess Primordial Leaves can be sold, enough to exchange for resources that will let us break through to the half-step Eternal Realm. And once we have condensed clones, I’m not afraid to send that person to brave the Primordial Sea, not even fearing death. By then, we will rise!”
“Remember, the Nirvana Origin Ancestor has the ability to create clones, so it is very difficult to completely kill him, but his Dark Forbidden Domain is right there and cannot run away.”
“The Nirvana Origin Ancestor is very young and must have feelings for his clan, and his family is still in the Dark Forbidden Domain. We’ll surround the Dark Forbidden Domain and threaten him. Otherwise, once the protection period of the Dark Forbidden Domain passes, we’ll completely destroy the Dark Forbidden Domain, and the Nirvana Origin Ancestor may directly hand over the Primordial Tree.”
“Then let’s do it that way. I can’t go; the Nirvana Origin Ancestor will recognize me, so I’ll leave it to you!”
After these six Ninth Supreme Beings discussed it, they immediately prepared to act.>
Otherwise, if they moved too slowly and were preempted by other experts, it might no longer be their turn.


Chapter 1625 You, I'm afraid, cannot leave!

Chapter 1625 You all, I'm afraid, cannot leave!

Outside the Dark Forbidden Domain.
One after another ninefold Supreme Beings appeared here. Suddenly, a human Third-Tier Invincible stepped out of the Dark Forbidden Domain and was immediately seized by one of the ninefold Supreme Beings.
“Seniors, what are you going to do?”
The human Third-Tier Invincible was very panicked. The auras of these people far surpassed his imagination; even a wisp of their aura suppressed him to the point that he could not move. They were certainly Supreme Beings above Invincible, and not ordinary Supreme Beings at that.
He had also met several Supreme Beings of the human race before. Aside from the mysterious Endless Ancestor, the auras of the others were far below these few.
These few were probably top-notch existences among Supreme Beings. Why would such powerful figures seize him?
He was very puzzled, unable to understand how exactly he had offended them, or whether the human race had offended them?
“Send word to your human race and have the Endless Ancestor come here.”
One of the ninefold Supreme Beings ordered.
The human Third-Tier Invincible immediately realized they were enemies of the Endless Ancestor, and he did not dare disobey their order. He hurriedly sent a message to the upper echelons of the human race, and then had the upper echelons send word to the Supreme Beings.
As for him, he had no way to contact a Supreme Being directly.
Very quickly, the human race’s Supreme Beings all learned of the situation, but they did not leave the Dark Forbidden Domain directly. After all, the other side had come specifically for Ye Tian, so they were certainly incomparably powerful Supreme Beings.
And they were too weak; they did not yet have the qualifications to contend against such powerful Supreme Beings. If they went out, they would merely be giving the enemy one more captive.
“No one of the human race is permitted to leave the Dark Forbidden Domain. A great enemy, a Supreme Being, has arrived outside!”
The human race’s Supreme Beings all sent out messages, and even shut down one Tier-three gate after another. At the same time, they contacted Ye Tian, who had returned not long ago and was in cultivation.
“Father, several Supreme Beings have appeared outside the Dark Forbidden Domain.”
Ye Xingchen came to pay his respects to Ye Tian.
“Xingchen, I know. Go down. You all cannot get involved in this matter.” Ye Tian murmured.
In fact, he had already learned of it immediately, and had even guessed the reason.
These Supreme Beings were probably here for the Primordial Tree. The Primordial Tree’s value was too high; even a single Primordial Leaf was enough to drive many Supreme Beings mad!
These Supreme Beings coming to snatch his Primordial Tree was very normal. Even without proof, it was still worth the risk.
Ye Tian could have ignored them, but if he did not go, they might become even more aggressive. Moreover, once the Dark Forbidden Domain was no longer sheltered by the Source Sea, the Supreme Beings outside would come in. If a great battle broke out then, it would instead sweep into the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Therefore, he planned to deal with this matter directly and let the outside forces know that Ye Tian was not someone to be trifled with either.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian took one step and crossed out of the Dark Forbidden Domain, arriving at the Source Sea outside, where he also saw five ninefold Supreme Beings.
These ninefold Supreme Beings were all at the peak of the ninefold Supreme Being realm, only one step away from the Half-Step Eternal realm. But without some heaven-defying opportunity, they would find it hard to break through to the Half-Step Eternal realm in their entire lives.
It was precisely because of this that they longed so much for the opportunity represented by the Primordial Tree.
“Five ninefold Supreme Beings!”
Ye Tian let out a breath of relief.
If it had been five Half-Step Eternal experts, he really would not have been able to establish his authority.
However, Half-Step Eternal experts were inherently rare. Only top loose organizations like the Source God Pavilion could have so many Half-Step Eternal experts.
In truth, many of the Source God Pavilion’s experts belonged to other factions, and in a sense, overlapped with some other forces.
But Ye Tian was certain that these five ninefold Supreme Beings were definitely from the same force as the inner-circle members of the Source God Pavilion; otherwise, they would not have been able to receive the news so quickly.
“What do you mean by this? Why have you seized one of my human race’s Invincible ones?”
Ye Tian asked.
One of the ninefold Supreme Beings said in a deep voice, “Endless Ancestor, we hear that you possess a Primordial Tree. Hand it over.”
“Primordial Tree?” Ye Tian sneered. “Who told you that I have a Primordial Tree?”
“Who said it is not important. The point is, if you do not hand it over, not only will this human Invincible perish, but after your Dark Forbidden Domain passes its protection period, we will destroy this Eternal Heaven and Earth.” The other side threatened.
“Are you threatening me?”
Ye Tian said coldly.
He was very clear that even if he denied it, the other side would not believe him; even if he swore an oath, they would not believe him either.
After all, he possessed the ability to manifest clones, and this information was already no secret. By then, even if he made an oath, it would only affect this body; the main body would not be affected.
Therefore, they would not believe his oath.
All five of them wore robes and masks that concealed their auras, but their identities could not hide from Ye Tian at all.
Through the probing of the Copying Talent and his knowledge of their names, Ye Tian quickly locked onto their identities.
“The five from Golden Orchid Mountain, are you really going to make enemies of me?”
Ye Tian asked.
“Our identities were exposed?”
The five ninefold Supreme Beings were very surprised.
They had not made a move yet; if they had, then it would have been impossible to completely conceal their aura and Half-Step Eternal techniques, so being guessed would have been normal.
But now, Ye Tian had recognized them with just one glance, which shocked them somewhat.
“You lot, aren’t you afraid I’ll take revenge on Golden Orchid Mountain, on your Eternal Heaven and Earth?” Ye Tian said.
“Not afraid!”
One of them smiled and said, “If we obtain your Primordial Tree, at worst we’ll abandon Golden Orchid Mountain. As for the Eternal Heaven and Earth behind us, destroy it if you want. Anyway, we’ll take our close people with us; what do the life and death of everyone else have to do with us? But you should care a great deal about the human race and the Dark Forbidden Domain, right?”
Ye Tian was silent for several dozen seconds before saying, “How about this: I will fight you all. If you win, I will hand over the Primordial Tree. If you lose, you are not to make any further plans for the Primordial Tree. How about it?”
“No problem!”
The five ninefold Supreme Beings immediately agreed.
However, they still did not release that human Third-Tier Invincible, instead sealing him up and tossing him into one of their void orbs.
After that, the battle began.
Boom!!!!!
Aside from not using the finger of the Eternal realm, Ye Tian displayed battle power between the ninefold Supreme Being realm and the Half-Step Eternal realm.
In truth, his regular battle power was already sufficient to fight a weaker Half-Step Eternal expert for a round or two, equivalent to the weakest Half-Step Eternal expert.
And these five ninefold Supreme Beings did not have Half-Step Eternal battle power, so naturally they were inferior to Ye Tian in his normal state.
If Ye Tian did not hide his strength, he was afraid he would scare them.
At the same time, he had another plan.
The moment they exchanged blows, the five Supreme Beings’ expressions changed drastically, and they were completely suppressed by Ye Tian.
Several hours later, the five Supreme Beings had already begun to suffer minor injuries.
“Retreat first. Once we gather more strength, we can come threaten the Endless Ancestor again!” one ninefold Supreme Being proposed.
“Agreed!”
“Agreed!”
The other ninefold Supreme Beings agreed.
Thus, they said in unison, “We admit defeat!”
“Release that Third-Tier Invincible. He is of no value to you. You wouldn’t go so far as to become mortal enemies with me over one human Invincible, would you?”
Ye Tian said.
“Release him!”
They freed that Invincible.
And after Ye Tian grabbed that human Invincible with one hand, he threw him into the Dark Forbidden Domain.
After that, Ye Tian intercepted the five ninefold Supreme Beings.
“You lot, I’m afraid, cannot leave!”
Ye Tian sneered.


Chapter 1626 All Killed!

Chapter 1626 All Killed!

Ye Tian blocked these five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings, which instead made them stunned.
“Endless Ancestor, you won’t let us leave? Ridiculous, could it be that you still have the confidence to keep us here?”
The five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings were very puzzled. Although Ye Tian’s strength was somewhat stronger than theirs, it was not that much stronger.
If they wanted to leave, Ye Tian simply could not stop them.
What right did Ye Tian have to stop and threaten them?
“Endless Ancestor, move aside immediately!”
The five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings said coldly.
“You actually dare to threaten the Dark Forbidden Domain and me, then perish here. I hope you have the ability to create incarnations, otherwise today you will really die!”
After speaking, Ye Tian made his move.
This time, he did not hold back, but displayed all of his combat power in full.
Boom!!!!!!
The perfected Endless Eternal Body fully burst forth with power, and one after another extremely powerful Eternal arts were also unleashed.
Buzz buzz buzz!!!!
Countless terrifying sword qi tore apart the laws and slashed toward the five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings. It was clearly the Eternal art, Void-Splitting Sword, unleashed with full force.
The current Void-Splitting Sword had been further perfected by Ye Tian and was even more terrifying than before, and it had been cultivated to a very profound level.
The power of this sword had already reached the level of the weakest half-step Eternal Realm power.
The five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings blocked this sword with all their might, yet they were still severely injured.
“Power of half-step Eternal Realm!”
The expressions of the five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings changed drastically.
How could a Seventh-Level Supreme Being unleash power comparable to a Ninth-Level Supreme Being?
Although it was the power of the weakest half-step Eternal Realm, it could not be compared with those top half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses at all, but they still could not defeat it!
They were not those monstrous geniuses whose Ninth-Level Supreme Being strength was enough to match half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses!
“Run!”
This thought immediately arose in the minds of the five Ninth-Level Supreme Beings.
At once, they used their trump cards and fled at the fastest speed.
For example, one Ninth-Level Supreme Being took out a top-grade source artifact that could pierce through the Source Sea void and cross the void over long distances, thereby escaping from here.
Another Ninth-Level Supreme Being used a secret treasure that could temporarily increase speed a hundredfold, but it could only be used once.
In short, they all tried every possible means to save their lives.
If they stayed here, they would not survive at all.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian also used his own trump card and unleashed the Destroying Finger, activating the power of the Eternal Realm finger bone.
Immediately, a strike comparable to a powerful half-step Eternal Realm directly shattered the Source Sea void. A large area collapsed and shattered on the spot, and three Ninth-Level Supreme Beings who did not escape in time were directly crushed into fragments, their vitality completely erased.
A single strike killed them instantly, and none of their trump cards could save their lives.
This was the difference between an ordinary top Ninth-Tier Peak powerhouse and combat power at the level of a powerful half-step Eternal Realm; the gap was simply too great.
At this time, another Ninth-Level Supreme Being was severely injured, and one more had pierced through the void and escaped.
“I already said, you cannot escape!”
Ye Tian murmured.
After another Destroying Finger strike blasted the heavily injured Ninth-Level Supreme Being to death, he immediately activated the Void Source Hall, locked onto the other party’s position, and began the pursuit.
……
Somewhere in the Source Sea.
The last of the five great Ninth-Level Supreme Beings, Qi Xue Source Ancestor, used a source artifact to pierce through the void and arrive at a certain region, then finally breathed a sigh of relief.
He felt that Ye Tian would not be able to catch up to him in time; by the time Ye Tian reached here, he would already have left.
“Leave this place first!”
Qi Xue Source Ancestor was just about to depart.
Suddenly, a powerful force appeared and suppressed this stretch of void.
Then Ye Tian’s body stepped out from the void.
“How could this be…”
Qi Xue Source Ancestor was stunned.
He had already roughly guessed why Ye Tian had caught up so quickly: he must have possessed some special source artifact or other treasure that could perform long-distance void teleportation and lock onto a position.
Moreover, during their battle, Ye Tian had silently locked onto the positions of all five of them, so when he used the source artifact to flee, he was already locked on.
Otherwise, Ye Tian would not know where he had teleported to, and would not be able to pursue him.
“So from the very beginning, he wanted to kill all five of us!”
Qi Xue Source Ancestor trembled inwardly.
“Endless Ancestor, I’ll tell you who wants to deal with you, just don’t kill me!”
Qi Xue Source Ancestor begged for mercy.
“No need, I can find out!”
Ye Tian activated the Destroying Finger and killed Qi Xue Source Ancestor with one strike.
After returning to the Dark Forbidden Domain, Ye Tian entered the Source God Pavilion and requested to meet Feng Gu Source Ancestor.
Very quickly, Feng Gu Source Ancestor met Ye Tian.
“Endless Ancestor, what do you seek me for?”
Feng Gu Source Ancestor asked.
Ye Tian hurriedly said, “Lord Feng Gu Source Ancestor, I want to ask, if there is a conflict between inner circle members of the Source God Pavilion and they kill each other, will the Source God Pavilion intervene?”
Feng Gu Source Ancestor understood Ye Tian’s meaning and directly said, “If an inner circle member asks for help, the twelve ancestors will make one move, but only one move; this is the welfare treatment of every inner circle member.”
“Feng Gu Source Ancestor, I understand!”
Ye Tian slightly nodded, then left immediately.
The twelve ancestors would make a move, but the premise was that Feng Gu Source Ancestor and the other twelve ancestors received the distress message and could arrive in time.
What if that inner circle member did not have time to ask for help?
Therefore, relying on the protection of the Source God Pavilion was of no real use at all.
For other Supreme Beings, the Source God Pavilion was just a loose organization; it was not bad for trading, but it would not truly help a member free of charge.
Afterward.
Ye Tian contacted other inner circle members and used some treasures and resources to exchange for a piece of information: which member had a relationship with Jinlan Mountain?
This intelligence was not hard to investigate, so Ye Tian naturally found it.
Among the many inner circle members, there was only one member belonging to Jinlan Mountain.
This person was Ge Fei Source Ancestor!
Ge Fei Source Ancestor was a Ninth-Level Supreme Being of Jinlan Mountain, and also one of its founders.
After receiving the news, Ye Tian immediately came to Jinlan Mountain.
Source Sea, Jinlan World.
This was the Eternal Heaven and Earth, while Jinlan Mountain was the ruling force of the Jinlan Heaven and Earth.
When Ye Tian descended here and used his copying talent to investigate Jinlan Mountain, he did not find Ge Fei Source Ancestor.
Immediately afterward, he captured a Supreme Being from Jinlan Mountain and interrogated him.
In the end, these Supreme Beings also could not contact Ge Fei Source Ancestor.
Clearly, Ge Fei Source Ancestor had run away.
Ye Tian did not kill these Supreme Beings of Jinlan Mountain. They were unaware, and killing them was useless, but Ye Tian still seized Jinlan Mountain’s treasury, counting it as their punishment.
In addition, if Ge Fei Source Ancestor was found in the future, he would pursue and kill him immediately, giving the other party no chance to survive.
Somewhere in the Source Sea void.
Ge Fei Source Ancestor appeared here, and at this moment he looked flustered and helpless.
“Damn it, the Endless Ancestor’s strength is actually so terrifying. Even Qi Xue Source Ancestor and the others have fallen. Luckily, I escaped fast enough, otherwise I would have been dead for sure!”
“I can’t return to Jinlan World in the future, and I also can’t enter the Source God Pavilion. I must find a place to hide.”
Ge Fei Source Ancestor muttered to himself.
Very quickly, he disappeared from this area, without a trace.


Chapter 1627 Ten Thousand Tribulation Yuan, Eighth Supreme Being!

Chapter 1627 Ten Thousand Tribulation Yuan, Eighth Supreme Being!

Ge Fei Domain Ancestor fled, but to Ye Tian, that was not a big deal at all.
In the future, once his strength became greater, Ge Fei Domain Ancestor would be even less daring to show up; otherwise, showing up would mean death.
Therefore, he did not care much about Ge Fei Domain Ancestor.
In addition, through this matter, Ye Tian's strength was considered exposed.
The outside world now knew that he possessed the strength of a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert, and that he was a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert with the ability to create clones.
Even an incomparably powerful Half-Step Eternal Realm expert would not offend Ye Tian without enormous benefits.
The Primal Tree was indeed very precious, but that was only speculation, and they had no confidence in seizing the Primal Tree, so they would not make a move.
Otherwise, once they offended a Supreme Being like Ye Tian, whose prospects were limitless, if Ye Tian's cultivation reached the Ninth Supreme Being, or even Half-Step Eternal Realm, then their trouble would be enormous.
Therefore, the other Supreme Beings, and even the Half-Step Eternal Realm experts, gave up the idea of dealing with Ye Tian.
The Dark Forbidden Domain also became calm, and the Invincible experts of the human race gradually dared to leave the Dark Forbidden Domain and venture out into the outside world.
Ye Tian also began to cultivate in closed seclusion, raising his cultivation.
In any case, he was not short of resources now, so naturally he wanted to raise his cultivation to the Eighth Supreme Being realm as soon as possible.
The stronger one's strength was, the more treasure lands and good places one could go to.
There were far too many mysterious places in Source Sea. With his current strength, he was not yet qualified to touch the true secrets of Source Sea; even the Void Source Ancestor of the Void Source Hall back then had only been an ordinary Half-Step Eternal Realm expert, a truly invincible existence in the eyes of ordinary Supreme Beings, and a top combat power in Source Sea.
But in truth, Void Source Ancestor was really not qualified.
Only after seeing the existence of Eternal Realm did Ye Tian truly realize that a powerhouse like Void Source Ancestor really was nothing much.
Even now, if he borrowed the finger of an Eternal Realm expert, he would be enough to exchange blows with Void Source Ancestor for a while.
“Back then, the number of Void Sons and Void Divine Sons was so small. In fact, many Invincible experts from powerful forces simply looked down on the Void Source Stele of the mere Void Source Hall; only the Invincible experts of some weak Eternal Heavens longed to become Void Sons!” Ye Tian murmured.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian continued cultivating.
And in the years that followed, one Supreme Being after another was born among the human race.
For example, Ye Tian's daughter and younger sister also successively broke through to the Supreme Being realm.
Moreover, Ye Tian provided the human race with a large amount of Eternal resources. For at least a very long period of time, anyone who reached the First Supreme Being would be qualified to obtain some Eternal resources.
This was a benefit Ye Tian gave to the human race.
Unknowingly, one Tribulation Yuan after another passed.
Ten thousand Tribulation Yuan!
Twenty thousand Tribulation Yuan!
Thirty thousand Tribulation Yuan!
……
Ye Jinpeng, Ye Xingchen, and the other Supreme Beings gradually advanced to the Second Supreme Being realm, and the number of Supreme Beings born in the human race had already reached more than ten, gradually catching up to the Tianlin Realm.
Before they knew it, the ten-thousand-Tribulation-Yuan protection period of the Dark Forbidden Domain was almost over.
And at this time, Ye Tian had also cultivated to the peak of the Seventh Supreme Being realm, and could step into the Eighth Supreme Being realm at any moment.
Not only that, his comprehension of the Eternal Laws had reached an incomparably terrifying level, because he had repeatedly copied Innate Eternal Lifeforms and comprehended the Innate Eternal Laws.
Therefore, Ye Tian understood the Innate Eternal Laws very well, and the Eternal techniques he created were naturally even more powerful.
In addition, Ye Tian's foundations were incomparably solid.
It was also because of the issue of foundations that he spent so long cultivating; otherwise, he would have already broken through to the Eighth Supreme Being realm, and would not have waited until today.
On this day.
Ye Tian began to charge toward the Eighth Supreme Being realm. After consuming several treasures and resources that aided breakthrough, Ye Tian easily broke through to the Eighth Supreme Being realm, and his strength once again crossed a limit.
At this point, his combat strength was already comparable to an ordinary Half-Step Eternal Realm expert, rather than the weakest Half-Step Eternal Realm expert.
However, at this level, it was not possible for Ye Tian to rapidly cultivate to the Ninth Supreme Being realm.
Unless he obtained the resources on the Black Mist Worm clone from the Primal Sea, but the Primal Sea could only be opened once every long span of time; ten thousand Tribulation Yuan was nothing at all.
According to what he knew, the interval between each opening of the Primal Sea was ten million Tribulation Yuan.
Even so, many Supreme Beings were still waiting for it, but Ye Tian could not afford to wait.
He had no way to wait through such a long stretch of time; perhaps by then, he would no longer need the resources of the Primal Sea.
Therefore, he wanted to leave the Primal Sea as soon as possible.
The Primal Sea was not without a way out; for example, those two Eternal Realm experts could casually tear apart the Primal Sea void and take away so many Black Mist Worms from the Primal Sea.
Therefore, he could also leave the Primal Sea, as long as his strength was strong enough, or he had special methods.
During these years, Ye Tian's Black Mist Worm clone had already cultivated to the extreme of the Ninth Stage, and could step into the Half-Step Eternal Realm at any time.
Moreover, the Black Mist Worm clone had also comprehended a number of Eternal techniques suitable for the Black Mist Worm clone. Combining these with the Black Mist Worm race, he even thought of an excellent method to raise his strength, but that would have a major impact on the foundation.
But this was only a clone; even if this clone was sacrificed, as long as the treasures were brought out, it would all be worth it.
On this day.
Ye Tian's Black Mist Worm clone arrived at the Primal Tree, and he uprooted the Primal Tree and stored it in his inner space.
Afterward, he also took away the newly born resources of the Primal Sea.
“I have to leave now, otherwise if I'm discovered by the Eternal Realm powerhouses, it would be a small matter if this clone perishes. But if those resources are taken away, the loss would be too great!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Thus, he began to charge toward the Supreme Being realm.
Boom!!!
Ye Tian executed an Eternal technique that devoured other lifeforms—Black Mist Worm Devouring Art!
Immediately, a large number of Black Mist Worms were swallowed by Ye Tian's Black Mist Worm clone and absorbed into his body, then refined by other means, turning into streams of power to help him charge toward the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
Very quickly, the shackle was broken!
The biggest difference between the Half-Step Eternal Realm and the Supreme Being realm was that Supreme Beings had unified flesh and soul, inseparable from each other, but the body and the Eternal Laws were not yet unified.
The Half-Step Eternal Realm was when the body and the Eternal Laws reached a state of compatibility, using that compatibility to break the shackle and thus advance to the Half-Step Eternal Realm, but in truth they still had not truly fused, only blended together.
It was like mixing two kinds of wine together; on the surface it looked like one wine, but upon careful distinction, it was still a mixture of two wines.
Precisely because of this, the Half-Step Eternal Realm was called “Half-Step.”
And the Black Mist Worm clone was forcefully using a large number of Black Mist Worms as energy, forcibly allowing the Eternal Laws within its body to blend with its body, thereby crossing into the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
This method was detrimental to the foundation, and future potential would be affected, with even no hope of becoming an Eternal Realm expert.
But Ye Tian did not care about that.
After breaking through to the Half-Step Eternal Realm, Ye Tian continued devouring other Black Mist Worms, and his strength grew stronger and stronger.


Chapter 1628 Refining an Eternal Source Weapon!

Chapter 1628 Refining an Eternal Source Weapon!

The densely packed black fog insects had become Ye Tian’s food, and this way of devouring made him increasingly terrifying at the half-step Eternal Realm. Even he did not know how powerful he had become.
However, he was very clear that only by becoming stronger could he leave this place.
In fact, after the source tide of the Primal Sea ended, it was not impossible to leave. It was just that, upon leaving, one would be killed by the black fog insects, which was why the top half-step Eternal Realm experts outside did not dare remain in the Primal Sea. Naturally, Ye Tian’s black fog insect clone was not afraid of black fog insects.
“Almost there!”
Ye Tian felt that it was difficult to further improve his strength, and there was no need to continue cultivating. He could try leaving the Primal Sea.
Boom!!!!
The void of the Primal Sea was shattered.
Ye Tian forcibly shattered the void of the Primal Sea. His not-so-huge body burned part of its body and power in exchange for even more terrifying strength, drilling his way out toward the outside world.
Space shattered, and time and space surged.
Ye Tian followed the connection with his true body and headed toward the Source Sea.
Very quickly.
Somewhere in the Source Sea, the void split open, and a black fog insect drilled out. At this moment, its whole body was already almost shattered. In order to break out of the Primal Sea, this clone was nearly ruined.
At this time, Ye Tian’s copy body had long been waiting here. It immediately took the countless resources from the black fog insect clone, then the copy body immediately fled, leaving only the black fog insect clone behind.
He did not dare take the black fog insect clone away. If it attracted other Eternal Realm experts, even the Void Source Hall would not be able to protect him.
Therefore, it was better to be careful. After the copy body left, Ye Tian immediately severed all aura, allowing this black fog insect clone to completely fall and perish, and its body also began to Annihilation.
In this way, even if an Eternal Realm expert came, nothing could be found out.
As expected.
A mysterious Eternal Realm expert, his whole body shrouded in darkness, appeared here and wanted to investigate something, but found nothing at all.
After that, this mysterious Eternal Realm expert left.
To him, this was only a trivial matter, not worth investigating.
……
“I’m back!”
Ye Tian let out a sigh of relief.
Immediately after, he took out those resources, and was instantly overjoyed.
These resources, when accumulated together, were enough to arouse greed in any half-step Eternal Realm expert.
“I now have a lot of Undying Primal Stones in my hands; I can forge an Eternal Source Weapon for myself. The weapons I’ve been using have all been top-grade source weapons, and they can no longer keep up with my strength.”
Ye Tian murmured.
In the following days, he began forging an Eternal Source Weapon.
Of course, he first spent a lot of materials tempering his weapon-refining skill.
In fact, he often refined source weapons for the human race. Now, refining ordinary source weapons was very simple for him; it was just that the success rate for refining top-grade source weapons was not very high.
But this time, he had gained too much. The materials for refining top-grade source weapons, he had obtained in endless quantities, and he was not afraid of consumption at all.
Time passed, and in the blink of an eye, dozens of tribulation eras had gone by.
During these dozens of tribulation eras, Ye Tian almost day and night tempered his weapon-refining level, and finally he had nearly a one hundred percent certainty of refining top-grade source weapons.
So, he began refining Eternal Source Weapons.
With so many Undying Primal Stones, it was enough for him to waste them, and there was no fear of failing.
The first refinement failed; Ye Tian wasted one Undying Primal Stone.
But he did not feel distressed and continued refining.
Just like that, Ye Tian failed at refining again and again, but his experience became more and more abundant, and his mistakes became fewer and fewer.
Finally, after wasting seventeen Undying Primal Stones, Ye Tian finally succeeded in refining an Eternal Source Weapon, a sword.
Ye Tian named this weapon the Endless Eternal Sword!
Afterwards.
Ye Tian refined another Eternal Source Weapon-level full-body armor, which consumed a full six Undying Primal Stones.
A set of full-body armor, a sword.
These two kinds of Eternal Source Weapons increased Ye Tian’s strength by at least more than thirty percent.
Afterward, Ye Tian bestowed some of the source weapons he had refined upon the Supreme Beings of the human race. After all, these things were of little use to him.
With Eternal Source Weapons in hand, Ye Tian no longer refined Eternal Source Weapons.
He called his wife, Xiao Yue.
“Husband!” Xiao Yue came over.
“Yue’er, this is the heart of the Primal Tree. Use it to refine a special clone. The clone and the true body will have the same strength, and it can also cultivate, with mutual sharing of insights.”
Ye Tian took out the heart of the Primal Tree and handed it to Xiao Yue.
Such a good thing—he only had one right now, so he would only give it to his wife, not even his son, let alone anyone else.
“It can be used to refine a clone?”
Xiao Yue was extremely excited.
She did not know the value of the heart of the Primal Tree; otherwise, she would not have accepted it so readily.
After that, Xiao Yue took the heart of the Primal Tree away to refine a clone.
Not long after, Xiao Yue’s clone was successfully refined, with no real difference from the true body.
··········求鮮花··· ·····
“Husband, I’m going out to gain experience.”
