“Husband, I understand!”
Xiao Yue nodded.
Afterward, Ye Tian no longer bothered with his wife Xiao Yue and let her go out to train as she pleased.
As for himself, he went into seclusion once more.
This time, he again copied the body of a Innate Eternal Life Form, and at the same time his true body began to consume Eternal Comprehension Flowers.
He had three Eternal Comprehension Flowers. Even half-step Eternal Realm experts would be incomparably eager to obtain one.
Moreover, Ye Tian possessed the Immortal Ancestor Gift, allowing him to bring out the effects of the Eternal Comprehension Flower to a greater extent.
The benefits he gained from absorbing one Eternal Comprehension Flower were absolutely comparable to the benefits other half-step Eternal Realm experts would gain from absorbing dozens or even hundreds of Eternal Comprehension Flowers.
This time, Ye Tian planned to use these three Eternal Comprehension Flowers to condense innate Eternal rules.
Eternal rules were divided into ordinary Eternal rules and innate Eternal rules. For example, the Eternal rules engraved within an Innate Eternal Life Form’s body were innate Eternal rules, which was what made Innate Eternal Life Forms so valuable and so immensely promising.
And for ordinary lifeforms, wanting to condense innate Eternal rules was almost impossible, unless they entered the Eternal Realm; only then could they condense innate Eternal rules and grasp them.
Although Innate Eternal Life Forms possessed innate Eternal rules within their bodies, in reality they had not mastered them. Only after breaking through to the Eternal Realm could they control them freely. This was also one of their flaws.
But compared with other lifeforms, Innate Eternal Life Forms unquestionably had too great an advantage.
“Among half-step Eternal Realm experts, only those half-step Eternal Realm experts who have grasped innate Eternal rules are truly nearly invincible. Half of the Twelve Ancestors have grasped innate Eternal rules, which is why they can stand above other half-step Eternal Realm experts and make countless top great powers of the Source Sea fear them.”
Ye Tian murmured.
His comprehension of Eternal rules was already very deep, but he was still a little short of condensing innate Eternal rules.
Therefore, he planned to rely on the three Eternal Comprehension Flowers he had obtained this time; he was absolutely hopeful of succeeding in one go.
This time, the innate Eternal rule he intended to condense was strength!
Because he possessed the Immortal Ancestor Gift of strength, he had the greatest chance of condensing the strength innate Eternal rule.
“Let’s begin!”
Ye Tian took out one Eternal Comprehension Flower and.


Chapter 1629: A Half-Step Eternal Realm at the Extreme Stage!

Chapter 1629: A Half-Step Eternal Realm at the Extreme Stage!

Ye Tian swallowed this Eternal Enlightenment Flower, and his comprehension instantly broke through some kind of shackle, rising to an unimaginably high level.
Ye Tian took this opportunity to begin comprehending the innate Eternal rules within the innate Eternal lifeform, and his understanding of the Eternal rules improved at an incredible speed.
Gradually, Ye Tian’s Eternal rules began undergoing a qualitative transformation.
But at this moment, the effect of the first Eternal Enlightenment Flower faded.
So, Ye Tian immediately took the second Eternal Enlightenment Flower and continued comprehending the innate Eternal rules.
It was only when the second Eternal Enlightenment Flower was about to lose its effect that Ye Tian finally comprehended the innate Eternal rules.
Buzz!!!!
The innate power Eternal rules were engraved onto Ye Tian’s body, faintly seeming as if they were about to merge with him, but the fusion failed. After all, he was not a true Eternal realm being yet, so he had no way to completely fuse with the Eternal rules, let alone the innate Eternal rules.
But even being merely engraved upon his own body allowed Ye Tian to grasp the innate power Eternal rules, and his strength underwent a heaven-shaking qualitative transformation.
“There’s still one Eternal Enlightenment Flower left. I won’t use it for now; I’ll keep it.”
Ye Tian muttered.
Moreover, having now mastered the innate power Eternal rules—just a single innate Eternal rule—Ye Tian had also broken through his shackle and stepped into the level of innate Eternal rules.
From now on, it would be much easier for him to comprehend other innate Eternal rules, equivalent to mastering one method and applying it to all methods.
Afterward, Ye Tian comprehended for some more time. His strength still improved somewhat, but he was still far from the Ninth Supreme Being Stage.
However, his normal combat strength was already crushing that of an ordinary Half-Step Eternal Realm, and within the Half-Step Eternal Realm, he could be considered quite outstanding.
Moreover, the finger of an Eternal realm expert was no longer of much help to him; at most, it could only increase his strength severalfold.
If he advanced to the Ninth Supreme Being Stage, then the finger of an Eternal realm expert would completely lose its usefulness to him.
But this was a good thing, enough to prove that Ye Tian was growing stronger and stronger.
On this day.
An enormous event occurred in the Source Sea: the top major force of the Source Sea, the Dragon Scale Sacred Hall, was destroyed, and even the Dragon Scale Sacred World was obliterated.
The key point was that after the Dragon Scale Sacred World was destroyed, other forces discovered it only afterward; before that, not a single plea for help had been transmitted.
If some ordinary force had been wiped out like this, that would have been one thing, but the key was that the Dragon Scale Sacred World was not weak—it was a true top major force, possessing three Half-Step Eternal Realm beings, dozens of Ninth Supreme Beings, and over one hundred thousand Supreme Beings. It was a truly ancient force.

Although the founder of the Dragon Scale Sacred Hall fell long ago, the Sea Ancestor of the Dragon Scale Sacred Hall is very powerful, much stronger than Void Source Ancestor. Such a force was actually destroyed without a sound; I’m afraid this involves an even more powerful existence, and it may even involve an Eternal realm being.” The spirit said.
“Forget it. This has nothing to do with us. Naturally, other forces will investigate it.”
Ye Tian muttered.
Some more time passed, and the impact brought by the destruction of the Dragon Scale Sacred Hall gradually faded.
But on this day, yet another force was destroyed.
This force was the Myriad Ancient Sect, a force that had risen through a sect. It had originally been a sect force in an Eternal Heaven and Earth, but later a powerful prodigy was born there. Rising all the way, that prodigy elevated the Myriad Ancient Sect to a level comparable to the major forces of the Source Sea, and even occupied a blessed land in the Source Sea, where a brand-new Myriad Ancient Sect was established.
The Myriad Ancient Sect was not as powerful as the Dragon Scale Sacred Hall, but it still had one Half-Step Eternal Realm being, and there were also many Supreme Beings in the sect.
Yet even so, the Myriad Ancient Sect was still completely annihilated.
In the days that followed, one force after another was silently destroyed; among them were even quite a few forces without Half-Step Eternal Realm beings, possessing only Eighth or Ninth Supreme Beings, and yet they were still targeted.

Source God Pavilion.

Only then did they move to destroy those forces. Extreme Stage!
Ye Tian also knew this division of levels: those who had mastered innate Eternal rules and whose strength far surpassed top Eternal realm experts were Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm beings.
It was said that Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm beings were further divided into First Extreme Stage, Second Extreme Stage, Third Extreme Stage...
The highest was the Ninth Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm, but such a Half-Step Eternal Realm could even defeat ordinary Eternal realm beings; in this era, they practically did not exist.
The twelve ancestors of Source God Pavilion possessed six Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm beings, but they were all at the First Extreme Stage. As for whether they had hidden strength, that was unknown.
But Source God Pavilion was a loose organization with no real constraints, so it posed no threat to many top major forces.
At this moment.
Some inner-circle members even suspected whether the twelve ancestors were behind this, but thinking about the twelve ancestors’ personalities, they probably would not do such a thing. However, if this matter was not resolved for a day, the fear in their hearts could not be erased.

Chapter 1630: The enemy’s identity has been uncovered!

Chapter 1630: The enemy’s identity has been uncovered!

Zhenhe Sword Ancestor said, “We went to investigate the ruins of the Dragon Scale Sacred World. The enemy left very quickly, and so there were some clues left behind. The other side clearly used another Eternal Source Weapon—the Blood Devouring Bead. Based on our speculation, some mysterious force is preparing this time to use the Blood Devouring Bead to devour a large number of Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm experts in order to break through to the Eternal Realm.”
“Can the Eternal Realm be broken through like that?”
Someone was very puzzled.
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor continued, “Of course it isn’t that easy. One must also prepare all kinds of other precious and rare resources, and even then the success rate is less than one in ten. Moreover, even if the breakthrough succeeds, it still does not count as a true Eternal Realm. It can only be considered a pseudo-Eternal Realm, possessing the strength of the Eternal Realm but not the power of the Eternal Realm. A true Eternal Realm can fuse with the Eternal Rule, and after breaking through and cultivating for some time, one can fuse with the innate Eternal Rule and wield the true power of the innate Eternal Rule. However, if one breaks through using a method like the Blood Devouring Bead, one cannot fuse with the innate Eternal Rule, and can even fail to perfectly fuse with an ordinary Eternal Rule.”
“But for some half-step Eternal Realm experts at the Extreme Stage, once they see no hope of breaking through, using this method to step into the Eternal Realm is enough so long as they gain the power of the Eternal Realm. They do not care about the future.”
“Furthermore, once one breaks through to the Eternal Realm, even if it is a flawed Eternal Realm, the actual battle strength is still that of a true Eternal Realm. And the Eternal Realm power gained after breaking through from the Extreme Stage is terrifying; some top-tier Eternal Realm experts who break through normally may not necessarily be stronger than them.”
After Zhenhe Sword Ancestor finished speaking, many Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm experts became rather worried about their own safety.
If that mysterious force set its sights on them, how could they possibly resist an Extreme Stage powerhouse!

If a half-step Eternal Realm expert at the Extreme Stage appears in Moon-Gathering Pavilion, the enemy will not show up. You go to Moon-Gathering Pavilion, and if the enemy appears, notify us immediately. However, the enemy’s strength is terrifying, so it is very likely we will not make it in time.”
At this, Ye Tian guaranteed, “Twelve Ancestors, I may not be able to block the enemy, but once the enemy appears, I have a way to investigate their identity.”
“Really?”
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor and the others were shocked.
Based on their understanding, the enemy concealed their aura, and even altered it. Moreover, when an Extreme Stage half-step Eternal Realm expert made a move, they almost instantly killed those ordinary or powerful half-step Eternal Realm experts and Supreme Beings.

Ye Tian shook his head and said, “This is my secret. Please do not ask, Twelve Ancestors. But I can guarantee that once the enemy appears, their identity will definitely be exposed. It would be useless even if they kill me instantly.”

Chapter 1631 The mastermind has been found!

Star Demon Source Ancestor has a disciple in the Eternal Realm?

Star Demon Source Ancestor thought to himself.

Ancient God Palace!

Suddenly.

The many half-step Eternal Realm experts from Star Demon Mountain were frozen in place. Although they had not yet died, once they were frozen for too long and their bodies were frozen and shattered, then they would truly die.


Chapter 1632 Star Demon Source Ancestor, Fallen!

Chapter 1632 Star Demon Source Ancestor, Fallen!

“Star Demon Source Ancestor, you have committed too many killings and slaughtered so many forces. You deserve to die!”
Absolute Ice Ancestor appeared.
She was a woman, wearing translucent battle armor, with grains of ice crystals floating around her. Those ice crystals were not real ice crystals, but Eternal source weapons—Infinite Ice Sand!
“Absolute Ice Ancestor, aren’t you afraid of the Eternal Being behind me? Moreover, you clearly had time to stop me just now, but you didn’t stop me. Instead, you set up a great array. I want to ask, what grudge is there between us?” Star Demon Source Ancestor questioned.
“You killed Lanyue!”
Absolute Ice Ancestor said coldly.
“Lanyue Source Ancestor, you have a relationship with her?”
Star Demon Source Ancestor was stunned.
How could Lanyue Source Ancestor be related to Absolute Ice Ancestor? Why didn’t Lanyue Source Ancestor say so back then?
No.
Even if Lanyue Source Ancestor had said so back then, he would not have believed it. He would only think that Lanyue Source Ancestor was deliberately saying that in order to save her life.
Moreover, in order to hide his identity, he was also impossible to listen to whatever Lanyue Source Ancestor said. He would not waste even a little time. Even if Lanyue Source Ancestor had said it, it would have been useless.
Precisely because of this, Lanyue Source Ancestor did not say it out.
“Lanyue is my junior. I never revealed it, and all my focus was on breaking through to the Eternal Realm, so I didn’t really manage Lanyue. Originally, I thought Lanyue’s strength was that of a powerful half-step Eternal Realm expert, and since she didn’t get involved in fights, there shouldn’t have been much danger in the source sea, so there was no need to rely on my influence. I never expected that you would actually kill her.”
Absolute Ice Ancestor was incomparably furious.
She had only been in seclusion for a little longer, and then she suddenly sensed that her junior Lanyue had fallen and died, which was what woke her up and made her come out of seclusion.
After coming out, she learned that Star Demon Source Ancestor had killed Lanyue.
In order not to kill the wrong person, she did not act immediately, but instead kept watch over Star Demon Mountain.
In the end, Star Demon Source Ancestor attacked again, and she confirmed the target, but she was too lazy to save the Ancient God Palace. Instead, she chose to directly set up a killing array in this area of the Ancient God Palace.
This time, she would definitely kill Star Demon Source Ancestor.
“Kill!”
Infinite Ice Sand activated, and the spacetime of this region directly shattered. Those half-step Eternal Realm experts could finally no longer hold on either. One by one, their bodies shattered and died, leaving only Star Demon Source Ancestor alone.
Star Demon Source Ancestor also had no time to feel sorry for the fall of these half-step Eternal Realm experts. If he could not escape today, he would also have to die.
Boom!!!
Star Demon Source Ancestor’s defenses collapsed inch by inch.
And Infinite Ice Sand transformed into a sword, piercing in.
No matter how Star Demon Source Ancestor defended, he was still pierced through by a single strike, and the injured area even showed signs of freezing. Even though his recovery ability was terrifying, the injured area was still shattering at a frequency of hundreds of millions of times per breath.
“Run!”
Star Demon Source Ancestor did not want to fight Absolute Ice Ancestor.
The other side was a half-step Eternal Realm expert at the Seven Extreme Stage, while he was only at the Three Calamities Extreme Stage; there was a huge gap in strength between them.
Moreover, as one of the six extreme experts of the source sea, she had many trump cards. He had not a shred of hope of winning.
Suddenly.
Star Demon Source Ancestor activated the Time-Space Grain Sand Pearl, shrinking the suppression range, wanting to suppress Absolute Ice Ancestor and thereby create a chance for himself to escape.
However, after all, the Time-Space Grain Sand Pearl was only the lowest-grade Eternal source weapon.
In just one breath, the Time-Space Grain Sand Pearl was forcibly shattered by Absolute Ice Ancestor.
In the source sea.
Star Demon Source Ancestor kept fleeing, while Absolute Ice Ancestor relentlessly pursued and killed him.
At this point, all the countless forces in the source sea knew that Star Demon Source Ancestor was being hunted, and each of them was extremely shocked.
……
“Star Demon Source Ancestor is being hunted by Absolute Ice Ancestor?”
Ye Tian was truly surprised upon learning this news.
He had thought that no half-step Eternal Realm expert would go and kill Star Demon Source Ancestor, but he hadn’t expected a strong expert to act so quickly.
As for Absolute Ice Ancestor, Ye Tian knew very little. He only knew that she was one of the six extreme experts of the source sea.
These six extreme experts were basically all half-step Eternal Realm experts at the Seven Extreme Stage. A few might have reached the Eight Extreme Stage, but there were no half-step Eternal Realm experts at the Nine Extreme Stage.
These six extreme experts were all trying to break through to the Eternal Realm.
However, strength had no necessary connection with breaking through to the Eternal Realm. Some weaker half-step Eternal Realm experts instead managed to break through, while half-step Eternal Realm experts like Absolute Ice Ancestor found it even harder to do so.
But once such a half-step Eternal Realm expert did break through, then after becoming an Eternal Realm expert, their strength would also be incomparably terrifying.
Time slowly passed, and many half-step Eternal Realm experts in the source sea were all paying attention to Star Demon Source Ancestor’s fate.
Although Star Demon Source Ancestor had an Eternal Being behind him, whether that Eternal Being would come or not was still uncertain.
Moreover, they were almost unable to contact Eternal Beings, and Star Demon Source Ancestor was probably the same.
Perhaps, even if Star Demon Source Ancestor were killed, that Eternal Being still would not know.
However, Star Demon Source Ancestor was after all a Three Extreme Stage half-step Eternal Realm expert. For a Seven Extreme Stage half-step Eternal Realm expert to kill a Three Extreme Stage half-step Eternal Realm expert still required some time; it was not something that could be instantly done with a single move.
……
In a spacetime ruin in the source sea.
Star Demon Source Ancestor’s entire body had been crystallized with ice, and his injuries were already extremely severe.
After all, this place was covered and completely sealed by Infinite Ice Sand.
Star Demon Source Ancestor had already used up many of his treasures, and coupled with his severe injuries, he simply could not break out and leave.
“Absolute Ice Ancestor, do you really want to kill me? If you kill me, my disciple, the Eternal Being Linghe Lord, will not let you go. You are already a Seven Extreme Stage expert, with an unlimited future. There’s no need to be killed by an Eternal Being because of this.”
Star Demon Source Ancestor tried to persuade her.
“Even if I am hunted by an Eternal Being, I will still kill you!”
Absolute Ice Ancestor said angrily.
And all around, the gazes of one half-step Eternal Realm expert after another were being cast over, as if they were watching the show.
And Star Demon Source Ancestor knew he could not persuade Absolute Ice Ancestor, and also feared that he would not be able to wait for Linghe Lord to arrive in time, so he could only ask for help from the surrounding onlooking half-step Eternal Realm experts.
“Whoever saves me will be able to obtain the friendship of Linghe Lord, and even receive Linghe Lord’s guidance!” Star Demon Source Ancestor’s voice spread across the surrounding region.
However, no one helped.
Who would dare offend Absolute Ice Ancestor? Are they courting death?
Unless it was the other five of the six extreme experts, but experts of that level were simply disdainful of Linghe Lord’s guidance, and Linghe Lord also simply could not provide guidance to them.
Soon.
Star Demon Source Ancestor’s body was pierced through again and again by Infinite Ice Sand, and the speed at which his body crystallized with ice became faster and faster. Moreover, the heavily injured Star Demon Source Ancestor simply could no longer recover from his injuries.
After a long time, Star Demon Source Ancestor finally could no longer resist, and his body was completely crystallized.
Then, after a crisp crack, Star Demon Source Ancestor completely shattered into countless powder, and his vitality as well as consciousness completely dissipated.
At this point, Star Demon Source Ancestor had fallen and died.
And at this moment, a terrifying aura transmitted over.
An Eternal Being had arrived!.


Chapter 1633: Spirit Crane Lord and Lianyi Lord!

Chapter 1633: Spirit Crane Lord and Lianyi Lord!

“Spirit Crane Lord!”
The Extreme Ice Ancestor felt Spirit Crane Lord’s aura and immediately frowned.
She had once had dealings with Spirit Crane Lord, but at that time, Spirit Crane Lord was only at half-step Eternal Realm and had merely come to visit her in the posture of a junior.
Of course, the two of them had only met once.
But she had never expected that Spirit Crane Lord would actually fortunately become an Eternal Realm existence.
Although Spirit Crane Lord had not broken through to Eternal Realm from the Extreme half-step Eternal Realm, he had advanced through a normal breakthrough, and it had already been countless years since he reached Eternal Realm. His strength was naturally terrifying, far beyond Extreme Ice Ancestor.
“Run!”
Extreme Ice Ancestor did not want to fight an Eternal Realm existence. Even if Spirit Crane Lord’s strength in Eternal Realm was not considered powerful, he was still not someone she could contend with.
“Extreme Ice Ancestor, you actually dare to kill this Lord’s master! You’re courting death~!!!”
A big hand covering the endless void of the Source Sea suppressed her.
Layers of domains shattered and collapsed, but Extreme Ice Ancestor escaped through the void in time.
Boom!!!!!
Spirit Crane Lord appeared and pursued Extreme Ice Ancestor.
Very quickly, Extreme Ice Ancestor was caught up.
Even though she was a seven-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm expert, escaping from an Eternal Realm expert’s pursuit was far too difficult.
Unless she hid in certain special regions, she would be able to evade an Eternal Realm expert’s pursuit.
For example, the Eternal Tribulation Race’s supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain. This world was extremely special; even Eternal Realm experts found it very difficult to enter, and they had to pay a huge price.
Otherwise, the Eternal Tribulation Race would no longer exist.
Aside from the supreme Eternal Tribulation Domain, there were also some special places that restricted Eternal Realm experts from entering, or would cause their strength to plummet.
And Extreme Ice Ancestor wanted to hide in such a place, but unfortunately she was a little too slow and was caught up to by Spirit Crane Lord.
Spirit Crane Lord threw a punch, and his body, fused with the Innate Eternal Rules, did not need to mobilize any Innate Eternal Rule power. It stood above the Innate Eternal Rules and shattered all rules.
Extreme Ice Ancestor activated the Eternal origin weapon, Endless Ice Sand, forming layer upon layer of ice defenses.
However.
With that punch descending, all things fell into silence.
The countless grains of ice sand transformed from the Endless Ice Sand Eternal origin weapon were all shattered and Annihilated, and then the punch pierced through many of Extreme Ice Ancestor’s defensive treasures and struck her body.
Crack!!!!
Extreme Ice Ancestor’s body shattered, with half of her body directly Annihilated, making it difficult to recover, while the other half was also covered in countless cracks.
If she took another blow, Extreme Ice Ancestor would probably fall.
“No wonder you’re a seven-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm expert. You actually survived one of my blows without dying. Unfortunately, as long as you do not enter Eternal Realm, you will always be an ant!”
Spirit Crane Lord struck again with a punch, wanting to completely erase Extreme Ice Ancestor.
But at that moment, a slender jade hand blocked Spirit Crane Lord’s punch and directly sent him flying.
Whoosh!
A beautiful figure appeared before Extreme Ice Ancestor, smiling as she looked at Spirit Crane Lord.
“Spirit Crane Lord, let’s let this matter end here. Star Demon Source Ancestor killed too many Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm experts, and even killed Extreme Ice Ancestor’s descendants. Extreme Ice Ancestor killing Star Demon Source Ancestor is not wrong!”
The woman spoke.
“Greetings, Lianyi Lord. Does Lianyi Lord really intend to step in for a half-step Eternal Realm expert?” Spirit Crane Lord asked.
“That’s right!” Lianyi Lord said with a smile. “I am protecting Extreme Ice Ancestor, and besides, why would Star Demon Source Ancestor have Blood Devouring Beads in his possession? The method for refining this item is only possessed by us Eternal Realm experts, and using Blood Devouring Beads to assault the pseudo-Eternal Realm is also a forbidden method that is not allowed to be spread. If Spirit Crane Lord insists on killing Extreme Ice Ancestor, I’m afraid I’ll have to report this to the Lord Alliance.”
Spirit Crane Lord’s expression changed, then he immediately changed his face and smiled. “Lianyi Lord is joking. This is just a small matter. I’ll leave at once.”
Whoosh!
Spirit Crane Lord turned and left.
“Many thanks, Lianyi Lord!”
Extreme Ice Ancestor said gratefully.
“Extreme Ice Ancestor, your talent is very good, and you have hope of becoming an Eternal Realm expert. Last time I invited you to become my follower, but you refused. What about this time?” Lianyi Lord invited her again.
“Lianyi Lord, I am willing to become your follower!”
Extreme Ice Ancestor agreed.
“Good, then I’ll take you with me!”
Lianyi Lord waved her hand, took Extreme Ice Ancestor with her, and disappeared.
··········求鲜花··· ·····
----------------
Star Demon Source Ancestor fell, Spirit Crane Lord appeared and pursued Extreme Ice Ancestor, only to be rescued by another Eternal Realm expert, Lianyi Lord.
This dramatic scene quickly spread, and many people were not very familiar with Spirit Crane Lord and Lianyi Lord, especially Lianyi Lord, whom almost no half-step Eternal Realm experts had any impression of.
However, with Star Demon Source Ancestor’s fall, this was a great thing for many factions; at the very least, they no longer needed to worry every day and could pass their days in fear.
However, Ye Tian had a different feeling.
That is, half-step Eternal Realm experts also had no sense of security. Facing an Eternal Realm existence, even half-step Eternal Realm experts were nothing more than ants.
Of course, Eternal Realm experts rarely appeared in the Source Sea, unless a special situation like this time involved something that drew out Eternal Realm existences.
.... ...... 0
Otherwise, even if a half-step Eternal Realm expert fought until death, he might not necessarily encounter an Eternal Realm powerhouse.
In the years that followed, Ye Tian diligently cultivated and raised his strength, gradually forgetting about this matter.
One Tribulation Era after another passed, and Ye Tian’s cultivation continued to improve, but he was still very far from the eight-Supreme Being Limit.
Thus, over the long years, he would occasionally go to various Eternal Heavens for training, and would even occasionally accompany his wife Xiao Yue as they roamed among many treasured lands.
Meanwhile, the human race was also developing at a rapid pace, giving rise to quite a few Supreme Beings, and had already surpassed the Tianlin Realm.
Now, even the Tianlin Realm had to rely on the Dark Forbidden Domain, and even take the Dark Forbidden Domain as its backing.
In the blink of an eye, hundreds of thousands of Tribulation Era years passed.
At this point, Ye Tian had finally cultivated to the eight-Supreme Being Limit and was qualified to attempt breaking through to the nine-Supreme Being realm, which was also the greatest dream of many Supreme Beings in their entire lives.
This breakthrough posed no difficulty at all, after all, Ye Tian had already comprehended the Innate Eternal Rules, so naturally there was no difficulty in charging toward the nine-Supreme Being realm.
Very quickly, Ye Tian broke through to the nine-Supreme Being realm, and his strength increased somewhat again.
With Ye Tian’s current strength, he was already enough to be comparable to top-tier half-step Eternal Realm experts. If he borrowed a finger of an Eternal Realm expert, he would probably be able to unleash attacks comparable to the Extreme realm, but his peak strength was still somewhat short of the true Extreme realm.


Chapter 1634 The Thirteenth Ancestor of the Source God Pavilion!

Chapter 1634 The Thirteenth Ancestor of the Source God Pavilion!

“With my current strength, although I’m no match for the six Extreme experts among the twelve ancestors, I should be able to defeat the other six.”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
He wanted to become the thirteenth ancestor of the Source God Pavilion.
Although the twelve ancestors had disappointed him before, refusing to deal with the Star Demon Source Ancestor, thinking about it carefully, that was actually normal. The twelve ancestors themselves were not as strong as the Star Demon Source Ancestor. If they dared to attack the Star Demon Source Ancestor, it would be no different from courting death. Even if they joined forces with other Extreme experts to besiege the Star Demon Source Ancestor, the final outcome would still be a miserable defeat.
After all, even someone like the Ice Ancestor of Ultimate Darkness, a Half-step Eternal Realm expert at the Seven Extreme Stage, was killed by the Star Demon Source Ancestor. If not for the rescue of Leader Lian Yi, she would have been killed by the Star Demon Source Ancestor’s disciple, Leader Ling He.
It was easy to see that, without Eternal Realm backing, forcing oneself into the spotlight would only mean death.
Therefore, the Source God Pavilion’s twelve ancestors made the right choice.
Perhaps to other forces, this seemed selfish or even cruel, but reality was just like that.
If Ye Tian were to choose, and if he were not strong enough, he would not step forward either.
Besides, becoming the thirteenth ancestor of the Source God Pavilion would bring many benefits. He could learn more secrets, and it might even greatly help him in his assault on the Eternal Realm.
……
Source God Pavilion.
Ye Tian came here and applied to the twelve ancestors to become the thirteenth ancestor.
In fact, some of the Half-step Eternal Realm members within the inner circle of the Source God Pavilion also wanted to become the thirteenth ancestor, but they all failed one after another. And once they failed, they would not be able to apply for this assessment again for a very long time.
Very soon, all twelve ancestors received Ye Tian’s application information.
“The Endless Ancestor wants to apply to become the thirteenth ancestor?”
True River Sword Ancestor and the others were extremely shocked.
What realm was the Endless Ancestor in, to actually dare apply for the thirteenth ancestor?
“Should we reject him? What realm is he even in? This is simply absurd!” Wind Ancient Source Ancestor shook his head and said.
“Any inner circle member has the qualification to apply to become the thirteenth ancestor, and we have no requirement for cultivation level. We only require strength and background. As long as it is not a force with huge conflict with the Source God Pavilion, we accept them! And the Endless Ancestor meets the standards. We have no reason to reject him.” True River Sword Ancestor said.
“Then agree to it. It won’t take much time anyway.” Wind Ancient Source Ancestor also agreed.
With all twelve ancestors in agreement, the assessment for the thirteenth ancestor was opened.
The assessment was very simple: Ye Tian would choose three of the twelve ancestors, and as long as he could hold out for one hour under any one of the twelve ancestors without being obviously at a disadvantage, he would qualify to become the thirteenth ancestor.
Boom!!!!
Within a void space inside the Source God Pavilion.
Ye Tian and the twelve ancestors appeared one after another.
“Endless Ancestor, are you really going to take the thirteenth ancestor assessment?” True River Sword Ancestor asked.
“Yes!”
Ye Tian nodded.
“Then choose three of the twelve ancestors!” True River Sword Ancestor said.
Ye Tian swept his gaze over the twelve ancestors and chose, “I choose Golden Chen Source Ancestor, Ten-Eyed Source Ancestor, and Eight-Faced Source Ancestor!”
The three Half-step Eternal Realm experts he chose were all not Extreme experts. Among the twelve ancestors, they were three of the weaker Source Ancestors, though all still possessed top-tier Half-step Eternal Realm strength, just not too far from the Extreme level.
True River Sword Ancestor and the others were not surprised by Ye Tian’s choice at all. If Ye Tian had chosen Extreme experts to challenge, that would have been strange.
The first to make a move was Golden Chen Source Ancestor. As soon as Golden Chen Source Ancestor attacked, he displayed incomparably terrifying strength, but he did not go all out, fearing that if he killed Ye Tian in one move, that would be far too disrespectful.
But very quickly, his expression changed.
Because Ye Tian’s strength was not weak; he actually took his punch with ease.
“Endless Ancestor, I won’t hold back anymore!”
Golden Chen Source Ancestor unleashed one Eternal technique after another, each strike erupting with his strongest offensive power.
Rumble rumble rumble!!!!
It was as if endless fists had appeared in the infinite void, each one seemingly capable of shattering endless spacetime.
Ye Tian also used one defensive Eternal technique after another to block Golden Chen Source Ancestor’s attacks, and from time to time he would also strike back at Golden Chen Source Ancestor.
But only after exchanging blows with Golden Chen Source Ancestor did Ye Tian truly realize that there was indeed a difference between top-tier Half-step Eternal Realm and top-tier Half-step Eternal Realm. His normal combat strength still was not Golden Chen Source Ancestor’s match.
As one of the Source God Pavilion’s twelve ancestors, naturally none of them were weak.
If he did not use his trump card, he simply could not become the thirteenth ancestor.
With a booming sound!
Ye Tian was sent flying, and Golden Chen Source Ancestor’s voice rang out: “Endless Ancestor, your strength is pretty good. You have reached the level of an ordinary top-tier Half-step Eternal Realm expert, but even so, you still cannot become the thirteenth ancestor. Come challenge again when your cultivation has reached the Ninth Supreme Being Extreme!”
“Golden Chen Source Ancestor, you are indeed very strong, but unfortunately this is not my full strength!”
As Ye Tian spoke, he used the Destruction Finger. .........
Boom!!!!
The aura of the Eternal Realm spread out from Ye Tian’s finger.
“An Eternal Realm aura!” True River Sword Ancestor and the others sensed it too.
In the next instant.
The Destruction Finger was unleashed, carrying the power of an Eternal Realm finger as it erupted forth. With one finger, it crushed the Eternal rules, and with inconceivable force it shattered Golden Chen Source Ancestor’s defense, directly pressing a small hole into Golden Chen Source Ancestor’s body.
Golden Chen Source Ancestor was injured!
“Stop, the assessment is over!”
True River Sword Ancestor shouted.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian stopped attacking and said, “Twelve ancestors, does that mean I’ve passed the assessment?”
“Passed!”
True River Sword Ancestor nodded, but he was still curious about the Eternal Realm aura Ye Tian had released: “Endless Ancestor, may I ask what that Eternal Realm aura from your finger just now was? Was it some kind of special treasure?”
Ye Tian explained, “I fused with a finger segment from an Eternal Realm expert, allowing me to unleash a sliver of Eternal Realm power and erupt with formidable strength, but it is no longer of much help to me now!”
As he spoke, Ye Tian summoned that finger segment.
“It really is a finger segment from an Eternal Realm expert!”
True River Sword Ancestor and the other twelve ancestors were all extremely shocked.
A Ninth Supreme Being dared to fuse with a finger segment from an Eternal Realm expert—his courage was simply too great.
If they knew that Ye Tian had successfully fused with a finger segment from an Eternal Realm expert while only at the Second Supreme Being realm, they would probably be completely dumbfounded.
Although this finger segment was not Ye Tian’s, he had already successfully fused with it and could exert its power, so naturally it counted as part of Ye Tian’s combat strength.
Borrowing outside objects was also strength, and the twelve ancestors of the Source God Pavilion recognized that as well.
At this moment, True River Sword Ancestor announced, “Endless Ancestor, from today onward, you are the thirteenth ancestor of the Source God Pavilion. We will announce it to the public.”
“Mm!”
Ye Tian nodded.


Chapter 1635 Time-Space Territory and the Eternal Realm Lord!

Chapter 1635 Time-Space Territory and the Eternal Realm Lord!

Not long after, the members of the Source God Pavilion all received a transmission, and the Source God Pavilion gave birth to the Thirteenth Ancestor.
And when they learned that the Thirteenth Ancestor was Ye Tian, who was at the ninth level of the Supreme Being realm, all of them were very puzzled, and even dissatisfied. They wondered whether the Twelfth Ancestors had given Ye Tian special treatment on purpose, deliberately making Ye Tian the Source God Pavilion’s Thirteenth Ancestor.
Although the Source God Pavilion was only a loose force, such behavior would still make them very angry.
However, some Half-Step Eternal Realm experts seized the opportunity and felt that if they applied to challenge now, and applied to become the Source God Pavilion’s Fourteenth Ancestor, they might just pass.
Thus, six Half-Step Eternal Realm experts successively applied to become the Source God Pavilion’s Fourteenth Ancestor.
It was obvious that they felt Ye Tian’s strength was weak, and as long as they could hold on in Ye Tian’s hands for one hour, or even defeat Ye Tian, then they could become the Fourteenth Ancestor.
“Interesting. Someone actually thinks the Endless Founding Ancestor is very weak and wants to take this opportunity to apply for the Fourteenth Ancestor!”
True River Sword Ancestor smiled.
However, since these Half-Step Eternal Realm experts had applied, he naturally could not refuse.
So, he approved the applications of these six Half-Step Eternal Realm experts.
……
The first Half-Step Eternal Realm expert arrived.
“Greetings, Thirteenth Ancestor!”
The Half-Step Eternal Realm expert, Eternal Night Source Ancestor, respectfully said.
“Eternal Night Source Ancestor, long ago you applied to challenge the Thirteenth Ancestor. You know the rules, so begin by choosing.” True River Sword Ancestor said.
Eternal Night Source Ancestor smiled faintly and said, “I know I am not a match for the Twelfth Ancestors, and it will be hard for me to hold on for one hour without falling behind. I’ll choose one then, and that is the Thirteenth Ancestor, the Endless Founding Ancestor.”
Anyway, as long as one could hold on for one hour without falling behind in the hands of one Thirteenth Ancestor, one would win, so choosing Ye Tian would be enough; there was no need to choose again.
“The rules are the rules, you must choose!”
True River Sword Ancestor said sternly.
“Fine!”
Eternal Night Source Ancestor casually chose two of the Twelfth Ancestors, and the assessment began.
Eternal Night Source Ancestor was still planning to defeat Ye Tian, dreaming of becoming the Source God Pavilion’s Fourteenth Ancestor.
However, as soon as they exchanged blows, Ye Tian’s Shatter Void Sword completely injured him.
In the blink of an eye, Eternal Night Source Ancestor was already seriously injured.
“I admit defeat!”
Eternal Night Source Ancestor immediately said.
“There are still two more; continue the assessment!”
True River Sword Ancestor said.
However, as soon as the remaining two Twelfth Ancestors took the stage, Eternal Night Source Ancestor immediately conceded defeat. He simply did not want to fight, or rather, did not want to keep making a fool of himself.
He only wanted to leave immediately; otherwise it would be too awkward.
After Eternal Night Source Ancestor left, the other five Half-Step Eternal Realm experts successively underwent the assessment, but all of them were defeated by Ye Tian.
After that, the inner-circle members of the Source God Pavilion all knew that Ye Tian’s strength was greater than theirs, and naturally no longer dared to mock him; they also acknowledged Ye Tian’s status.
Moreover, they also knew very clearly that Ye Tian’s potential in the future would surely surpass the other Twelve Ancestors.
After all, Ye Tian was only at the ninth level of the Supreme Being realm now. If he became a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert, wouldn’t his strength be comparable to Limit existences?
Of course, there were some heaven-defying prodigies who were brilliant from the very start, but ultimately could not break through to the Half-Step Eternal Realm. Such situations also existed.
Thus, if one was not as good as a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert, one could not enter the eyes of those true powerhouses.
This was also why Ye Tian could fight above his level, yet very few people feared him, while the lofty Eternal Realm experts had never even paid attention to him.
-------------------
In the Source God Pavilion’s most core space, inside a spacious room.
The Thirteen Ancestors sat on chairs like ordinary people, gathered around a table covered with all kinds of rare fruit resources.
They chatted while eating, looking nothing like Half-Step Eternal Realm existences at all.
Ye Tian quickly blended into this atmosphere as well; everyone said whatever came to mind.
“Everyone, I have already become the Source God Pavilion’s Thirteenth Ancestor. I wonder if some secrets can be known?” Ye Tian asked.
“Endless Founding Ancestor, ask whatever you want. If we know it, and if it does not involve our own secrets, we will tell you!” True River Sword Ancestor said.
“I’m quite interested in Eternal Realm existences. Why is it that the Eternal Realm is looked down upon in the Source Sea? Could it be that Eternal Realm existences are in areas outside the Source Sea? But the Source Sea seems boundless, and there are no records or legends of other places.”
Ye Tian asked this question.
“Hahaha!!!!” Wind Ancient Source Ancestor laughed and said, “Endless Founding Ancestor, I guessed that you would ask this question too. In fact, many Supreme Being experts, and even some slightly weaker Half-Step Eternal Realm experts, are curious about this. This is not particularly confidential information, so I can tell you.”
“The Source Sea is indeed boundless. Around the Source Sea are the places where the projections of time and space extend. You could say they are places outside the Source Sea, or you could say they are part of the Source Sea. If the Source Sea is compared to a main world, then there are many small worlds around the main world, and although some of these small worlds are not as large as the main world, the resources and cultivation environment they contain are even better than the main world.”
“That’s right. The Source Sea seems to be the origin of everything, but in the dark it is still constrained, which makes it very difficult to change here. The time-space territories surrounding the Source Sea, however, are varied, unlike the Source Sea, which remains eternally unchanged. Those time-space territories may even give birth to all kinds of precious treasure resources, which are beneficial to Eternal Realm cultivation and development. If some time-space territory develops for a long enough time, the number of top experts it gives birth to may even exceed that of the Source Sea. For example, in the Source Sea, Limit existences are relatively rare, but some time-space territories have many Limit existences.”
“Of course, the Source Sea has one advantage: its innate Eternal Rules are complete. Only the Source Sea can truly give birth to Half-Step Eternal Realm experts at the Nine-Extreme level, while time-space territories can at most give birth to Half-Step Eternal Realm experts at the Eight-Extreme level.”
“Thus, the other Eight-Extreme Half-Step Eternal Realm experts in time-space territories may even pay a huge price to enter the Source Sea in order to break through to the Nine-Extreme level. But exactly how many prodigies can truly break through to Nine-Extreme existences, we also are not too sure.”
“Almost all Eternal Realm existences control a time-space territory, and thus they are also called lords. Between the Source Sea and the time-space territories there is a huge Source Sea membrane, which can only be broken by Eternal Realm lords. Therefore, we Half-Step Eternal Realm experts have no way to leave the Source Sea and go to those time-space territories, unless we are Nine-Extreme Half-Step Eternal Realm experts, who can forcibly tear apart the Source Sea membrane to descend upon those time-space territories.”
“Likewise, if Half-Step Eternal Realm experts from the time-space territories want to come over, they also have to ask an Eternal Realm expert for help.”
After the Twelfth Ancestors finished speaking, Ye Tian more or less understood this secret.
“I know that in order to become an Eternal Realm expert, one must fuse with the Eternal Rules. Then why is it that Limit experts have such a hard time breaking through to the Eternal Realm? Logically speaking, shouldn’t it be easier?”
Ye Tian asked this question.
Many Supreme Being experts knew that the stronger a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert was, it did not necessarily mean the greater their hope of breaking through to the Eternal Realm. Many experts who broke through to the Eternal Realm had never even stepped into the Limit.
Thus, he was quite puzzled by this question and still had not figured it out.
At this moment, True River Sword Ancestor and the others sighed.
Wind Ancient Source Ancestor said, “Because of the innate Eternal Rules. Endless Founding Ancestor, you have also comprehended the innate Eternal Rules, haven’t you? We could sense it.”
“Yes. Isn’t comprehending the innate Eternal Rules a good thing? It means one’s control over the rules is deeper!” Ye Tian said.
“No!” True River Sword Ancestor shook his head and explained, “If you only comprehend the Eternal Rules, and have not understood the innate Eternal Rules, then you only need to fuse with the Eternal Rules to advance to the Eternal Realm. But once you accidentally comprehend the innate Eternal Rules, then you can no longer fuse with ordinary Eternal Rules. You must fuse with the innate Eternal Rules before you can advance to the Eternal Realm. This is the real reason why Limit experts have such a hard time breaking through to the Eternal Realm.”
“What? One must fuse with the innate Eternal Rules to advance to the Eternal Realm?”
Ye Tian was learning of such a secret for the first time.
“Endless Founding Ancestor, this secret must not be spread. It is a rule set by the Eternal Realm experts!” True River Sword Ancestor reminded him, fearing that Ye Tian would leak it.
“Why hide this secret?” Ye Tian was puzzled.
True River Sword Ancestor guessed, “There may be two reasons. The first is that they do not want more Eternal Realm experts to be born. Many geniuses originally had a great chance of advancing to the Eternal Realm, but because they did not know this secret and instead comprehended the innate Eternal Rules, the difficulty of breaking through became many times greater. But it may also not be this reason, because although Eternal Realm experts restrict us from spreading it, they have not completely forbidden it, and they did not make us swear an oath. Thus, there is also the possibility of the second reason.”
“The second reason is that Eternal Realm experts also hope to give birth to more Eternal Realm experts who advanced by way of the Limit. Such Eternal Realm experts have greater potential, a higher future, and can step into even higher levels.”
“Endless Founding Ancestor, you have already comprehended the innate Eternal Rules, so you must also advance to the Limit before fusing with the innate Eternal Rules, and only then can you advance to the Eternal Realm.”
Ye Tian suddenly understood. In his heart, he was not panicking at all; he was very confident in himself and believed that he could certainly fuse with the innate Eternal Rules and thus advance to the Eternal Realm.
Next, Ye Tian chatted continuously with the other Twelve Ancestors, learning more and more secrets.
Suddenly.
True River Sword Ancestor suggested, “In some time, the Wuhen Territory will open, and we are preparing to go there again this time.”.


Chapter 1636 The Three Great Opportunities of the Homeless Domain!

Chapter 1636 The Three Great Opportunities of the Homeless Domain!

“The Homeless Domain—is it perhaps a temporal-spatial Domain? Aren’t we unable to enter temporal-spatial Domains?”
Ye Tian raised his doubt.
True River Sword Ancestor explained, “The Homeless Domain is indeed a temporal-spatial Domain, but it is a shattered temporal-spatial Domain. The temporal-spatial ruler has also been shattered and thus embedded in the source sea. Just like fragments of a small world embedded in the main world, there will be a passage that allows one to enter it.”
After hearing this, Ye Tian fully understood.
Then, Ye Tian came to understand the value of the Homeless Domain.
The Homeless Domain had once been the temporal-spatial Domain of the Homeless Ruler, but unfortunately, the Homeless Ruler had fallen. As for how he fell, even True River Sword Ancestor and the others did not know.
However, a huge fragment of the Homeless Domain is now embedded in the source sea and has completely become part of the source sea, which is why these half-step Eternal Realm experts can enter it.
Of course, the Homeless Domain is also extremely dangerous. Within it exists a very terrifying creature—the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python, perhaps once a pet raised and studied by the Homeless Ruler.
But now that the Homeless Ruler has fallen, the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python is no longer under control, yet it still persists in fulfilling its mission of guarding the Homeless Domain. Once anyone enters the Homeless Domain, they will be attacked by the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python.
And the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python is incredibly powerful, basically all of them are half-step Eternal Realm, and the strongest among them can even rival half-step Eternal Realm experts at the Extreme level.
Therefore, Supreme Beings are simply not suited to enter the Homeless Domain; entering means death.
According to information revealed by the other twelve ancestors, the Homeless Domain has three great opportunities.
The first opportunity is the Boundless Sea. The Boundless Sea within the Homeless Domain gives birth to many rare resources, but there is also the main base of the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python. Without absolutely formidable strength, entering there is courting death.
The second opportunity is Rift Wind Valley. This valley can be said to be a place for cultivation, or it can also be said to be a marvel.
Rift Wind Valley constantly blows a strange wind, and this strange wind can affect the will of half-step Eternal Realm experts.
The soul and body of a half-step Eternal Realm expert have fused, but that does not mean they have no will. Will still exists, and it has a great influence.
If one’s will is strong, one can hold fast to one’s original heart, which is of great benefit to breakthroughs, and can even provide some help in breaking through bottlenecks.
Moreover, the will of half-step Eternal Realm experts is already very strong, so tempering it is extremely difficult, yet Rift Wind Valley can help temper the will.
Furthermore, there are no Temporal-Spatial Dragon Pythons in Rift Wind Valley; the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Pythons do not like to go there.
Therefore, Rift Wind Valley is the safest and easiest opportunity to enter, but raising one’s will requires a very long period of time.
More importantly, even half-step Eternal Realm experts find it difficult to stay in Rift Wind Valley for long. Once too much time passes, Rift Wind Valley will cause the will to shatter, and the body will collapse as a result.
Moreover, Rift Wind Valley can only be entered at specific times; at other times, it simply cannot be entered, and no half-step Eternal Realm expert would remain in the Homeless Domain all the time, as that would be far too dangerous.
So those half-step Eternal Realm experts would only stay in Rift Wind Valley for a period of time before leaving.
Ye Tian quietly remembered this place, Rift Wind Valley.
The third opportunity is Homeless Mountain. This was once the residence of the Homeless Ruler. Although it was left in a shattered state after a great battle, many good things still remained, which is why Homeless Mountain is also the greatest opportunity in the Homeless Domain and the place that many half-step Eternal Realm experts all want to enter.
The day the Homeless Domain opens will be three kalpa epochs from now, so the thirteen ancestors agreed to enter the Homeless Domain together after three kalpa epochs.
As for the other inner-circle members, they are not qualified to enter it; even the other half-step Eternal Realm experts among the inner-circle members are not qualified to enter.
This kind of opportunity is a shared opportunity exclusive to the thirteen ancestors. If Ye Tian had not become one of the thirteen ancestors, he would also not have been qualified to enter it.
Of course, if Ye Tian later discovered similar opportunities, he could also tell True River Sword Ancestor and the others, sharing some of the opportunities. This was also one of the purposes for founding the Source God Pavilion.
In the blink of an eye, three kalpa epochs passed.
On this day, the thirteen ancestors gathered at the Source God Pavilion.
“Let’s go!”
The Source God Pavilion teleported the thirteen ancestors, crossing a vast distance and directly arriving at a relatively remote region.
Very soon, the thirteen ancestors arrived at a place, and here several half-step Eternal Realm experts were hidden.
“True River Sword Ancestor, your Source God Pavilion actually brought a Ninth Supreme Being. What kind of background does this Ninth Supreme Being have?” a half-step Eternal Realm expert appeared and asked curiously.
“Rift Wind Source Ancestor, this is the thirteenth ancestor of our Source God Pavilion, Endless Primordial Ancestor.” True River Sword Ancestor casually said a sentence, and then did not say much more; moreover, his tone toward Rift Wind Source Ancestor was not very good.
It could be seen that the relationship between True River Sword Ancestor and Rift Wind Source Ancestor was not good.
At this moment, Wind Ancient Source Ancestor sent a message to Ye Tian, saying: “Rift Wind Source Ancestor is also one of the Extreme-level experts of the source sea, but his relationship with True River Sword Ancestor is not very good. The reason is that he once took away an opportunity that belonged to True River Sword Ancestor. You should be a bit careful of Rift Wind Source Ancestor in the future, but don’t worry too much. He is also only at the first Extreme level, just a little stronger than you.”
Ye Tian nodded and said nothing.
Very soon, one half-step Eternal Realm expert after another arrived, and here gathered as many as several hundred half-step Eternal Realm experts.
“It’s starting!”
The rules of the Homeless Domain and the rules of the source sea collided, and a gap began to tear open.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!!
One half-step Eternal Realm expert after another charged into the fissure and entered the Homeless Domain.
Ye Tian, together with True River Sword Ancestor and the others, also charged into the Homeless Domain.
Upon entering the Homeless Domain, bursts of roaring sounds came from all directions.
These sounds were unmistakably those of the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python!
Boom!!!!
One Temporal-Spatial Dragon Python after another that stretched across the sky came threading through the void, each one unimaginably huge and exuding a terrifying aura.
“Kill!”
One half-step Eternal Realm expert after another took action and began battling the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Pythons, but their purpose was not to kill them; it was to escape from here.
Some half-step Eternal Realm experts charged toward Rift Wind Valley, where it was relatively safe and the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Pythons would not go.
Some others did not want to go to Rift Wind Valley and instead went to Homeless Mountain. Although the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Pythons could also force their way into Homeless Mountain, there were certain places in Homeless Mountain that the Temporal-Spatial Dragon Pythons could not enter.
As for the Boundless Sea, no one dared to go there.
Of course, there were even fewer half-step Eternal Realm experts wandering around aimlessly.
True River Sword Ancestor and Wind Ancient Source Ancestor directly chose Homeless Mountain, while Ye Tian chose Rift Wind Valley.
He planned to first experience the will enhancement brought by this opportunity in Rift Wind Valley; as for Homeless Mountain, it would not be too late to go there a bit later.


Chapter 1637: The Will Impact of Rift Wind Valley!

Chapter 1637: The Will Impact of Rift Wind Valley!

Ye Tian possessed the map of the Seamless Domain, and his own strength was not weak either. Moreover, there were also some half-step Eternal Realm experts heading to Rift Wind Valley, so the pressure on him was not very great.
Very quickly, he broke out of the encirclement of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons and arrived at Rift Wind Valley.
As soon as he entered Rift Wind Valley, a gust of wind blew over.
The Space-Time Dragon Pythons did not dare approach Rift Wind Valley one by one. They all retreated, or lingered outside Rift Wind Valley, but simply refused to go in.
Ye Tian also sensed the strangeness of Rift Wind Valley.
Boom!!!!!!
Waves of gentle breeze swept over and blew onto Ye Tian's will, as if his will were enduring endless pounding. This feeling was extremely painful.
Moreover, the longer the gentle breeze blew, the stronger the impact on his will became.
This was only the outer area of Rift Wind Valley. If it were the inner area, the impact would probably be even more severe.
Inside Rift Wind Valley, one had to withstand will impact; outside Rift Wind Valley, one had to endure the siege of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons.
Therefore, no one dared to stay here for too long. Otherwise, their will would be severely injured, their strength would greatly decline, and they might even find it difficult to resist the attacks of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons.
Ye Tian walked step by step toward the depths of Rift Wind Valley, feeling the will impact brought by the gentle breeze, and actually quietly enjoyed it.
“Compared with other Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm experts, I have hardly encountered any major setbacks. Although my willpower is not weak, compared with those half-step Eternal Realm experts, it is still somewhat lacking. Perhaps Rift Wind Valley can make up for the deficiency in my will!” Ye Tian muttered.
Very quickly, he arrived at a relatively suitable location, sat down cross-legged, and silently endured the impact on his will.
At the same time, he let the copied body begin copying out another body to serve as a clone.
Whoosh!
Another Ye Tian appeared.
Ye Tian let the other Ye Tian go to Seamless Mountain. He also did not want to waste the opportunities in Seamless Mountain, so one copied body tempered his will in Rift Wind Valley while one clone went to seek opportunities, without delaying anything at all.
Whoosh!
The clone moved, breaking out of Rift Wind Valley, and then entering the encirclement of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons.
Although Ye Tian's strength was not very great, in terms of life-saving ability, he was even more formidable than Zhenhe Sword Ancestor and the others.
After becoming a nine-realm Supreme Being, his life-saving ability was almost comparable to Star Ancestor's, perhaps even a bit stronger. There were too few half-step Eternal Realm existences who could kill him.
Back then, Star Ancestor was sealed by a half-step Eternal Realm expert, and that half-step Eternal Realm expert was also one of the top half-step Eternal Realm experts, not far from the Extreme realm. No matter what method the other side used, they could not kill Star Ancestor, and could only seal him.
Therefore, even if ten Extreme experts surrounded and killed Ye Tian together, it would still be very difficult to kill him.
Unless a seven-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm expert like Wuji Ice Ancestor made a move against him, there would be hope of killing him, and it would take quite some time.
So Ye Tian was not afraid at all of being surrounded and killed by the Space-Time Dragon Pythons.
After a round of fighting, Ye Tian finally reached Seamless Mountain.
Seamless Mountain was very large. Though called a mountain, it was actually a mountain range. Many blessed lands and buildings stood here.
Ye Tian did not hesitate at all and directly rushed toward one of the mountain peaks.
The Twelve Ancestors had revealed one piece of information: there was a place on Seamless Mountain that was extremely suitable for nine-realm Supreme Beings, where one could rapidly increase one's cultivation.
This was East Return Mountain on Seamless Mountain. On East Return Mountain, there was a special array that could combine the power of this space-time territory and convert various energies into a special kind of energy.
This energy was called Seamless Liquid. Seamless Liquid could not be preserved in the outside world for very long, so it could not be taken away and had to be refined promptly.
Seamless Liquid was likely a special energy once developed by the Seamless Domain, extremely easy to absorb and refine, surpassing any kind of energy in the Source Sea, and even worth far more than many priceless treasures that could raise one's cultivation.
If one refined Seamless Liquid, cultivation could be raised in a short time, though it would not help half-step Eternal Realm experts much.
But for nine-realm Supreme Beings, the help was immense.
That was why Ye Tian came to East Return Mountain.
After entering East Return Mountain, Ye Tian discovered that he was the only one here; the other half-step Eternal Realm experts had not come.
Very quickly, Ye Tian arrived at a rather ruined great hall. This was East Return Hall.
Although the great hall was in utter disrepair, the array could still be used.
Ye Tian activated the array here, then took out countless resources and materials.
This array could not produce Seamless Liquid out of thin air; Ye Tian had to provide the resources himself.
When countless resources surged into the core of the great array, the array began to convert energy.
As time slowly passed, a droplet of green water began to appear in the void; this green droplet was Seamless Liquid.
Ye Tian swallowed Seamless Liquid in one gulp and began refining it.
Boom!!!!
The energy of Seamless Liquid erupted, rapidly merging into Ye Tian's body, helping him temper his body and raise his cultivation.
“Such a powerful effect, pity this is not my true body. Even if the copied body increases its cultivation, it cannot feed back to the true body!”
Ye Tian muttered.
He knew full well that raising the copied body's cultivation would not help much, but he still came here. Mainly because his current strength was too weak, and he had to raise his cultivation a bit before he could obtain good things on Seamless Mountain.
Of course, his true body could also come here, but Ye Tian was unwilling to take the risk.
After all, the opportunities in the Seamless Domain had not yet reached the point where he needed to gamble his life. Besides, if he wanted to reach the Extreme of nine-realm Supreme Beings, it would just take a bit more time.
So he did not care too much.
After a long while, Ye Tian's cultivation increased greatly, and his body also became much stronger. Although he was still some distance away from the Extreme of nine-realm Supreme Beings, his ordinary combat strength was probably enough to match Gold Chen Source Ancestor among the Twelve Ancestors.
“About enough. It's time to go to another place on Seamless Mountain.”
Ye Tian muttered.
Whoosh!
His body disappeared from East Return Mountain, and very soon he arrived at Seamless Tower on Seamless Mountain.
Seamless Tower was a test tower once built by the Seamless Domain Lord for disciples or servants. The tower had nine levels, and for every level passed, one could obtain the corresponding reward.
Now, although the Seamless Domain Lord had fallen, Seamless Tower still remained, and there were still some rewards inside.
At this moment.
Outside Seamless Tower, strands of Space-Time Dragon Pythons were shuttling back and forth.
After Ye Tian arrived here, he forcibly charged into Seamless Tower and came to the hall inside it.
Here, he saw a few familiar faces.
“Zhenhe Sword Ancestor, Fenggu Source Ancestor, you're here too!”
Ye Tian greeted them.
“Endless Ancestor, you've come too!”
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor and Fenggu Source Ancestor said with a smile.


Chapter 1638 Secret Art: World of Will!

Chapter 1638 Secret Art: World of Will!【Please complete the full subscription】

“True River Sword Ancestor, have you all challenged the Wuhen Tower?”
Ye Tian asked curiously.
“We already did!” True River Sword Ancestor said. “I only made it through the fifth level, the same as last time, so there wasn’t much reward. We’re waiting for Qingxu Source Ancestor. Last time he only made it through the fourth level, but this time he broke through to the Extreme, so he should be able to pass the fifth level. The reward for the fifth level is still quite good.”
Ye Tian did not wait for Qingxu Source Ancestor. He directly went to challenge the first level of the Wuhen Tower.
The first level of the Wuhen Tower was very easy to pass. As long as one’s strength among the Ninefold Supreme Beings was at the top, there was a certain chance of passing the first level.
Inside the first level.
A spatiotemporal dragon python actually appeared.
“It’s not a real spatiotemporal dragon python, it’s a spatiotemporal dragon python condensed by a formation!”
Ye Tian recognized it at once.
Boom!
Ye Tian threw a punch and directly blasted the spatiotemporal dragon python apart.
Just like that, the first level was passed!
After passing the first level, Ye Tian obtained a reward.
“Dragon Whisk Sacred Stone!”
This reward was not cheap. After refining the Dragon Whisk Sacred Stone, it could be worn on the body to temper the physique at all times. It was of little help to Ninefold Supreme Beings, but for those Supreme Beings with lower cultivation, the value of the Dragon Whisk Sacred Stone was precious indeed.
Originally, Ye Tian would not have recognized the Dragon Whisk Sacred Stone, but after becoming the thirteenth ancestor of the Source God Pavilion, he naturally obtained a list of treasures from the twelfth ancestor, which included treasures born within the Time Domain. And there was no Dragon Whisk Sacred Stone in the Source Sea; it was born in the Time Domain.
“The Dragon Whisk Sacred Stone isn’t of much help to me, but I can give it to Yue’er!” Ye Tian thought.
After that, Ye Tian went to challenge the second level of the Wuhen Tower, and the result was still an easy pass.
The requirement corresponding to the second level was half-step Eternal Realm. If one had only the strength of an ordinary half-step Eternal Realm, they could not even enter the second level.
The third level corresponded to the strength of a powerful half-step Eternal Realm.
The fourth level corresponded to the strength of a top-tier half-step Eternal Realm.
The fifth level required the strength of the Extreme.
Ye Tian challenged the Wuhen Tower level by level and quickly passed the fourth level, and the reward he obtained was not low. In particular, the reward after passing the fourth level was actually a Void God Leaf.
The Void God Leaf was a lifesaving treasure. It could instantly pierce through void and escape with one’s life. It could also conceal aura and block any probing power. Even a Ninefold Supreme Being, once using the Void God Leaf, could escape pursuit from an Extreme level powerhouse.
Of course, for Eternal Realm beings, the Void God Leaf was of no use.
But even so, in the Source Sea, the Void God Leaf was enough to rank among the top ten lifesaving treasures. It could not be traded at all, because it could only be used at most three times. Thus it was too rare and too scarce; no one would be foolish enough to take it out for trade.
After passing the fourth level, Ye Tian actually obtained the Void God Leaf, and his luck was definitely not bad.
Afterwards.
Ye Tian arrived at the fifth level of the Wuhen Tower.
The fifth level required Extreme strength to pass. Ye Tian had not brought an Eternal Realm finger into the Wuhen Domain, so originally he would have been unable to pass here.
But he had first gone to Donghui Mountain and increased his strength.
Now, his strength had surged, and he was almost at the Extreme. Coupled with the lifesaving ability of the Endless Eternal Body, he should have some hope of passing the fifth level.
Even True River Sword Ancestor felt that the reward for the fifth level was extremely precious, so it was certainly very good. Thus, of course he wanted to pass the fifth level.
Very soon, the fifth level was reached!
Boom!!!!!
A spatiotemporal dragon python comparable to a First Extreme appeared.
Perhaps its true combat strength was a bit weaker than a First Extreme, but it was definitely not much weaker.
For a half-step Eternal Realm powerhouse at the First Extreme level, passing the fifth level would probably require a very long time, perhaps even a protracted battle lasting ages.
Ye Tian knew very clearly that he could not kill this spatiotemporal dragon python in a short time at all.
“Then I’ll wear it down to death!”
Ye Tian decided.
Rumble!!!!!
The battle between Ye Tian and this spatiotemporal dragon python began.
As soon as they exchanged blows, Ye Tian was slightly at a disadvantage, but he barely held on and did not suffer any injuries.
Time slowly passed. Relying on the Endless Eternal Body, Ye Tian forcibly dragged out the battle, while from time to time he would land a blow on the spatiotemporal dragon python, inflicting some injuries upon it.
And although the spatiotemporal dragon python could also injure Ye Tian, Ye Tian’s recovery ability was too terrifying, and he recovered almost instantly.
Time slowly passed. Although Ye Tian’s consumption was great, he also absorbed resources from his inner world to recover energy. This did not count as cheating, and the Wuhen Tower would not care.
No one knew how much time had passed before Ye Tian finally wore this spatiotemporal dragon python down to death and passed the fifth level.
By this time, the injuries on this clone body of Ye Tian were also relatively light. After a while, all of the injuries recovered.
This time, Ye Tian seemed to have passed the fifth level without paying much of a price.
But he knew very clearly that if he had not improved his cultivation and strengthened his power, he probably would not even have been able to injure the spatiotemporal dragon python. If he could not injure it, then no matter how long the battle dragged on, he still would not be able to kill it.
· ·········求鮮花··· ·····
Obviously, the decision he made earlier was very correct.
After passing the fifth level, the reward from the Wuhen Tower also appeared.
Whoosh!
A treasure appeared before him.
It was a legacy orb!
“Inheritance!”
Ye Tian was somewhat looking forward to it. What exactly was the inheritance from an Eternal Realm lord?
If it were an ordinary inheritance, he would not be interested, but what if it could help him?
Ye Tian directly accepted the inheritance. Very soon, the inheritance ended, and the legacy orb also shattered directly. Clearly, it was a one-time legacy orb. If it were a legacy orb that could inherit continuously, then its value would be enough for a force to rise completely.
But the more advanced the inheritance, the more troublesome it was to create, and it could even not be tolerated by heaven and earth, so naturally it could not be inherited too many times. This was a limitation.
.... ....... .......
“World of Will!”
This was an inherited secret art, a secret art that helped increase willpower.
“Looks like the Wuhen Lord had a deep study of willpower. Not only does his domain have the Rift Wind Valley that tempers willpower, he also created this World of Will secret art!”
Ye Tian thought.
But after reading this World of Will secret art, he felt that the Wuhen Lord was a madman.
Willpower transformed into a world, forming countless billions upon countless billions of worlds of will throughout the body. When willpower becomes strong enough, it can even allow the body to erupt with explosive power and combat strength that surpasses the limit.
Even more, willpower can affect innate Eternal rules.
Once the World of Will reaches the ninth level, willpower can directly shatter innate Eternal rules and shatter the fleshly body of an Eternal Realm being.
But this was an incomplete secret art, and every step of cultivation was extremely dangerous.
More importantly, willpower was far too difficult to increase. It was almost impossible to reach the ninth level of the World of Will; this was a secret art conceived by the Wuhen Lord.
Moreover, ordinary avatars simply could not cultivate the World of Will, because an avatar is not the true body. It does not possess some of the abilities the true body has, nor can it bear the World of Will.
But who would dare use the true body for experimentation?
“Could it be that the Wuhen Lord had many people cultivate the World of Will, using them as experiments, causing many deaths, and even capturing many geniuses, ultimately enraging some powerful Eternal Realm being, and finally being killed.”
Ye Tian guessed.
Then he smiled.
This secret art was very suitable for him!
His clone body was no different from his true body, so he could use the clone body to cultivate the World of Will. Even if it collapsed, nothing would happen.


Chapter 1639 The Forbidden Stele That Disappointed Ye Tian!

Chapter 1639 The Forbidden Stele That Disappointed Ye Tian!

For Ye Tian, obtaining the secret art of the world of will this time was the greatest gain, even more precious than all kinds of rare resources.
Ye Tian did not challenge the sixth tier. To pass the sixth tier, even the strength of a second-tier half-step Eternal Realm was not enough; it probably required a third-tier one.
Therefore, Ye Tian gave up challenging the sixth tier and came out directly.
When he came out, True River Sword Ancestor and the others were already no longer here; clearly, they had left.
Mistless Mountain was not limited to East Return Mountain and the Mistless Pagoda as places of opportunity; there were also other blessed places. Therefore, True River Sword Ancestor and the others did not want to waste time.
Very soon, Ye Tian arrived at another blessed place on Mistless Mountain—the Forbidden Stele!
The Forbidden Stele was the greatest opportunity on Mistless Mountain. Comprehending the Forbidden Stele did not improve one’s control over the Eternal Law or the Innate Eternal Law, but instead allowed one to comprehend the mysteries of the fusion between the body and the Innate Eternal Law.
The fusion of the body with the Innate Eternal Law was too difficult. Many peak half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses could not even figure out the direction, but the Forbidden Stele could offer some help.
Of course, this so-called help could only raise the success rate by less than one percent, but that was still quite good.
If there were more such opportunities, would that not mean there would be hope of advancing to the Eternal Realm?
Therefore, the Forbidden Stele was extremely precious to half-step Eternal Realm cultivators, unfortunately they could not take it away.
As for Eternal Realm cultivators, they likely looked down on the Forbidden Stele, or perhaps they could not take it away either, which was why the Forbidden Stele had always remained on Mistless Mountain in the Mistless Territory.
The Forbidden Stele was located at the summit of Forbidden Peak on Mistless Mountain, where there were many Space-Time Dragon Pythons.
At this moment.
One after another, half-step Eternal Realm cultivators set up formations to resist the attacks of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons, allowing the other half-step Eternal Realm cultivators to peacefully comprehend the Forbidden Stele. Everyone worked together to comprehend it.
“They’re actually collaborating to comprehend the Forbidden Stele!”
Ye Tian had not expected these half-step Eternal Realm beings to cooperate. But when he thought about it, if they did not cooperate, they would simply be unable to comprehend it in peace. The Forbidden Stele did not prohibit Space-Time Dragon Pythons from approaching, so without anyone to protect them, comprehending it alone would be courting death.
After that.
Ye Tian also joined in, but since he had joined later, he naturally was not qualified to comprehend the Forbidden Stele immediately; he had to wait for the next batch.
After a long while, it was finally Ye Tian’s group of powerhouses’ turn to comprehend the Forbidden Stele.
The Forbidden Stele was not very large, only about a hundred meters tall. It was purple in color, surrounded by special purple halos, and within the range of the halo, one could use the Forbidden Stele to comprehend the mysteries of the fusion between the body and the Innate Eternal Law.
At this moment.
Many half-step Eternal Realm cultivators took out various resources to assist their comprehension, helping themselves comprehend quickly.
However, this clone of Ye Tian did not bring much in the way of resources, so he could only rely on himself.
Boom!!!!
In his perception, strands of Innate Eternal Law continually evolved and slowly merged with life, demonstrating the process of the fusion of various forms of life with the Innate Eternal Law.
