Very soon, one lifeform after another collapsed and perished during the fusion; the fusion attempts of billions upon billions of lives all ended in failure, but a few lives successfully fused and advanced into the Eternal Realm.
“The Forbidden Stele is actually showing the fusion process in a special way, allowing half-step Eternal Realm cultivators to comprehend it!”
Ye Tian finally understood why the Forbidden Stele had the effect of assisting fusion.
Just by watching this, even a fool could gain something!
However, this straightforward method was indeed effective, and very useful.
Ye Tian also quickly became immersed in his comprehension, even placing himself into the situation, though unfortunately these lives fusing with the Innate Eternal Law were not using their own bodies as experimental subjects.
And everyone’s body was different; the Innate Eternal Law each comprehended was also different, and the methods and difficulty of fusion were different as well.
Therefore, these examples of fusion could not be fully combined; they could only provide some limited gain.
Of course.
The Forbidden Stele still allowed half-step Eternal Realm cultivators to gain a deeper understanding and insight into their own Eternal Law or Innate Eternal Law, and that was also one of its benefits.
“Too bad it isn’t of much help to me!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
He would be better off using cloned bodies in the future to repeatedly attempt fusion, finding experience through countless failures; that would definitely be more useful than comprehending the Forbidden Stele.
But other half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses did not have methods like his, so naturally they could not do that. They could only rely on treasures like the Forbidden Stele, seeking hope again and again.
After comprehending it for some time, Ye Tian gave up on the Forbidden Stele and chose to leave.
Afterward, at various blessed places on Mistless Mountain, he also gained some things.
For example, in one place on Mistless Mountain there were traces of an Eternal Realm battle; those traces still remained, and one could still feel the profound mysteries of Eternal Realm techniques.
Another example was the rows of stone statues on Mistless Mountain. These stone statues contained some inheritances, and if one carefully comprehended them, one could still gain some Eternal techniques.
However, this was only helpful to ordinary half-step Eternal Realm cultivators. Those ordinary half-step Eternal Realm cultivators had not comprehended any Eternal techniques before, which was why they wanted to obtain some Eternal technique inheritances and use other Eternal techniques to create their own.
But Ye Tian already possessed a large number of Eternal techniques, so he looked down on such inheritances.
One blessed place after another was rather disappointing to Ye Tian.
It had to be said that his vision was now higher, and he no longer looked favorably upon the benefits here.
“Mistless Territory was discovered long ago. I don’t know how many half-step Eternal Realm cultivators have entered here; the benefits that can be left behind are too few........”
Ye Tian thought.
But this time, his greatest gains still came from the Rift Wind Valley and the world of will; next were treasures like the Void God Leaf.
After some more time passed, True River Sword Ancestor and the others invited Ye Tian to go to certain territories of the Mistless Territory to collect resources. As long as they could withstand the attacks of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons, they could seize some of the resources that were born here.
As long as they did not go to Endless Sea, there was actually still a great chance of surviving.
But there would definitely be powerhouses who went to Endless Sea, such as those half-step Eternal Realm cultivators of the fifth and sixth tiers. They probably would join forces to force their way into Endless Sea and seize those extremely precious resources.
Ye Tian rejected True River Sword Ancestor’s suggestion; he had no interest in this now.
At this moment.
Ye Tian was trying to cultivate the world of will in Rift Wind Valley, and his clone had also returned here.
In fact, clones and copy bodies both possessed the Copying Talent. Even if one of them fell, the Copying Talent could copy another one again.
Therefore, he could continuously try to cultivate the world of will without fear of falling.
And the environment of Rift Wind Valley was perfectly suited to the world of will; it was the best place.
The wind of Rift Wind Valley tempered the will, while the world of will strengthened the will. The two combined perfectly, but without many lives to spare, even the Mistless Territory Lord would not dare to cultivate so crazily—yet Ye Tian did.
On this day.
When Ye Tian was cultivating the world of will, a problem arose with his will, causing a problem with his body.
Coupled with the wind of Rift Wind Valley blowing over, his will collapsed and his flesh began to disintegrate.
Instantly, this clone dissipated.
“The clone has fallen; copy another one!”
Ye Tian accelerated time, and very soon he could condense another body and begin cultivating again.
No one knew how long had passed when True River Sword Ancestor sent a transmission.
“Endless Ancestor, the entrance is about to close. We have to leave!”
Ye Tian immediately replied to him: “True River Sword Ancestor, what I entered with was a clone, and I didn’t bring any treasures. I’m not planning to leave. I intend to cultivate here for a few more days!”
True River Sword Ancestor did not try to persuade Ye Tian anymore; he guessed that Ye Tian was cultivating in Rift Wind Valley.
But if one cultivated for too long, the clone would not be able to hold on and would still have to come out. Once it came out, it would have to withstand the attacks of the Space-Time Dragon Pythons, and still would not survive.
Therefore, doing this would only let him stay a few more days; it was of little use.
However, he also knew that Ye Tian was only a clone, so the loss was not great, and thus he did not try to persuade him.
Very soon, one after another half-step Eternal Realm cultivators left the Mistless Territory, leaving only Ye Tian behind.


Chapter 1640: Will World, Second Stage!

Chapter 1640: Will World, Second Stage!

Only one person remained in Wuhen Territory.
However, before the entrance of Wuhen Territory disappeared, Ye Tian still sent his clone out for a trip, letting his main body take away some of the treasures carried by the clone.
For example, the Void God Leaf; this item was relatively valuable and could not be lost.
Afterward, the clone self-Annihilated, and the copied body recondensed again in Wuhen Territory.
In this way, Ye Tian could boldly and confidently use Split Wind Valley to cultivate the Will World.
His copied body was at the very edge of Split Wind Valley, where the will impact was the weakest, so the copied body could endure for a very long time without needing to leave Split Wind Valley.
Meanwhile, his clone was within the inner region of Split Wind Valley, enduring the intense will impact, crazily tempering its own will, and cultivating in coordination with the Will World.
Just like that, with the clone collapsing again and again and cultivating again and again, Ye Tian came to understand the Will World more and more.
Will was unlike cultivation; as the will of the copied body and the clone increased, Ye Tian's main body's will would also increase. This was much like accumulating experience and comprehension.
As the clone collapsed time and time again, his will still kept improving, and he also gradually gained a deeper comprehension of this secret art, the Will World, combining it with Ye Tian's own situation to turn it into a secret art belonging to Ye Tian, while steadily perfecting it step by step.
He would not safely and directly cultivate according to Wuhen Territory Lord's secret art method; that would easily lead to collapse. He had to improve it himself and adapt it to his own body before it could become a truly powerful will secret art.
On this day.
The Will World had made new progress, and he was preparing to open up a Will World.
Once a Will World was opened up, it meant that the Will World secret art had reached the first Stage.
Ye Tian continuously condensed will through the Will World secret art, opening up a Will World inside a certain cell of his body. The Will World was not a real world, so even a single cell could bear it.
“Will World, open!”
In the unknown layer of the cell, a Will World was forcibly opened up, and endless will manifested there in tangible form.
At the same time, Ye Tian had complete control over this cell and could erupt with terrifying power.
Moreover, he could use this cell as the core and radiate it throughout his entire body, thereby allowing his body to erupt with far more power than usual.
More importantly, once the Will World was opened up, it could slowly strengthen his will, which was also one channel for will improvement.
One could imagine how fast the will improvement speed would be, and how powerful the will would become, once large numbers of Will Worlds were opened up.
It had to be said that the Will World secret art created by Wuhen Territory Lord was indeed terrifying; it was just a pity that even he himself did not dare cultivate it.
The clone successfully opened up a Will World, but the main body naturally could not automatically open up a Will World.
Thus.
Ye Tian's main body also needed to open up a Will World, and since this process had already been improved, there would be no danger.
Ye Tian then began opening up a Will World inside the Void Source Hall.
Very soon, the main body successfully opened up a Will World.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian's clone stayed in Split Wind Valley. Because a Will World had been opened and his will strengthened, he could remain in Split Wind Valley for a longer time.
Moreover, Ye Tian could go deeper into Split Wind Valley.
Just like that, another period of time passed.
On this day, Ye Tian began to open up the second Will World.
Unfortunately, the opening of the second Will World failed.
Ye Tian quickly found the reason: it was influenced by the first Will World. The first Will World radiated throughout the entire body, and under its influence, if the second Will World were opened in the same way as the first, it would inevitably fail.
The failure to open up the Will World directly dealt a severe blow to Ye Tian's will.
Helplessly, Ye Tian self-Annihilated this clone and then recondensed another one, which was more convenient than slowly recovering his will.
In the years that followed, Ye Tian continuously studied how to create a second Will World and discovered that this had a great deal to do with the chosen cell position.
It could be said that the cell position chosen for each subsequent Will World had to follow a certain pattern in order to avoid interference.
After many attempts, Ye Tian finally found the proper position and opened up the second Will World.
After the second Will World was successfully opened, Ye Tian's main body began to open up the second Will World as well, succeeding in one go without any problems.
Unknowingly, Ye Tian's copied body and clone had stayed in Split Wind Valley for several tribulation eras.
Such a long span of years, with Ye Tian's clone still existing there, would probably be unimaginable in the eyes of people like True River Sword Ancestor and the others, yet no one knew about it.
By now, Ye Tian had already opened more than three hundred Will Worlds.
If he opened one thousand Will Worlds, that would be equivalent to stepping into the second Stage of the Will World secret art.
“According to the introduction of the Will World secret art, once the Will World reaches the second Stage, the will will undergo a transformation!” Ye Tian was not sure whether this was true, but he very much wanted to raise the Will World to the second Stage.
Now, his understanding of the Will World secret art was deepening more and more, and the speed at which he opened up Will Worlds was also getting faster and faster.
Moreover, his clone had already reached the core area of Split Wind Valley.
Few half-step Eternal Realm experts dared to come here; otherwise, their will would be blasted into collapse by the impact.
Ye Tian knew very well that, with his current level of will, he originally would not have been able to reach this place. But more than three hundred Will Worlds radiating through his body had made his resistance to will impact terrifyingly strong, allowing him to come here.
On this day.
Ye Tian truly walked to the most core area of Split Wind Valley, where he saw a huge rock.
This huge rock was gray in color, covered with densely packed patterns that were not engraved onto it, but naturally formed.
“The will impact in Split Wind Valley should be emanating from this rock. In other words, this rock created the anomaly of Split Wind Valley!”
Ye Tian said in surprise.
He wanted to take this rock away, but found that he could not move it.
Clearly, Wuhen Territory Lord had also placed a restriction on this rock, perfectly fusing it with Wuhen Territory so that it could not be taken away.
Afterwards.
Ye Tian sat cross-legged on this will rock, enduring the impact of will while cultivating the Will World.
Unknowingly, another five tribulation eras passed.
At this time, the number of Ye Tian's Will Worlds had reached 999; just one last one remained before he could reach the second Stage of the Will World and trigger a transformation of will.
Boom!!!!
The 1000th Will World was born!
Ye Tian's will began to undergo a qualitative change, as though it had stepped into an entirely new tier.
At this moment.
The countless cells in Ye Tian's body all resonated with the transformation of his will, and his body radiated endless will light, illuminating the surrounding void.
After a long while, the transformation of will came to an end.
“My will has increased tenfold!”
Ye Tian said in shock.
Before, the improvement of his will had been very, very slow, but this time the increase was too terrifying!
Moreover, his will had become even more tenacious.
In addition, Ye Tian discovered that when he infused his will into his fist or weapon, it became incomparably sharp and could easily tear apart the body of a half-step Eternal Realm expert.
Of course, this was tested with Ye Tian's copied body.
Moreover, will could also enhance his defense.
“After will reaches the second Stage, it is actually this terrifying. Perhaps the will of Eternal Realm existences is also like this! Second Stage will should be equivalent to the will of an Eternal Realm existence!”
Ye Tian speculated.
In short, after the transformation of his will reached the second Stage, his strength also transformed; at the very least, he could already match a true First Realm, and was not weaker than True River Sword Ancestor and the others.


Chapter 1641 Breakthrough, Half-Step Eternal Realm!

Chapter 1641 Breakthrough, Half-Step Eternal Realm!

Very quickly.
Ye Tian’s true body and clone body both stepped into the second stage of the will world, each condensing 1000 will worlds, and both completed their transformation.
After the transformation of his will, Ye Tian discovered that the Rift Wind Valley could no longer create any impact on his will at all.
In other words, Rift Wind Valley could no longer help him.
He could continue cultivating his will world, but he could no longer rely on Rift Wind Valley.
“Forget it. I’ve already gained such great benefits this time; I should be satisfied!”
Ye Tian muttered.
During this long period, Ye Tian had claimed that his avatar was always in the Traceless Territory, so the other twelve ancestors did not look for him, and he had not even attended any meetings.
But from time to time, some important notices were still sent to him by message.
The Twelve Ancestors also made one move, but Ye Tian did not go to participate.
For experts like True River Sword Ancestor at the Extreme Stage level, they had already been stuck at the Half-Step Eternal Realm for countless years, and in their dreams they all wanted to break through and become Eternal Realm beings.
Therefore, they would participate in any opportunity and never give up. What if they really happened to break through by chance?
On this day.
Ye Tian dissolved his clone body and avatar by himself, leaving the Traceless Territory in this way.
And the several treasures he had obtained from the Traceless Tower back then, after True River Sword Ancestor and the others left, also had their avatars walk out of the entrance, allowing the true body to take away treasures such as the Void God Leaf.
Thus, these treasures were not lost either.
Void Source Hall.
The clone body and avatar were once again condensed. The avatar cultivated the will world, while the clone body comprehended the Innate Eternal Rule, and as for the true body, it mainly focused on improving its cultivation.
What Ye Tian most wanted to do right now was raise his cultivation to the Extreme of the Ninth-Stage Supreme Being. Only in that way would his strength advance by leaps and bounds, even becoming much stronger than True River Sword Ancestor, perhaps giving him hope of matching a Second Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm being.
However, cultivating from Ninth-Stage Supreme Being to the Extreme of Ninth-Stage Supreme Being also required enormous resources and time; the deeper the foundation, the longer it naturally took.
Ten calamity eras!
One hundred calamity eras!
One thousand calamity eras!
Unknowingly, tens of thousands of calamity eras had passed.
After such a long period, and after expending many resources, Ye Tian finally raised his cultivation to the Extreme of Ninth-Stage Supreme Being.
At this moment, he was only one step away from the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
To break through from Ninth-Stage Supreme Being to the Half-Step Eternal Realm, the Eternal Rule needed to fit with the body, and there was no need for perfect fusion; if one could truly fuse, that would be the Eternal Realm.
But even merely fitting with the body was extremely difficult, and if one’s bodily potential was insufficient or one’s foundation inadequate, there would be no way to break through the shackle.
Only with sufficient potential and foundation could one borrow the moment of fitting with the Eternal Rule to break the shackle and advance into the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
It was not too difficult for Ye Tian to advance into the Half-Step Eternal Realm, but he currently had one trouble: he had comprehended the Innate Eternal Rule.
In other words, while others only needed to fit with the Eternal Rule, he needed to fit with the Innate Eternal Rule in order to borrow that power of compatibility to break the shackle and advance into the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
Thus, the difficulty had increased by more than tenfold.
But once he broke through, the increase in strength would surely be the greatest as well.
“If the true body directly attempts the breakthrough, the success rate won’t be very high. Let the clone body try breaking through repeatedly first! Even if it fails, it can still accumulate some experience. There’s no need to rush the matter of breaking through to the Half-Step Eternal Realm!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian occasionally let the clone body attempt a breakthrough, but at the beginning, it failed every time.
After all, the shackle from Ninth-Stage Supreme Being to the Half-Step Eternal Realm was very difficult to overcome, and many Half-Step Eternal Realm cultivators had relied on external objects when they first broke through, more or less damaging their foundations.
Ye Tian did not want to rely on external objects. Otherwise, he still had the Void True Liquid in his possession; if he took the Void True Liquid, he would be able to break through to the Half-Step Eternal Realm with one hundred percent certainty.
But if that were the case, it would have a huge impact on his future attempt to impact the Eternal Realm.
Therefore, he did not want to use Void True Liquid to break through.
After many attempts, Ye Tian gradually mastered quite a bit of breakthrough experience, and finally on this day successfully broke through to the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
Of course, this was only the clone body breaking through, not the true body.
Afterwards.
Ye Tian dissolved the clone body and began breaking through again.
Gradually, Ye Tian could almost guarantee that he would break through with one hundred percent certainty.
-------------------
“Break through!”
Ye Tian’s true body began to choose to assault the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
Only to see that his incomparably powerful body and the Innate Eternal Rule reached a certain degree of compatibility in a short time, as though the Innate Eternal Rule was fusing with the body on another level, but it was not a true fusion.
And the shackles in the dark, under this state of compatibility, began to become very easy to assault.
Thus, Ye Tian went all out to assault the shackles.
Crack!!!!
The shackles were shattered, the bottleneck was broken, and Ye Tian officially stepped into the Half-Step Eternal Realm level.
At this moment, his body began to transform, and even the power within him began to convert into Half-Step Eternal power.
Not only that, Ye Tian’s will also rose by a great margin.
After a long time, Ye Tian’s breakthrough was finally completely finished.
“Far, far stronger power than before!”
Ye Tian said excitedly.
At this moment, he could already be considered Extreme Stage.
Because he had reached the Half-Step Eternal Realm, created many Eternal Techniques, and also comprehended the Innate Eternal Rule, there was no real difference from Extreme Stage.
The only somewhat weak point was that his Half-Step Eternal power was still relatively weak.
However, the Half-Step Eternal Realm did not emphasize cultivation level, so he could be considered an Extreme Stage-level Half-Step Eternal Realm.
Ye Tian closed his eyes and sensed the state of his body, immediately realizing what level his current strength was probably at.
Three Extreme Stage!
Before the breakthrough, he had been between One Extreme Stage and Two Extreme Stage, or rather, the weakest Two Extreme Stage. But now, he could already be considered a top-tier Three Extreme Stage, only one step away from Four Extreme Stage.
As long as he stabilized his realm and increased his Half-Step Eternal power, his strength would formally step into the level of a Four Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm.
And the cultivation of Extreme Stage was to strengthen the Innate Eternal Rule, using the compatibility between the Innate Eternal Rule and the body to stimulate the body to strengthen step by step, thereby reaching a higher Extreme Stage.
With Ye Tian’s current potential and standard, before becoming Seven Extreme Stage, he would practically not encounter any bottleneck at all.
As for other Half-Step Eternal Realm cultivators, such as True River Sword Ancestor, they found it very difficult to continue improving already at the One Extreme Stage level, because what he could improve had basically already been improved, and the remaining parts were very hard to improve.
After breaking through to the Half-Step Eternal Realm, Ye Tian quickly discovered a problem: his cultivation consumed too much. Although he had once obtained massive resources in the Primordial Sea, even that could not withstand such consumption.
In addition, condensing clone bodies also required resources, and the resources consumed by countless condensations and dissolutions were an astronomical number.
According to his estimate, by the time he became a Five Extreme Stage Half-Step Eternal Realm, he would probably have no resources left.


Chapter 1642 The Opportunity of One Hundred Thousand Eternal Years!

Chapter 1642 The Opportunity of One Hundred Thousand Eternal Years!

“In the future, I still need to collect more resources!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
With his current strength, collecting resources would not be too slow either. After all, he would soon be able to reach the Half-Step Eternal Realm Stage of the Four Extremes Realm, and in the Source Sea, Half-Step Eternal Realm powerhouses above the Four Extremes Realm were exceedingly rare, numbering no more than fifteen.
Coupled with his life-preserving ability, it could be said that in the Source Sea, he was almost not afraid of anyone; no one could kill him unless an Eternal Realm expert came over from the Time-Space Territory.
In the following years, Ye Tian worked hard to improve his cultivation, strengthen his comprehension of the Innate Eternal Rules, and at the same time cultivate the Will World.
In the hundreds of thousands of calamity eras since coming out of the Wuhen Territory, Ye Tian's progress in the Will World had not been great. After all, without a treasure land like the Rift Wind Valley to assist him, and with the Will World having already stepped into the second tier, it became very difficult to increase his will.
And because increasing will was very difficult, opening up the Will World became very slow. In the later stages, if will did not improve, then he simply could not continue opening up the Will World.
Now, although Ye Tian's Will World had far exceeded 1,000, reaching 5,289 Will Worlds, it was still a long way from breaking through to 10,000 Will Worlds. Only by reaching 10,000 Will Worlds could he advance to a third-tier Will World and usher in yet another transformation of his will.
But no matter what, Ye Tian's will was still slowly improving now. This was the improvement brought about by the Will World secret art. Before reaching a bottleneck, the improvement of his will would not stop; it would only become slower and slower.
After another long period of time passed, Ye Tian's cultivation had improved quite a bit, and he had passed the rapid improvement period of the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
At this point, his combat strength had improved considerably and had already reached the Half-Step Eternal Realm Stage of the Four Extremes Realm.
It could be said that he was now already the top combat strength of the entire Source Sea, standing above the other twelve ancestors of the Source God Pavilion. If he displayed his strength, he would be enough to become the first ancestor among the thirteen ancestors.
However, that had no real meaning.
-------------------
Source Sea, True Extremity Palace.
True Extremity Palace was one of the top major powers in the Source Sea, even much stronger than a loose power like the Source God Pavilion, yet it was extremely low-key and did not accept ordinary disciples. As a result, its numbers were not many, but every single one was an elite among elites, a prodigy among prodigies.
Just the Extreme Realm alone numbered nine, even more than the Source God Pavilion; the most important thing was quality.
True Extremity Palace had Half-Step Eternal Realm powerhouses of the Four Extremes Realm, while before Ye Tian, the Source God Pavilion did not have a Four Extremes Realm expert at all, not even a Second Extremes Realm one.
Therefore, True Extremity Palace was much stronger than the Source God Pavilion.
Moreover, True Extremity Palace was incomparably united, a true power rather than a loose one.
At this moment, the palace master of True Extremity Palace, Qingming Sacred Ancestor, a Half-Step Eternal Realm expert at the Four Extremes Realm, was entertaining three guests.
“Qiyuan Source Ancestor, Fengling Source Ancestor, Wulong Source Ancestor, the three of you have descended upon my True Extremity Palace. Could it be that Lord Beihai Territory Lord has some order to issue?”
Qingming Sacred Ancestor asked.
The Beihai Territory Lord he mentioned was the Eternal Realm he served, and in fact the Beihai Territory Lord was once a palace master of True Extremity Palace. After breaking through to the Eternal Realm, he left the Source Sea, occupied a Time-Space Territory, established the Beihai Territory, and became the Beihai Territory Lord.
But True Extremity Palace had always been serving the Beihai Territory Lord, gathering intelligence and supplying talent.
However, the geniuses born from True Extremity Palace were not many, and compared with the Beihai Territory, they fell far short. Thus the Beihai Territory Lord did not pay much attention to True Extremity Palace and rarely sent people over.
But this time, he had sent three Four Extremes Realm experts, which showed that the task was not simple.
Qiyuan Source Ancestor said solemnly, “Qingming Sacred Ancestor, Lord Beihai Territory Lord sent us here because of the opportunity of one hundred thousand eternal years!”
“The opportunity of one hundred thousand eternal years?”
Qingming Sacred Ancestor was first stunned for a moment, but then he immediately reacted to what Qiyuan Source Ancestor meant.
An eternal year was a unit of time used by Eternal Realm experts; one eternal year was equivalent to one million calamity eras. How long was one hundred thousand eternal years?
Even he, Qingming Sacred Ancestor, had not yet lived through one hundred thousand eternal years; he was only seven or eight thousand eternal years old, and that was already an incomparably great age.
The era in which he was born could be called the beginning of the Source Sea. The Source Sea had abundant resources, and all kinds of rare resources were born one after another.
But for Eternal Realm experts, seven or eight thousand eternal years ago was merely the beginning of one Source Sea cycle. When the next cycle began, the resources of the Source Sea would explode again, just like the scene at the beginning of the Source Sea.
And exactly how many eternal years the Source Sea had truly existed for, no one was too sure.
Although Qingming Sacred Ancestor had not been born in the era of one hundred thousand eternal years ago, he had heard of a secret: every one hundred thousand eternal years, the Source Sea would give birth to an astonishing opportunity, even causing slaughter among Eternal Realm experts.
The last time, one hundred thousand eternal years ago, many Eternal Realm experts fought and turned the entire Source Sea into ruins. After many years, the Source Sea finally recovered its vitality and ushered in a great explosion of resources. It was named by later generations of cultivators as the Beginning of the Source Sea Era, which also meant the rebirth of the Source Sea.
In fact, before one hundred thousand eternal years ago, Eternal Realm experts often appeared in the Source Sea. But after that great war, the Territory Lord Alliance issued an order forbidding Eternal Realm experts from staying in the Source Sea. Even if they had business to attend to in the Source Sea, they were not allowed to remain for too long, all to prevent similar things from happening.
After all, the Time-Space Territory Lords were attached to the Source Sea, and they also did not want any problems to occur in the Source Sea.
Once the Source Sea had problems, then the countless Time-Space Territory Lords would also cease to exist.
“The three of you were sent by Lord Beihai Territory Lord to seek that great opportunity?” Qingming Sacred Ancestor asked.
“Yes!”
Qiyuan Source Ancestor nodded. “Lord Beihai Territory Lord asked us to investigate, and True Extremity Palace must also dispatch all its forces. Once we investigate the location of the opportunity and the time of its birth, we will immediately notify Lord Beihai Territory Lord. At that time, Lord Beihai Territory Lord will personally descend upon the Source Sea.”
“I understand. I will fully cooperate with the three of you!”
Qingming Sacred Ancestor replied.
Similar things were unfolding in one power after another, with many Eternal Realm experts sending Half-Step Eternal Realm powerhouses of the Extreme Realm down to the Source Sea.
This kind of news could not be hidden at all, and the Source God Pavilion also learned of it.
Thus.
True River Sword Ancestor transmitted the message to the thirteen ancestors and opened a meeting.
And after Ye Tian received the news, he immediately sent his replicated body to the Source God Pavilion.


Chapter 1643 Five Extreme Stage, the Sea of Silence!

Chapter 1643 Five Extreme Stage, the Sea of Silence!

Inside the Source God Pavilion.
Ye Tian and the other twelve ancestors all came and took their seats one by one.
Ye Tian also roughly understood the situation, but not much.
When True River Sword Ancestor and the other twelve ancestors saw Ye Tian and sensed Ye Tian’s cultivation, they were immediately shocked.
“Congratulations to the Endless Founding Ancestor on advancing to the Extreme Stage!”
“Congratulations to the Endless Founding Ancestor on advancing to the Extreme Stage!”
“Congratulations to the Endless Founding Ancestor on advancing to the Extreme Stage!”
The twelve ancestors all congratulated him one after another.
They even felt that Ye Tian’s strength was more terrifying than theirs, but it was hard to say exactly how many Extreme Stages he had reached; but he was definitely above the first Extreme Stage.
For a time, everyone’s attitude toward Ye Tian changed slightly, and perhaps even they themselves did not notice it—there was a faint trace of respect.
Very quickly, everyone returned to the main topic.
True River Sword Ancestor said, “Everyone, the main topic of this meeting is to discuss a major event that happened recently. I believe all of you know that many temporal lords have dispatched many Extreme Stage experts to the Source Sea, all for the sake of seeking an opportunity.”
Wind Ancient Source Ancestor followed up, “I don’t know much about this matter. I only know that it is related to an opportunity from one hundred thousand Eternal Years ago, but I myself have not existed for even sixty thousand Eternal Years, so I don’t know much about such distant ages.”
“I know even less!”
Ye Tian shook his head.
One Eternal Year was equivalent to a million Tribulation Yuan years. How many Eternal Years had he lived for?
So, he had no idea about such a secret at all.
Seeing this, True River Sword Ancestor said, “In fact, in the Source God Pavilion, I should be the only Half-step Eternal Being who truly experienced one hundred thousand Eternal Years. One hundred thousand Eternal Years ago, that was the era known as before the beginning of the Source Sea. Many Eternal Beings fought to seize an opportunity. The number of fallen Eternal Beings alone reached double digits or more; countless Eternal Heavens were blasted apart, and endless small heavens were shattered into nothingness. As for the Supreme Beings who were affected and killed, there is no way to know how many there were. I count as one of the lucky Half-step Eternal Beings who survived.”
“It is said that once every one hundred thousand Eternal Years, the Source Sea will give birth to an opportunity, and the opportunity from last time was too precious, which made many Eternal Beings tempted, and that was why such a terrifying war erupted. I learned from a secret channel that the last opportunity was a supreme treasure that could greatly increase the strength of even an Eternal Being, and even gave hope of standing above other Eternal Beings. However, I don’t know exactly what it was, and I don’t even know whose hands it fell into.”
“However, after the last war among Eternal Beings, the Lord Alliance stipulated that Eternal Beings were not allowed to stay in the Source Sea for long periods of time. This time, it should not become as great a war as last time. Still, once that opportunity appears, there will definitely be no shortage of Eternal Beings taking part in the battle.”
True River Sword Ancestor spoke at length, allowing Ye Tian and the others to basically understand the situation.
At this time, they were also very interested in such an opportunity.
If they were to obtain such an opportunity, could they become Eternal Beings?
Of course, the greater possibility was that while fighting over the opportunity, they would be casually crushed to death by an Eternal Being.
Unless they were lucky enough for the opportunity to be born without much commotion, and just happened to be discovered by them.
But based on what they had learned, when the opportunity first appeared, there would be an anomaly, and although the range covered by the anomaly was not large, the chance of it being discovered was very, very high.
Especially now, when the major forces had all deployed countless people, once the opportunity appeared, it would definitely be discovered.
At the meeting.
Some Half-step Eternal Beings proposed not participating in this matter, while others proposed taking a gamble—what if they were lucky?
It was obvious that quite a few Half-step Eternal Beings still yearned desperately for such an opportunity; perhaps this was their only chance to charge toward Eternal Being.
In the end.
True River Sword Ancestor said, “I don’t really recommend that you participate, and in today’s era, it is very easy to come into conflict with those Extreme Stage experts who have arrived from the temporal lands. If you don’t plan to participate, then cultivate in seclusion during this period. If there are any unexpected situations, everyone can share information. If the opportunity appears and the Eternal Beings’ battle becomes too tragic, I will provide a place for everyone to take shelter.”
Very quickly, the meeting ended.
One after another, the Half-step Eternal Beings left, and Ye Tian also left.
……
“What exactly is the opportunity that appears once every one hundred thousand Eternal Years?”
Ye Tian was somewhat curious.
If it did not endanger his own life or affect the Dark Forbidden Domain, then he would not mind joining in. If he truly gained a bit of benefit, perhaps it would be enough for him to grow into an Eternal Being.
Perhaps that was also the thinking of many Half-step Eternal Beings.
Time passed, and more and more Extreme Stage experts from the various temporal lords came to the Source Sea, naturally bringing about some conflicts with the major forces.
News of Supreme Beings being killed was often heard, and most of it involved Extreme Stage and Half-step Eternal Being powerhouses from the temporal lands.
· ·········求鮮花··· ·····
Meanwhile, Ye Tian remained very low-key, cultivating all the while, and the Dark Forbidden Domain side remained very peaceful.
Unknowingly, several hundred thousand Tribulation Yuan years passed again.
The opportunity born once every one hundred thousand Eternal Years had still not appeared. Even those Eternal Beings were anxious now; some Eternal Beings even personally came to the Source Sea to investigate certain regions, but they quickly left again.
Void Source Hall.
Ye Tian ended his cultivation.
At this time, he had already cultivated to the Five Extreme Stage. After all, before the Seven Extreme Stage, he had basically no bottleneck; he only needed to increase his cultivation, and his strength would rise accordingly.
However, after reaching the Five Extreme Stage, he had almost used up the resources on him. Although he still had a few treasures left, even if he took them out to trade for resources, they would not fetch many valuable resources.
.... ....... .......
On this day.
The artifact spirit of the Void Source Hall came to inform Ye Tian of a major matter.
“Master, some changes have occurred outside the Void Source Hall.”
The artifact spirit reported.
Changes outside the Void Source Hall?
Ye Tian’s expression changed.
The Void Source Hall was located in a forbidden zone of the Source Sea, and this forbidden zone was the Sea of Silence.
Even a Half-step Eternal Being like Void Source Ancestor did not dare to step into the Sea of Silence, and had thrown the Void Source Hall into the Sea of Silence. The enemies of Void Source Ancestor also did not dare to enter the Sea of Silence to search for the Void Source Hall.
This shows how terrifying the Sea of Silence was.
Even a Half-step Eternal Being at the first Extreme Stage would not dare to risk entering the Sea of Silence, because the Sea of Silence possessed a peculiar power. Those with unsteady wills would sink into total silence and become a floating corpse in the Sea of Silence.
Although the Void Source Hall could resist the power of the Sea of Silence, once it went outside, it still would not be enough.
There had once been an Extreme Stage expert who conducted experiments. Basically, one needed at least the strength of the third Extreme Stage to walk in the Sea of Silence, but even then there was still some danger, and only Half-step Eternal Beings above the sixth Extreme Stage could completely ignore the dangers of the Sea of Silence.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian’s duplicate body directly walked out of the Void Source Hall and arrived in the Sea of Silence.
Buzz!!!!
Waves of power surged in, but Ye Tian’s will had already reached the second level of the Will World, and his will power was almost comparable to an Eternal Being, so he ignored those strange powers.
Ye Tian investigated his surroundings and discovered an astonishing scene.


Chapter 1644 A Chance That Comes Once Every One Hundred Thousand Eternal Years,..

Chapter 1644 A Chance That Comes Once Every One Hundred Thousand Eternal Years Has Been Found!

On the Sea of Silence, one corpse after another floated on the surface.
There were corpses of Supreme Beings, corpses of half-step Eternal Realm experts, and even some corpses of Invincible Beings.
“Strange, where did so many corpses come from?”
Ye Tian was puzzled.
It was not as if he had never been to the Sea of Silence before. He had been here earlier, but the Sea of Silence had contained nothing at all.
In the past, there had indeed been many Supreme Beings and even half-step Eternal Realm experts who had fallen in the Sea of Silence, but after these experts fell, they quickly disappeared.
This was also one of the Sea of Silence’s secrets. As for the reason, no one knew.
But now, the corpses of these experts had surfaced.
At once, Ye Tian sensed the Sea of Silence’s eeriness; it seemed that some special change had taken place here.
He did not think too much about it, and immediately collected the Void Balls of these experts.
The resources accumulated by these experts added up to a considerable amount. Although there might not be many resources useful to him, leaving so many resources to the human race was still not bad.
Before long, Ye Tian had collected all the Void Balls of these experts.
As for the corpses of these experts, he sent them away to be buried in a blessed land.
……
“I’m afraid something has happened to the Sea of Silence. The Void Source Hall can’t stay here anymore!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Moreover, for him, the Sea of Silence was not a forbidden land anymore; this was also true for those powerful extreme experts.
Therefore, there was no need for the Void Source Hall to remain in the Sea of Silence; it could be directly taken back to the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Whoosh!
The enormous Void Source Hall entered Ye Tian’s body, and Ye Tian flew out of the Sea of Silence, quickly returning to the Dark Forbidden Domain.
After placing the Void Source Hall in the Dark Forbidden Domain, Ye Tian’s clone body once again came to the Sea of Silence, watching the changes in the Sea of Silence at all times.
As time passed, the void in the Sea of Silence gradually fluctuated, and the fluctuations came from a deeper void.
And those experts who had fallen in the Sea of Silence back then had been swallowed up by the unknown void; now that the void was fluctuating, those corpses appeared again.
However, before the changes in the Sea of Silence were completely over, Ye Tian found it difficult to do anything.
He tried to follow the void fluctuations into that unknown void, but an unknown force blocked him, preventing him from entering at all.
He had already reached the level of a Five Extreme Stage half-step Eternal Realm expert, and yet this force could easily block him. It was clear that if there really was a chance here, it would be extremely extraordinary.
“Could the once-in-one-hundred-thousand-eternal-years chance that those Eternal Realm lords want to find be right here?”
Ye Tian guessed.
If it really were here, then the Sea of Silence would probably become a battlefield!
Fortunately, the Dark Forbidden Domain was relatively far from the Sea of Silence. If they were close, even a little bit of battle ripple from an Eternal Realm expert would probably cause an eternal world to collapse.
In the blink of an eye, another kalpa era passed.
The void fluctuations in the Sea of Silence became increasingly intense, even extending beyond the Sea of Silence, but because there were no living beings nearby, the news had not yet spread.
But Ye Tian was very clear that this place would eventually be discovered.
This day.
The changes in the Sea of Silence reached a certain limit, and endless golden light enveloped the entire Sea of Silence, even covering the territories around the Sea of Silence.
Ye Tian saw a golden tree within the golden light. This golden tree did not seem very large, but its radiance actually suppressed time and space, suppressed everything, as if it were the source of all things, and as if it were the essence of everything.
And around the golden tree was an endless land, but because the distance was too far and the scenery around it did not possess an aura as powerful as the golden tree’s, it could not be projected over, and Ye Tian could not see it clearly.
“This is absolutely a chance that only arises once every one hundred thousand eternal years!”
Ye Tian did not say another word and directly charged toward the depths of that unknown void.
Perhaps Eternal Realm experts would arrive very soon, but if he did not fight for such a chance, he would regret it for the rest of his life.
This time, the unknown force did not hinder Ye Tian.
Ye Tian followed a golden road deeper into that unknown void, and soon arrived at that void location.
And just at that moment, a strange force struck, several times stronger than the eerie force of the Sea of Silence.
Ye Tian ignored this force, stepped off the golden road, and landed on a stretch of land. .........
Faintly, he saw the golden tree in the distant distance, but it was still relatively far from here.
Moreover, the eerie force here was constantly affecting him.
Added to that, the suppression here was terrifying, so it would probably take Ye Tian some time to reach the golden tree.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian moved quickly, wanting to reach the golden tree sooner.
But very soon, his expression changed.
“How can this be?”
The more distance he moved, the stronger the impact of the strange force became.
“I’m afraid I won’t be able to reach the golden tree!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
But after advancing for a stretch, Ye Tian was no longer worried.
Because he had discovered a treasure.
“This is the Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass!”
Ye Tian said in shock.
The Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass was an incomparably precious resource in the source sea, and this was true even for half-step Eternal Realm experts. It could increase the strength of the body, improve cultivation, and also enhance the Eternal Body.
If someone’s Eternal Body had not yet reached the Perfected realm, then just a small section of the Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass would be enough to raise their Eternal Body to the Perfected realm.
It could be said that there was nothing on Ye Tian’s person whose value could compare to the Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass, not even the Void True Liquid.
Even if an extreme half-step Eternal Realm expert saw this stalk of Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass, they would probably be extremely excited.
“Hahaha, it seems that aside from that golden tree, there are other resources here. Even if I can’t reach the location of that golden tree, obtaining these resources is already enough!”
Whoosh!
A clone condensed and immediately took this stalk of Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass back to the outside world.
He did not want to fall here and let the resource be left behind.
The clone’s speed was very fast. It quickly left this place, and after leaving the Sea of Silence, it rapidly traversed back to the Dark Forbidden Domain, then delivered the Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass to the main body’s hands.
After that, the clone continued toward the Sea of Silence.
Not long after, Ye Tian found some more resources. Although they were not as good as the Void Scale Golden Leaf Grass, they were not far off, and the clone took on the role of a porter.
Not long after.
The changes in the Sea of Silence also drew the attention of other half-step Eternal Realm experts.


Chapter 1645: Lords of the Eternal Realm Descend One After Another!

Chapter 1645: Lords of the Eternal Realm Descend One After Another!

A half-step Eternal Realm expert arrived here and discovered the changes in the Sea of Silence.
“This is……”
The half-step Eternal Realm expert, Qianyu Domain Ancestor, stared in shock at that golden tree, immediately sensing that this was surely a heaven-shaking opportunity, and it might even be the kind of opportunity that was said to be born only once every one hundred thousand Eternal years recently.
“I’m very likely the first one!”
Qianyu Domain Ancestor was incomparably excited and immediately flew toward the depths of the void where that golden tree was located.
However, an eerie force came surging in.
“Not good!”
Only then did he remember the terror of the Sea of Silence, and that the place where the golden tree was located was not within the Sea of Silence, but was very likely the true source of the Sea of Silence.
He had been blinded by the opportunity and had not thought of this problem at all.
Boom!!!!!
Under the impact of that eerie force, Qianyu Domain Ancestor’s will was destroyed, his consciousness gradually faded away, and his body turned into a corpse floating on the golden road.
Not long after, the anomaly here was completely discovered and spread throughout the entire Source Sea.
Qingming Saint Ancestor of the True Extreme Palace and Qi Yuan Domain Ancestor from the Space-Time Territory, as well as other extreme experts, also arrived here.
At the same time, a large number of extreme experts descended upon the area.
Of course, most of the extreme experts here came from various Space-Time Territories, while the extreme experts native to the Source Sea were relatively few.
“Found it. This is the true opportunity that is born only once every one hundred thousand Eternal years!”
The extreme experts were absolutely certain.
Immediately after, they notified the lords of the Space-Time Territories.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!!!
One extreme expert after another wanted to rush in, otherwise once the Eternal Realm lords descended, how would it still be their turn?
When one extreme expert after another charged into the golden road, they soon turned into corpses, and only a Five-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm expert did not fall.
However, under the impact of that eerie force, his whole body trembled, clearly suffering tremendous pain as well.
Seeing this scene, the weaker extreme experts no longer dared to enter.
So many extreme experts had fallen at once; when had something like this happened in the Source Sea in all these years?
“Get down. Before our Lord Xuanyu arrives, none of you are allowed to go in!”
A Seven-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm expert made his move, extending a hand into the golden road, grabbing that Five-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm expert directly, and throwing him to a faraway place.
Boom rumble!!!!!
A group of Six- and Seven-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm experts blocked the area, not allowing any stronger expert to enter.
Very soon, the Eternal Realm lords descended.
Northern Sea Lord, Xuanyu Lord, Lianyi Lord, Linghe Lord……
One lord after another descended. The aura of each lord made those half-step Eternal Realm experts tremble uncontrollably, not daring to meet their gaze at all.
When Lianyi Lord saw that golden tree, his eyes lit up brilliantly.
“If I’m not mistaken, this should be the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree. The opportunity born this time is actually it!”
“Hahaha, it really is the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree. The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree can give birth to Eternal Knowledge Golden Fruits; it can enhance our wills and even help break through bottlenecks and shackles. The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree also has another enormous function, and that is upgrading Space-Time Lords, turning ordinary Space-Time Lords into Eternal Space-Time Territories. The resources born from an Eternal Space-Time Lord are beyond imagination. If I can snatch the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree, I will certainly become a top existence among the Eternal Realm!”
“What a joke. You can also snatch the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree? It will definitely belong to me!”
“The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree belongs to me!”
The lords immediately started arguing.
They did not waste time continuing the argument, and all of them charged into the golden road at once, entering the unknown depths of the void and heading toward the place where the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree was located.

Voices sounded from within.
“You lot can come in too. There are some good things here, and they’re useful to you as well!”
The lords reminded their servants through transmission.
“There are other good things?”
The extreme experts became excited and all rushed in.
As far as they knew, the opportunity born one hundred thousand Eternal years ago had only one treasure and no other treasures, which was why it had only caused slaughter among the Eternal Realm experts, while the half-step Eternal Realm experts had gained no benefits at all and instead been affected, suffering heavy losses in the fighting.
“We came at the right time this time. Hurry and go in!”
A Six-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm expert said excitedly.
In the Space-Time Territories, many Seven-Extreme, and even Eight-Extreme, half-step Eternal Realm experts were unwilling to obey the orders of the Eternal Realm and come here to search for the once-in-one-hundred-thousand-Eternal-years opportunity, and thus they were unable to descend into the Source Sea.
So, those experts had lost this opportunity this time.
Basically, half-step Eternal Realm experts above the Four-Extreme Realm had all passed through the golden road, but even if Four-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm experts paid the price to get through it, they could only barely walk onto the land in the depths of the void and could not go deeper at all. Whether they could find good things depended entirely on luck.
As for Three-Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm experts, they did not dare enter at all. Once they stepped onto the golden road, they would be blasted to death by the eerie force before they could go far.
Outside the golden road.
Zhenhe Sword Ancestor and the others from the Source God Pavilion stood there, all sighing endlessly and not daring to go in at all.
“Forget it. This opportunity has nothing to do with us. Registration is more important. Let’s go!” Zhenhe Sword Ancestor suggested.
“Mm, let’s go. I wonder if the Endless Ancestor has gone in?” Fenggu Domain Ancestor asked curiously.
“The Endless Ancestor has never appeared, so he probably didn’t go in either?” Zhenhe Sword Ancestor was not sure.
However, no matter what, this opportunity had nothing to do with them anymore.
