“Undying Golden Sun Flower, another treasure that drives even extreme experts crazy!”
Ye Tian was incomparably excited.
In such a short time, he had already found dozens of treasures, and most of them were treasures he did not recognize.
Boom rumble rumble!!!!!
Auras of one Eternal Realm after another came from the distance, not the least bit concealed.
“The Eternal Realm lords have come in!”
Ye Tian immediately concealed his aura, even hiding himself with a second-tier will.
As long as the Eternal Realm lords did not investigate carefully, he could still conceal himself.
The true target of those Eternal Realm lords was only that Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree, so they did not investigate other places.
They also did not want to waste time and end up having that Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree snatched away.
Therefore, they did not discover Ye Tian’s traces.
However, when these Eternal Realm experts approached the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree, their speed all slowed a great deal, and the eerie force also affected them.
Ye Tian was interested in the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree, but he knew he could not compete with the Eternal Realm experts for it, so his target was only the other resources.
Compared with the other extreme experts, his will was comparable to that of an Eternal Realm expert, so he could go to more places.
Therefore, he could obtain more resources.
“About time. Let’s have the clone take these resources back!”
Ye Tian murmured.


Chapter 1646: The Taichen Sacred Flower, Ye Tian’s Excitement!

Chapter 1646: The Taichen Sacred Flower, Ye Tian’s Excitement!

Whoosh!
The clone returned to the Source Sea with various resources, but just as it was about to reach the golden avenue and leave, a figure blocked Ye Tian.
“Hand over what you gained inside!”
the figure said.
“Dream on!”
Ye Tian refused.
“You’re courting death!”
The other side directly made a move, and his strength was fully exposed.
Seven Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm!
And Ye Tian was only at Five Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm, not his opponent.
However, with the other party’s strength, it was still impossible to kill him.
Boom!!!!
The two sides fought fiercely.
Ye Tian found that he was not suppressed much, and he quickly understood why.
Because he ignored the impact of the strange power, while this Seven Extreme Realm still had to resist it, preventing him from unleashing his full strength.
Moreover, Ye Tian’s Endless Eternal Body was a legendary Eternal Body, surpassing the upper Eternal Body, and its life-preserving ability was even more terrifying.
Thus, even if he was injured, he could quickly recover.
This caused Ye Tian to fight for a long time without being harmed at all.
“Damn it, I can’t kill him!”
The Seven Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm expert finally gave up. If he continued to tangle with him, he would probably gain very little.
So, he stopped fighting and entered this world.
“Hmph!”
Ye Tian snorted coldly.
He knew this Seven Extreme Realm half-step Eternal Realm expert’s identity: he was one of the native Seven Extreme Realm experts of the Source Sea, and also one of the six great Extreme Realm experts of the Source Sea, the Wuyu Domain Ancestor.
Wuyu Domain Ancestor’s strength was no less than that of Wuji Ice Ancestor, and he was also very low-key, rarely ever appearing.
This time, he had appeared as well.
“Wuyu Domain Ancestor, you dared to ambush me. I will never spare you in the future!”
Ye Tian rushed out of the golden avenue, returned to the Source Sea, and soon went back to the Dark Forbidden Domain, delivering all the resources one by one to his main body’s hands before returning.
……
In the void world where the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree was located, the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree radiated out in all directions. The closer one was to the center, the stronger the impact of the strange power; the closer to the edge, the weaker the impact.
Thus, many Extreme Realm experts who could not advance simply moved forward along the edge, not daring to go deeper.
Even some Extreme Realm experts saw a treasure and fought over it.
However, very few Extreme Realm experts fell.
After all, when the difference in strength was not too great, killing one was rather difficult.
Ye Tian did not clash with other Extreme Realm experts. The place he was in was simply unreachable by other Extreme Realm experts.
But Ye Tian also did not want to encounter Eternal Realm lords, so he only searched for resources continuously in that area.
In short, almost all the resources in that area belonged to him, and no one came to seize them from him.
Time slowly passed, and Ye Tian harvested wave after wave of resources. Each time he obtained more than ten kinds of resources, he would send the clone away.
Gradually, Ye Tian’s harvest grew larger and larger.
On this day.
Ye Tian found a treasure that even made him unable to help but cry out in surprise.
“Taichen Sacred Flower!”
The Taichen Sacred Flower was an incomparably precious treasure, extremely rare in the Source Sea. Every time it appeared, it would trigger countless fights among Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm experts.
Once, a Taichen Sacred Flower appeared in the world. Too many half-step Eternal Realm experts fought over it, and in the end it drew the attention of an Eternal Realm expert, who took away that Taichen Sacred Flower.
This showed that even Eternal Realm experts would not ignore the Taichen Sacred Flower.
Because the Taichen Sacred Flower could allow a living being to easily reach half-step Eternal Realm, and its foundation would become incomparably strong. It could even reverse the tribulation body; even without condensing an Eternal Body, it could still raise the tribulation body to a level comparable to a lower Eternal Body.
In other words, if he obtained this Taichen Sacred Flower, he could directly raise his wife to half-step Eternal Realm, and her cultivation would reach the Extreme of half-step Eternal Realm.
In addition, during a period after the breakthrough, her comprehension and insight would erupt, and she could easily comprehend all kinds of Eternal techniques.
Thus, it would not be a problem for his wife to directly reach the Extreme of the top Eternal Realm.
Of course, he did not recommend that his wife step into the Extreme Realm, otherwise it would be somewhat difficult for her to break through to Eternal Realm.
“Take it!”
Ye Tian immediately took the Taichen Sacred Flower, then had the clone immediately bring it back to the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Otherwise, once an Eternal Realm expert learned of it, they probably would not mind erasing him and snatching this Taichen Sacred Flower away.
After all, even Eternal Realm experts probably had relatives who had not reached half-step Eternal Realm and also needed the Taichen Sacred Flower.
Very soon.
The clone successfully returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain, and Ye Tian immediately called his wife, Xiao Yue.
He wanted Xiao Yue to refine the Taichen Sacred Flower as soon as possible; otherwise, keeping it by his side would always make him worry about it being snatched away.
Once Xiao Yue refined the Taichen Sacred Flower, there would be nothing to worry about.
Soon, his wife Xiao Yue arrived.
“Husband!”
Xiao Yue called out.
“Yue’er, immediately refine this Taichen Sacred Flower!”
Ye Tian said hastily.
“．‖What is the Taichen Sacred Flower?” Xiao Yue asked.
Ye Tian explained: “The Taichen Sacred Flower can be said to be one of the few top treasures in the Source Sea. It can immediately raise your cultivation to half-step Eternal Realm, and it can also allow you to comprehend Eternal techniques. Your strength will definitely be comparable to the most top-tier half-step Eternal Realm experts.”
“Husband, such a precious treasure, you should refine it yourself.” Xiao Yue did not want such a treasure wasted on her.
Ye Tian shook his head: “Yue’er, your husband’s strength has already surpassed the top half-step Eternal Realm. Using it on me would be a waste.”
“Then give it to Xingchen and Xingyue to use!”
Xiao Yue said again.
“Don’t worry, after I find other treasures in the future, I will definitely let them use them. This time, you must use it!” Ye Tian said in an imperative tone.
Only then did Xiao Yue stop refusing, and she began refining the Taichen Sacred Flower in front of Ye Tian.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian immediately accelerated time, allowing Xiao Yue to break through quickly.
At the same time.
Ye Tian’s clone also returned to the void world where the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree was located, continuing to act as a porter.
On the other side.
One Eternal Realm expert after another advanced with difficulty. They were not too far from the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree, but there was still some distance before they could reach it.
So, they each took out precious treasures to lessen the suppression of heaven and earth and resist the impact of the strange power.
In this way, they moved a bit faster again.
Among the Eternal Realm experts, there were strong and weak ones.
And Xuanyu Lord was undoubtedly one of the more top-notch existences among these lords, stronger than the other lords, and his will was also very strong.
Thus, he was the closest to the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree.
Suddenly.
Xuanyu Lord took out a mirror, and this mirror blocked the impact of the strange power released by the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree.
Then, he instantly arrived in front of the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree汗.
“Xuanyu Lord, you actually possess the Heavenly Insight Mirror!”
The other Eternal Realm lords were dumbfounded.
“Hahaha, the Yongshi Golden Sea Tree is mine!”
Xuanyu Lord said excitedly.


Chapter 1647 The Battle of the Eternal Realm!

Chapter 1647 The Battle of the Eternal Realm!

Countless golden runes appeared, and under the control of the Xuan Jade Lord, they sealed this Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree.
Although the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree could unleash strange shocks, it was after all just a tree, not an Eternal Realm powerhouse, so it had no way to resist the seal of an Eternal Realm.
Very quickly.
The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree was sealed.
And at the very moment it was sealed, the strange shock instantly disappeared.
The Xuan Jade Lord immediately took away the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree, then prepared to flee.
“Xuan Jade Lord, hand over the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree!!!”
One Eternal Realm Lord after another blocked the Xuan Jade Lord.
Even though the Xuan Jade Lord was somewhat stronger than the other Eternal Realm powerhouses, he still could not withstand so many Eternal Realm powerhouses, and was thus blocked.
Rumble!!!!
A great battle erupted!
Buzz!!!!!!
The terrifying aftershock of the Eternal Realm clash swept in all directions, and countless treasures and resources were shattered into pieces by the aftershock of the Eternal Realm.
The place where Ye Tian was located was not far from where the Eternal Realm powerhouses were fighting, and he was affected immediately.
“The speed of the Eternal Realm powerhouses is too fast, right? They took away that golden tree so quickly. If they had been a little later, I could still have found some resources. What a pity!”
Ye Tian said helplessly.
At once, he swallowed his clone into his inner world, using the copied body to withstand the aftermath of the Eternal Realm battle.
In this way, even if the copied body was annihilated in the end, the clone would not be annihilated as well.
“Run!”
Ye Tian quickly moved through space, but his body was still struck by the aftermath of the Eternal Realm battle until it cracked open. Had it not been for the fact that the recovery power of the legendary Eternal Body, the Endless Eternal Body, was too powerful, even to some extent more terrifying in terms of life-preserving ability than a Seven Extreme Stage half-step Eternal Realm powerhouse.
Otherwise, he would have already been annihilated by that wave just now.
Not only Ye Tian was fleeing, but the other Peak powerhouses were also fleeing.
Ye Tian and the others had not yet escaped this stretch of the void-heaven and earth when it cracked apart.
And the golden path was also torn apart, with countless terrifying aftershocks sweeping through the world.
Some Supreme Beings and half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses watching from the outside were the first to bear the brunt, directly struck into ashes.
Boundless expanses of territory began to collapse, and some nearby alien heavens and even Eternal heavens could no longer withstand the aftermath of the Eternal Realm battle.
Although the rules of the Source Sea were protecting the alien heavens and the Eternal heavens, they still could not withstand the shock of Eternal Realm powerhouses.
Moreover, under such circumstances, traversing space was simply impossible.
At this moment, Ye Tian had already burst out of the Sea of Stillness, but he still had not moved far away from the aftermath of the Eternal Realm battle.
His physical body had already been torn apart quite badly, but overall there was still no major problem.
However, the reason he became like this was that he was too close to the Eternal Realm powerhouses, and had not received any information that they were making a move, so he had not fled immediately.
As for those Peak powerhouses from the Space-Time Territory, they had basically received the news in advance. Even if it was only one second earlier, that was enough to save their lives.
Therefore, those Peak powerhouses from the Space-Time Territory had hardly suffered any losses, but the Peak powerhouses from the Source Sea who had not taken refuge under the Eternal Realm Lords were miserable.
Very soon, Ye Tian’s copied body finally moved far away from the battlefield of the Eternal Realm battle.
Then the clone came out of the copied body’s inner world; it was also injured, but nothing serious.
After that, the clone returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain, and only then did it breathe a sigh of relief.
……
The Xuan Jade Lord was injured, and quite badly at that.
Surrounded and attacked by so many Lords, he simply could not hold them off.
“Are you really going to stop me? This is only my clone. One of you may not have a clone, so be careful—I might fight to the death and take one of you down with me!”
the Xuan Jade Lord threatened.
The Cloud Crane Lord smiled and said, “Xuan Jade Lord, threats are useless. The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree is far too valuable. Whoever gets it will rise. Do you think we’ll give up?”
Not a single Lord was willing to give up; all of them wanted to kill the Xuan Jade Lord’s clone and seize the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree.
Boom!!!!
The Xuan Jade Lord was blasted away by wave after wave of attacks, his physical body shattered, as if he were about to fall.
And at that moment, a figure tore through the void and descended, forcibly entering the battlefield.
He swung a sword across the sky, shattering many Eternal Realm attacks, then came to the Xuan Jade Lord’s side.
The Xuan Jade Lord thought that a powerful Lord had come to save him, but when he saw who it was, his expression changed.
“Void Sword Lord, you actually came!”
The Xuan Jade Lord’s expression changed drastically.
This person could not possibly have come to save him; there was only one possibility, and that was also for the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree.
The Void Sword Lord said nothing and struck with a sword.
The Xuan Jade Lord simply could not withstand it; no method was of any use.
Puff!!!!
This sword shattered the Xuan Jade Lord’s many defenses, annihilating every single cell completely, and even his will was utterly destroyed.
With just one sword strike, this clone of the Xuan Jade Lord was completely fallen.
Although it was because the Xuan Jade Lord was already heavily injured, even without being injured, three sword strikes would have been enough to kill him.
“Lord Void Sword, if you join in, isn’t that against the rules?”
Lord Linghe said somewhat unhappily.
The other Eternal Realm Lords also expressed dissatisfaction, believing that the Void Sword Lord should not have interfered.
Within the Lord Alliance, there was an unwritten rule: Eternal Realm Lords like the Void Sword Lord should not participate in the chance encounter that comes once every one hundred thousand eternal years.
This was an opportunity fought over by ordinary Eternal Realm Lords, and besides, it was of no use to Eternal Realm powerhouses like the Void Sword Lord.
Precisely because of this, they were qualified to snatch it; otherwise, where would they have the chance to obtain such an opportunity?
“This Lord has snatched it—what can you do about it?”
The Void Sword Lord snorted coldly, then took the sealed Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree from the corpse of the Xuan Jade Lord’s clone.
Throughout the entire process, none of the other Eternal Realm Lords dared to make a move, allowing the Void Sword Lord to take the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree away.
It was not until the Void Sword Lord had completely disappeared that these Lords voiced their anger.
“Damn it, the Void Sword Lord openly broke the unspoken rules. Too hateful!”
“The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree indeed has the qualifications to draw the attention of a strong being like the Void Sword Lord, but the Void Sword Lord definitely isn’t doing it for himself. The Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree isn’t of much use to him; his Time-Space Lord has already been upgraded to an Eternal Time-Space Territory. He’s probably doing it for his little lover, Lord Qingxue.”
“Humph, Lord Qingxue’s talent isn’t good, yet he forcibly raised her to the Eternal Realm. Now he’s even prepared the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree for her—she may end up surpassing us.”
“There’s nothing we can do. Who told Lord Qingxue to hook up with the Void Sword Lord? At the Eternal Realm level, the only Lord who can still be influenced by love and affection is probably the Void Sword Lord.”
“Let’s go. Since we didn’t seize the opportunity this time, after we return, we’ll report the intelligence to the Lord Alliance. We must have the Lord Alliance sanction the Void Sword Lord.”
“The most miserable one should be the Xuan Jade Lord. He lost a clone and also lost the Eternal Knowledge Golden Sea Tree. He’s probably going to go mad. We must not provoke him recently!”
Very soon, these Eternal Realm Lords all left the Source Sea one by one.
And this area gradually returned to calm.


Chapter 1648: Seven Peak Realms, Half-Step Eternal Realm!

Chapter 1648: Seven Peak Realms, Half-Step Eternal Realm!

After the Eternal Realm lords left, one after another Half-Step Eternal Realm beings came here and saw how miserable this area had become; each of them let out a sigh.
This is the clash of Eternal Realm experts!
This was still with only a few Eternal Realm beings taking part, and the battle lasted for a very short time. If it continued, the Eternal Realm would probably wage war across every part of Source Sea.
Of course, by then, the Lord Alliance would definitely move to stop them.
But by that time, it would already be too late. No one knew how many heavens in Source Sea would be destroyed, and how many cultivators would fall and die.
Especially some Supreme Beings, who were even more furious. They learned that a chance encounter that appears once every one hundred thousand Eternal Years had been born here, and they fled immediately, but the Eternal heavens they were in did not leave, and thus were destroyed in the aftermath of the battle between Eternal Realm experts.
Therefore, they were angry, but helpless.
Those were Eternal Realm beings; to them, they were like ants. What could they do?
“The forbidden zone, Sea of Silence, is gone!”
Ye Tian muttered.
It had to be said that the power of Eternal Realm was too terrifying. Even he could do nothing about the Sea of Silence, yet the battle of Eternal Realm experts could destroy it.
Compared with the strength of Eternal Realm experts, he was still too weak now, unable even to withstand the aftermath.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian left this place and returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain.
This great opportunity that appeared once every one hundred thousand Eternal Years did not actually bring much gain to those Eternal Realm experts, but he had reaped many benefits.
Among all the Peak Half-Step Eternal Realm experts, his harvest was definitely first.
Moreover, he had also obtained many resources that could improve his own strength.
Therefore, his strength could absolutely be raised a great deal, and he could absolutely easily step into a higher tier.
So next, he needed to go into seclusion for a period of time.
Dark Forbidden Domain.
Ye Tian stayed in the Void Source Hall and began his secluded cultivation.
He took out the Virtual Scale Golden Leaf Grass and directly refined it.
Boom!!!!
Terrifying energy frenziedly tempered his body, his bodily strength continuously increased, and his cultivation continually rose.
It was a pity that his Endless Eternal Body had already reached the Perfected realm, so the Virtual Scale Golden Leaf Grass could no longer continue to improve his Endless Eternal Body.
Time slowly passed, and finally the energy of this stalk of Virtual Scale Golden Leaf Grass was exhausted.
“My strength has increased several times; I’m probably close to the Six Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level!”
Ye Tian said excitedly.
After that, he continued refining some resources.
Although he did not recognize many of the resources, after careful investigation he could still find out what they were. Once he understood their uses, he could use these resources to improve his strength.
Gradually, Ye Tian’s strength reached the Six Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level.
This time, he planned to charge into the Seven Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level before coming out of seclusion.
And the resources he had obtained this time were enough to let him reach the Seven Peak Realm level, more than enough in fact.
Of course, there were also some treasures that were not suitable for improving strength and had other uses; he planned to keep them, or give them to the human race as their foundation.
Unknowingly, several more kalpa eras passed.
On this day.
Ye Tian laughed wildly, incomparably excited.
He had successfully reached the Seven Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level.
However, the remaining resources could no longer continue to improve his strength, because his cultivation had reached a limit and it was very difficult to advance further.
If he wanted to keep improving, he would have to continue comprehending the Innate Eternal Laws; only then would there be hope of reaching the Eight Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level.
Otherwise, the Seven Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level would be his current limit.
For example, the six great Peak Realms of Source Sea, at most could only reach the Seven Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm, and could never break through to the Eight Peak Realm level.
In fact, their Eternal Bodies were not bad either. They were not far from the legendary Eternal Body, and they had also created a large number of Eternal Bodies. Their comprehension of the Innate Eternal Laws might even be deeper than Ye Tian’s, and their cultivation foundation had also reached an inconceivable degree.
Perhaps their foundation was not as good as Ye Tian’s at the beginning, but once they reached the Peak Realm, there were many, many resources to make up for or strengthen their foundation.
Therefore, compared with these people, Ye Tian did not have much advantage. If he did not have other opportunities, it would also be very hard for him to reach the Eight Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian thought of a way to improve his strength, and that was to improve his world of will.
His world of will was currently at the Second Stage. If it reached the Third Stage, perhaps he would have a chance to reach the Eight Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm level.
After cultivating for several more kalpa eras, Ye Tian’s strength did not improve much, so he began striving to raise the strength of the human race.
With his help, the strength of the human race’s Supreme Beings improved very quickly, and Ye Xingchen, Ye Xinyue, and the others also obtained several treasures bestowed by Ye Tian, remade their foundations, and increased their potential. In addition, with many resources for improving cultivation, each of them quickly rose to above the Seven-stage Supreme Being level.
· ·········求鮮花··· ·····
At this rate, it would not be difficult for them to raise their cultivation to the One-stage Supreme Being level.
If they wanted to reach the Half-Step Eternal Realm, they could either consume Void True Liquid, or rely on their own efforts to charge into the Half-Step Eternal Realm.
On this day.
His wife Xiao Yue came out of seclusion.
“Husband, I’ve broken through!”
Xiao Yue appeared before Ye Tian, saying excitedly.
Ye Tian looked over and saw that Xiao Yue’s cultivation had already reached the limit of the Half-Step Eternal Realm, and her comprehension of the Eternal Laws had also reached a very high level. Perhaps she had even created quite a few Eternal techniques.
.... ....... .......
Therefore, Xiao Yue’s strength was definitely at the very top of Half-Step Eternal Realm battle power, no weaker than several of the twelve ancestors of the Source God Pavilion, and perhaps even a bit stronger.
This was the effect of the Supreme Morning Flower; it was too heaven-defying!
With Xiao Yue’s breakthrough, the human race now had two Half-Step Eternal Realm experts.
In the years that followed, relying on his Seven Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm strength, Ye Tian stormed through many treasure lands and looted many resources one by one.
Many of those resources were useless to him, and he did not take them for himself, but for the human race.
Unknowingly, another long several million kalpa eras passed, equivalent to several Eternal Years.
By now.
The human race had given birth to a large number of Supreme Beings, and even Ye Xingchen and the others had reached the Nine-stage Supreme Being realm. Among them, Ye Yu directly used Void True Liquid to raise herself to the Half-Step Eternal Realm and no longer planned to rely on herself to break through.
At the same time, Ye Tian found many resources that could help them refine avatars, and thus many upper echelons of the human race now had avatars.
But Ye Tian’s own strength still had not improved much. Only his will had improved somewhat, and he had opened dozens more worlds of will. He had also created several more Eternal techniques, and refined some of his previous Eternal techniques.
In addition, his comprehension of the Innate Eternal Laws had become somewhat stronger.
But even so, he was still a long way from the Eight Peak Realm Half-Step Eternal Realm.
Thus, Ye Tian decided to leave Source Sea and head to the Time-Space Territory to seek opportunities.
Of course, he would only send a duplicate body there, while his true body would remain in the Dark Forbidden Domain and.


Chapter 1649 Maple Leaf Domain, Initial Entry!

Chapter 1649 Maple Leaf Domain, Initial Entry!

Among the half-step Eternal Realm cultivators in the Source Sea, the most common way to go to the time-space Domains was to take refuge under some time-space lord and have that lord bring them out of the Source Sea.
But after years of investigation, Ye Tian also learned of another method: entering the time-space Domains through a time-space island. This was also an opportunity the Lord Alliance gave the half-step Eternal Realm cultivators of the Source Sea to enter the time-space Domains.
Among the countless time-space Domains, many time-space lords did not have lords of their own, and instead they were public time-space Domains that allowed any half-step Eternal Realm cultivator to enter.
However, the time-space Domains were only open to Extreme cultivators, and even ordinary Extreme cultivators still could not enter the time-space Domains; they had to pass an assessment before they could leave the Source Sea.
In addition, even after passing the assessment, one still had to pay a certain fee to the administrator of the time-space island as a toll.
Otherwise, they would still be stopped.
This day.
Ye Tian's clone body came to the time-space island. In fact, the time-space island was made by remodeling a fragment of a time-space Domain, and the entrance was very hidden.
Ye Tian entered the time-space island and was immediately stopped by two puppets.
These were not ordinary puppets, but puppets whose strength was comparable to a Six-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm cultivator.
“I am here to participate in the time-space island assessment, to go to the time-space Domains!”
Ye Tian stated his purpose.
“Come with me!”
One puppet brought Ye Tian to a tower within the time-space Domain.
Here, Ye Tian needed to undergo an assessment.
In fact, as long as one's strength was at the Five-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm, there was a very high chance of passing the assessment, but not many people wanted to go to the time-space Domains.
After all, with an eternal lifespan, cultivating in the Source Sea at the Five- or Six-Extreme level was extremely comfortable, and if one happened to find a great opportunity, no one would compete with them for it.
And after going to the time-space Domains, it was relatively difficult to find good opportunities, and the chance of falling was also very high.
Very soon.
The time-space island arranged Ye Tian's assessment: he would fight against a puppet with Five-Extreme strength. Ye Tian easily defeated the opponent, thereby passing the assessment.
In front of the time-space passage of the time-space island, an old man stood guard there.
He was not a puppet, but an Extreme half-step Eternal Realm existence, and his strength was very powerful.
Ye Tian estimated that his strength had at least reached the Seven-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm, and may even have reached the Eight-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm.
“To enter the time-space Domains, you need to pay resources worth one hundred thousand Time-Space Coins.”
The old man said coldly.
Time-Space Coins were a currency of the time-space Domains, and Ye Tian knew this.
So, he took out some resources and quickly gathered enough to make up one hundred thousand Time-Space Coins.
“This time-space passage can lead to three time-space Domains: Green Marsh Domain, Hundred Snow Domain, and Maple Leaf Domain. They are all relatively large and publicly ownerless domains among the time-space Domains. Choose one, and I will activate the time-space passage to send you there.” the old man introduced.
“Maple Leaf Domain!”
Ye Tian chose casually.
Rumble!!!!!
The time-space passage opened, forming a huge time-space vortex.
Ye Tian stepped into the time-space vortex and was immediately pulled by a powerful force; his entire body directly shattered the time-space rules of the Source Sea, even shattering the Source Sea barrier, and entered another world.
……
Darkness, void, emptiness, infinity.
This was the void region between the Source Sea and the time-space Domains. There were no rules here, no energy, everything was void.
Ye Tian was in the time-space passage and felt the suffocating pressure of the void region; even his body felt somewhat uncomfortable.
But very soon, he arrived at the end of the time-space passage—the Maple Leaf Domain.
He truly knew nothing at all about the situation in the Maple Leaf Domain.
Therefore, after arriving here, the first thing he needed to do was familiarize himself with the environment here and understand the situation of the time-space Domains.
Maple Leaf Domain, Heavenly Imperial City.
This city connected one time-space Domain after another, and was a rather famous city in Maple Leaf Domain.
After Ye Tian settled down in Maple Leaf City, he began to learn about the situation in Maple Leaf Domain.
After some time, Ye Tian roughly understood the situation here.
Maple Leaf Domain was not very large. In terms of area, it was only about as big as a foreign world, and compared with the Source Sea, it was simply not worth mentioning.
But although the time-space Domains were small in area, the cultivation environment here was even better than in the Eternal Heaven and Earth. Just a bit of resources, if placed in the Eternal Heaven and Earth, would be enough to make many Supreme Beings compete for them.
Moreover, the races born in the time-space Domains were all very powerful, and they could easily cultivate to the Supreme Being level. .........
Of course.
In the time-space Domains, becoming a half-step Eternal Realm cultivator was extremely difficult.
What surprised Ye Tian was that the living beings in the time-space Domains could not exist eternally; their lifespans were limited.
For example, the Supreme Beings of the time-space Domains had a lifespan limit of one hundred thousand Eternal Years. Although that was a very long span of time, there was ultimately a limit, whereas many ordinary powerhouses in the Source Sea had infinite lifespans.
“This may be the flaw of the time-space Domains!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
In the time-space Domains, even half-step Eternal Realm cultivators could only live for ten million Eternal Years; only Eternal Realm lords were truly eternal.
Perhaps it was precisely this limitation that prevented the time-space Domains from facing an extinction crisis due to the expansion of living beings.
In addition, because struggles in the time-space Domains were very frequent, each time-space Domain could maintain a balanced operation.
Maple Leaf Domain had many half-step Eternal Realm cultivators, and even Extreme powerhouses, with the strongest being three Eight-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses.
Eight-Extreme half-step Eternal Realm powerhouses held status second only to ordinary Eternal Realm experts. In Maple Leaf Domain, they possessed very high prestige and power, and many half-step Eternal Realm cultivators had taken refuge under them.
Besides these, Ye Tian also learned about the division of the time-space Domains.
Time-space Domains were divided into ordinary time-space Domains and Eternal time-space Domains, and Maple Leaf Domain was an ordinary time-space Domain, though it was considered quite good among ordinary time-space Domains.
However, Maple Leaf Domain had not produced top-tier resources, so it was not valued by newly ascended Eternal Realm lords, and to this day it was still a publicly ownerless domain.
Among the endless time-space Domains, there were many such ordinary time-space Domains, and there were also quite a few damaged time-space Domains.
But Eternal time-space Domains were not many, only a little over a hundred. Every Eternal time-space Domain lord was an incomparably terrifying existence among Eternal Realm experts.
For Ye Tian, Maple Leaf Domain was fairly suitable for him and could serve as his starting place.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian began to make friends with one Extreme after another. Only by making many Extreme acquaintances would he have the chance to come into contact with some opportunities and intelligence.
Finally, on this day, an Extreme invited Ye Tian to join a relatively free faction.
